Chapter 853: The Qilin Immortal’s Wives

“Was it like that?” Dean Qi thought that “Lu Yang”’s account didn’t quite match his expectations. On the other hand, Jin Caiwei’s depiction was more aligned with his perception of immortals, marked by grand and sweeping moves, with a bearing that looked down upon all under heaven.

Jin Caiwei hesitated, a rare occurrence for her. She was unsure whether she should affirm or deny Lu Yang’s answer.

She was born in the late ancient era, when the age of prodigies vying for supremacy had already passed. The Four Ancient Immortals were at their zenith, ruling the universe. Her father, the Old Qiongqi, was one of the formidable figures of ancient times, his status second only to the Four Ancient Immortals.

At that time, her cultivation was insufficient to participate in many events, such as battles between immortals, so she could only rely on her father to recount them to her.

She had learned about the battle between the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Epoch Immortal through her father’s narration.

I remembered the Qilin Immortal saying that much of history had been whitewashed by that shameless Heaven Mandate Immortal and that one must not simply look at appearances but examine the actual situation.

The scene Lu Yang described fits perfectly with what the Qilin Immortal referred to as the “actual situation.”

Moreover, Lu Yang’s tone sounded far more assured than my own, as if he had witnessed it firsthand; he described it in such vivid detail.

Jin Caiwei lacked such confidence.

“I don’t know either.” Jin Caiwei shook her head helplessly, unable to tell whether Lu Yang's words were true or false.

“I see.” Dean Qi felt that the battle was indeed mysterious and unfathomable, which was in line with the characteristics of ancient history.

Dean Qi then spoke earnestly to Ye Gu. “Little Gu, I’ve long told you not to assume that learning a smattering of ancient history makes you remarkable. What kind of period was the ancient era? It was the most glorious and resplendent age of the cultivation world, teeming with countless legends. Even if one devotes their entire life to studying it, they might hardly glimpse a corner.

“Look at these two young friends. Their understanding of ancient history surpasses yours, yet they offer two different answers about the same event. This demonstrates how mysterious ancient history is.”

Ye Gu was overwhelmed with shame by Dean Qi’s words.

“Teacher, I know I’m in the wrong.”

“It’s good that you know your mistake. Alright, return to the Meng Family and continue teaching.”

After Dean Qi chased Ye Gu back to the Meng Family, he further discussed ancient history with Jin Caiwei and Lu Yang. Jin Caiwei’s depictions truly broadened his horizons, allowing him to learn of many ancient secrets.

“You’re saying that the Qilin Immortal had not only the Dragon and Phoenix ancient ancestors as wives, but also a little ancestor of the Qiongqi Tribe as his wife?”

Back when Jiang Lianyi publicly announced that the Qilin Immortal had two wives—herself and Ao Ling—it caused an uproar in the academic circles of ancient history. Who would have thought that the Qilin Immortal had another wife?

Dean Qi only knew that the Fellow Daoist Jin before him was named Jin Caiwei, but he was unaware that the Qiongqi Tribe’s little ancestor also had the same name, so he made no connection between the two.

Unlike ancient mighty experts like Ao Ling and Zhu Tian, Jin Caiwei didn’t have a resounding reputation. Later generations only knew of the Old Qiongqi, clueless that there was also a little qiongqi.

“Fellow Daoist Jin, may I ask if this was recorded in some ancient text?”

As a scholar, Dean Qi naturally could not believe whatever Jin Caiwei said; evidence was required. He had perused many texts, but none had ever mentioned the Qilin Immortal having three wives.

“Of course, it was.” Jin Caiwei mysteriously produced an ancient text that clearly recorded that the Qilin Immortal had three wives, the third being from the Qiongqi Tribe. freewebnovel.com

Dean Qi accepted this ancient text, feeling like he had obtained a treasure. This records many things unknown to later generations; its value is immeasurable.

“No wonder I always found it odd. Even the current emperor can have three palaces and six courtyards in his harem. How could an almighty immortal like the Qilin Immortal have only two wives?”

The Xia Emperor, “...”

Dean Qi, I’ve never offended you, right? I have never withheld funding for your Imperial Taixue Academy.

“Immortal Fairy, what’s going on here?” Lu Yang was greatly perplexed. While Dean Qi was translating the ancient language sentence by sentence, Lu Yang had long finished reading.

What ancient text would dare write that the Qilin Immortal had three wives? Did it treat Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi as pushovers, taking them for figures molded from clay?

“Is this ancient text forged?”

“It’s not forged. This book is indeed from the ancient era. Little Tiger probably wrote it herself.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy guessed correctly. Jin Caiwei had indeed written this ancient text in the ancient era. Anyone who scrutinized it would conclude that it was authentic.

The only issue was that no rule dictated that what was recorded in an ancient text must be true.

Lu Yang genuinely felt that being a historian was no easy task. First, there was the Heaven Mandate Immortal who stopped at nothing to show off; now, there’s Jin Caiwei who fabricates history to elevate her status. Anyone researching this would be befuddled.

Fortunately, I have the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who knows the complete truth of ancient history... Wait, no, ‘fortunately’ my ass! It would be best if I didn’t know!

One of Jin Caiwei’s purposes in coming to the Imperial Taixue Academy was to spread rumors. Although she couldn’t defeat Ao Ling or Jiang Lianyi, she could gain the upper hand in public opinion.

Having deceived Dean Qi, Jin Caiwei watched Lu Yang warily. This Lu Yang isn’t simple; he likely knows I’m lying.

While Dean Qi was engrossed in the ancient text, Jin Caiwei bared her fangs, snarling threateningly at “Lu Yang” to prevent her from revealing the truth.

“The Qilin Immortal did have another wife—the Little Qiongqi.” Contrary to her usual behavior, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy did not expose Jin Caiwei’s lie but instead helped her, which greatly puzzled Lu Yang.

“Immortal Fairy, you...”

“What’s the matter? What Little Tiger said isn’t wrong. The Qilin Immortal admitted it himself.”

“Something like that happened?!”

“That was before the Qilin Immortal married Little Ling and Lianyi. The two of them pressed him, demanding to know who he loved and who he would take as his wife.

“The Qilin Immortal embraced them both and said, ‘I love both of you, so both of you are my wives.’

“Following this logic, since the Qilin Immortal also liked Little Tiger, she is naturally also his wife.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke bluntly. I always say things that are grounded and highly logical.

“Hence, the Qilin Immortal actually had quite a lot of wives—the Little Qiongqi, the Nine-Tailed Fox, and so on.”

Lu Yang felt it was fortunate that the Qilin Immortal became an immortal. If he had been only a half-immortal, he might have shared the same fate as that cultivator with the Harem Golden Core, ending up dismembered.

“Later on, since the Qilin Immortal liked so many people, I wanted to know if he had a favorite. Just like how I ranked the Ten Ancient Beauties, although everyone was rather beautiful, there had to be an order.

“Therefore, I gathered all his wives and asked the Qilin Immortal who he liked most.

“The Qilin Immortal was so excited that he kept trembling. Noticing how he was shaking so violently, I tied him to a chair and bound him securely. Only then did he stop shivering.

“He probably liked everyone equally, because in the end, he couldn’t say who he liked most.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head regretfully, extremely dissatisfied with the outcome.

“After I left, I heard the Qilin Immortal got beaten up, and he cried out quite loudly. It was probably just some marital play. Since it was a private matter, I didn’t pry.”

Jin Caiwei was oblivious to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s thoughts. But judging from how he helped me to cover the lie, he is a pretty promising junior who can be properly groomed in the future.

Chapter 854: Enough Manpower

Having achieved her purpose at the Imperial Taixue Academy, Jin Caiwei saw no need to stay further and soon bid goodbye to Dean Qi.

“Little Tiger, wait a moment. Would you like to follow me?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy half-crouched, blocking Jin Caiwei’s smile, and asked with a beaming smile.

Jin Caiwei had a tiger-shaped pendant, so it wasn’t inappropriate for “Lu Yang” to call her Little Tiger.

It was rare to encounter someone from the ancient era. Although she no longer remembered the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the latter was still willing to interact with her.

Besides, establishing a new dynasty requires people, after all.

“Follow you?” Jin Caiwei sized “Lu Yang” up. If it were anyone else daring to speak to her like this, they would have been ripped in half already.

However, she felt an inexplicable and indescribable familiarity with Lu Yang, which reined in her impulse.

“That’s right, follow me,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy repeated gleefully, pointing at her follower, the Xia Emperor. “See, there’s already one person willing to follow me.”

Jin Caiwei pondered. My aim in coming to Great Xia is to find out what kind of sect the Dao-Seeking Sect is. Following Lu Yang indeed aligns with my goal.

“Very well, then I shall follow you for some time.”

In the mental space, Lu Yang’s eyelids twitched as he listened to their conversation. If it were me, I would never dare let a half-immortal follow me.

“Who is this person willing to follow you?” Jin Caiwei noticed the rather inconspicuous Xia emperor.

“His name is Xia Tian, and he is a remarkable talent.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy held the Xia Emperor in high regard.

Jin Caiwei had little interest in the Xia Emperor and simply uttered, “Oh.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy walked ahead, with the two followers, the Xia Emperor and Jin Caiwei, trailing behind.

The Xia Emperor highly valued Jin Caiwei’s knowledge of ancient times and stealthily approached her. “Miss Jin, would you be interested in joining the Imperial Taixue Academy? With your talents, you could quickly rise to the position of dean.” Even Dean Qi acknowledged that he is inferior to Jin Caiwei in the field of ancient history.

Jin Caiwei tilted her head up, casting a disdainful glance at the Xia Emperor. She wasn’t tall and had to look up at everyone, so she had a fairly favorable impression of “Lu Yang,” who was willing to half-crouch to speak to her.

“Psycho.”

“Hey, you girl! You don’t know how to recognize a good-hearted person!” Given the Xia Emperor’s status, no one had dared to speak to him like this.

But I’m not a petty man. When this girl encounters a crisis, I’ll step forward to reveal my identity, and that’s when she’ll regret it!

Jin Caiwei quickened her pace, taking large strides to keep up with Lu Yang. “Where did you learn all this ancient knowledge?”

Dean Qi might not realize the intricacies, but she understood how incredible the depth of “Lu Yang”’s ancient knowledge was. He knows so many detailed aspects of ancient knowledge; those couldn’t have come from books alone.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Jin Caiwei meaningfully and transmitted an auditory message. “Why would I need to learn it? I already knew it.”

Jin Caiwei frowned, feeling more strongly that Lu Yang was no simple person. “Just who are you?”

She suspected that the Lu Yang before her was not the real Lu Yang, his body long been taken over by a formidable figure from the ancient era. This would also explain Lu Yang’s terrifying talent.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy extended an index finger and pressed it to her lips. With her gaze slightly lowered, she whispered, “Shh, Little Tiger. The current you should not know who I am yet.”

Jin Caiwei’s expression shifted slightly. Lu Yang identifying my race earlier was indeed no coincidence!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hushed her voice once more, speaking with an air of mystery. “This immortal has slumbered from ancient times until now, intending to overthrow the Great Xia Dynasty and establish a new dynasty. Little Tiger, are you willing to lend me a hand?”

Jin Caiwei was horrified. Lu Yang actually wants to overthrow the Great Xia Dynasty? The Great Xia Dynasty is suspected to have an immortal, yet he dares to say such words. Could he also be an immortal?!

This is a massive trap. I want no part of it. Once I get implicated, there’ll be no escape! This likely involves battles between immortals, something far beyond my reach!

“I refuse!” Jin Caiwei firmly rejected the olive branch extended by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy chuckled softly, as if mocking Jin Caiwei’s naive and ignorant action.

Jin Caiwei regarded Lu Yang warily, fearing he might make a move. She no longer dared to view him as merely a Nascent Soul cultivator. “What are you planning to do?!”

“Rest assured, this immortal won’t force you. Speaking of which, this immortal and you have crossed paths before, but you’ve forgotten. I’d even held you once.”

“Nonsense!” Jin Caiwei didn’t believe the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words. I don’t recall myself being held by anyone. Wait, it seems like I really had been held by someone.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy let out a long sigh. “Across the endless eons, great waves wash away the sand, concealing countless truths. Is your memory truly reliable? However, you need not rush to flee from this immortal. Follow me, and I shall unveil the truth for you.”

It was unclear what Jin Caiwei was thinking, but after hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words, she truly didn’t flee from her.

In the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy excitedly shook Lu Yang’s shoulders.

“Well, how was it? How was it? Did this immortal act convincingly? Could I intimidate and fool people?!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, you were actually doing just fine maintaining your previous demeanor. Could you please not completely let loose in the mental space?

Lu Yang flung his sleeves and bowed deeply. “Your Exalted Majesty is a wise ruler through the ages, bearing all living beings of the world in your heart. Every facet of human life is within Your Exalted Majesty’s grasp, so you can naturally play any role convincingly.”

Hearing Lu Yang’s praise, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy smiled elatedly. Suddenly, she seemed to remember something and began counting on her fingers. “Little Tiger, Xia Tian... the manpower is a bit lacking.”

“Not enough for what?” Lu Yang asked.

“Not enough for rebellion. Although Little Tiger is a half-immortal and theoretically pretty capable in combat, it’s still a bit lacking for a rebellion.

“If only a few more helpers would come.”

Lu Yang dared not answer, fearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would include him in the list of personnel for rebellion.

Wait, it seems that whether I’m counted or not makes no difference. The Immortal Fairy is using my body to rebel in the outside world!

As they spoke, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy led Jin Caiwei and the Xia Emperor through Luotian Forest, the shortest route back to the Meng Estate.

The trees towered into the sky. The Meng Family had long since replanted the trees that were broken or toppled in battle, leaving no trace that a fierce struggle had once broken out here.

Suddenly, an icy voice sounded nearby.

The Xia Emperor narrowed his eyes as he glanced in that direction. Several cultivators were blocking two delicate, fragile women. The cultivators wielded magical treasures, their expressions hostile.

The leader, a cultivator in black robes, spoke sinisterly while channeling spirit energy into his magical treasure. “You two obtained something good at the auction house, didn’t you? Could you part with it? In return, we shall spare your lives!”

The two delicate women had never encountered such a situation before. Terrified and at a loss, they trembled uncontrollably. They weren’t cultivators from the imperial city and had only come after hearing that the auction offered good items. Never did they expect that simply winning a highlight lot would make them targets. freewebnovel.com

The Xia Emperor was delighted. Isn’t this the opportunity for me to reveal my identity while traveling incognito among the people?

Before he could take any action, he heard Lu Yang calling out joyfully to the two besieged female cultivators and waving his hand. “Little Ling, Lianyi, what are you doing here?”

Chapter 855: Then Lu Yang’s Identity Is Obvious

Originally, the atmosphere was tense with the two female cultivators besieged, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s greeting shattered this impasse.

Hearing the two exceedingly intimate forms of address, the Xia Emperor stiffened abruptly. He stared incredulously at the jubilant “Lu Yang,” then turned to look at the two female cultivators who were being waylaid and robbed.

As renowned ancient half-immortals, portraits of Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi had long been circulated among the major factions. However, the appearance of these two female cultivators before him clearly differed from that of the two ancient half-immortals.

Could Lu Yang have mistaken them?

Or was he not calling Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi?

The two female cultivators found it odd upon hearing “Lu Yang” call out to them with unusually affectionate forms of address. Senior Brother Lu Yang would never address us like that.

Initially, the two had intended to relive their lifestyle in the ancient era, where they would disguise themselves as rogue cultivators to attend an auction, win the highlight lot, be targeted by plundering cultivators, and then reveal their astonishing identities just as the plundering cultivators were about to strike.

Now that Lu Yang had exposed their identities, there was no further need to maintain the disguises. The two women shed their disguises, revealing two peerlessly beautiful faces so exquisite that they could captivate one’s heart.

They were none other than Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi. freewebnovel.com

“You two...” The plundering cultivators who had acted out of greed now paled drastically, turning to flee.

However, how could there be any chance of escape before two half-immortals? A gigantic dragon claw phantom descended, slow yet impossible to evade. Several plundering cultivators were casually pressed into the ground by Ao Ling. Immobilized, their hearts were drowned in boundless terror.

After dealing with the minor underlings, Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi walked over to Lu Yang and scrutinized him carefully. They hadn’t expected to encounter Lu Yang in the imperial city, and they vaguely sensed that the Lu Yang today was somewhat different.

“What’s wrong? Don’t you recognize me?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy greeted them with a smile, startling Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi. Their pupils contracted, but the two soon broke into delighted smiles.

It’s Everlasting-jiejie!

“It’s really you!”

The two women affectionately linked arms with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy on each side. Onlookers could only envy “Lu Yang” for having two beauties in “his” arms.

“What are you two doing here?!” Jin Caiwei stared warily at Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi. These were the two people she least wanted to meet now, and she had run into both at once.

She focused all her attention on guarding against the two women to the point where maintaining her human form became challenging. Her eyes turned into vertical golden pupils, and two white tiger ears sprouted from her head. Baring her teeth, she revealed two small tiger fangs.

“Jin Caiwei! You’re still alive?” Earlier, Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi had their attention wholly on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Only now did they notice that Jin Caiwei was also here.

Believing that no one recognized her now, Jin Caiwei hadn’t disguised herself since leaving the Demon Region. She kept her original appearance, making her recognizable at a glance.

“Of course, I’m alive. Don’t think only you two have an Incipient Dao Fruit!” A white ferocious tiger with wings of bones on its back appeared behind Jin Caiwei. This was the manifestation of her true form—the White Qiongqi, an aberrant breed among qiongqi.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi were half-immortals who had fought their way through the ancient era. How could they fear Jin Caiwei, a flower grown in a greenhouse?

Ao Ling sneered. Behind her appeared a black dragon exuding a primordial, ancient aura. She looked down upon Jin Caiwei. “Oh? Then I shall see what substance your Incipient Dao Fruit has!”

Jiang Lianyi stepped forward. A phoenix phantom soared from a sea of flames, its cry echoing through the nine heavens.

The White Qiongqi, the Black Dragon, and the Golden Phoenix—three great ancient immortal beasts—gathered here, none yielding. The oppressive pressure from the Black Dragon and the Golden Phoenix clearly overshadowed the White Qiongqi’s.

A huge battle was on the verge of erupting.

The Transcendent Tribulation cultivator responsible for covertly protecting the Xia Emperor inwardly lamented his circumstances. What kind of situation is this? I had originally thought that His Majesty couldn’t possibly meet any danger in the imperial city. I was convinced it’d be a leisurely assignment. No one had told me that I would run into three great ancient immortal beasts contending in the imperial city!

Three half-immortals! And all with immortals backing them! I’m afraid even burning my lifeblood dry won’t suffice to protect His Majesty.

“Alright, alright, we’re all on the same side. Withdraw it, everyone.” Seeing that a fight was about to break out, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hurriedly interposed herself to halt the conflict.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi obediently withdrew the phantoms of their true forms. Jin Caiwei immediately felt the pressure reduce drastically and also withdrew her phantom, though the atmosphere remained tense.

“Little Ling, Lianyi, what are you doing here?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grabbed their hands, smiling happily.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi’s cheeks flushed slightly. They were somewhat accustomed to hearing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s question and casually pointed at the plundering cultivators lying on the ground.

“Well, we wanted to experience life in the ancient era, so we came to the imperial city, found an auction, and randomly bought a few valuable items, thus drawing their attention.”

The plundering cultivators, firmly suppressed by the dragon’s oppressive pressure, were filled with regret. We didn’t check the almanac before going out today. How did we bump into these unparalleled, mighty experts when we were simply attempting a robbery?

What kind of life were you two living in the ancient era? Going to auctions? Are auctions such interesting places?!

“So that’s how it is.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy. She was the one who taught Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi the good habit of going to auctions to fish.

“Who told you we’re on the same side? Just who are you?!” Jin Caiwei stared at “Lu Yang.” With merely a single sentence, she could make the proud Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi voluntarily lower their guard. What exactly is this person’s identity?

The Xia Emperor was also astounded. He had long known that the sensational ancient Heavenly Court was fabricated by the Dao-Seeking Sect and that its founder was none other than Lu Yang. However, he was unaware of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence, simply assuming the Dou Heavenly Sovereign to be another identity of Yun Zhi.

As for Lu Yang knowing Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi, he wasn’t surprised. After all, Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi had publicly admitted to being members of the ancient Heavenly Court.

What surprised him was how close Lu Yang’s relationship with Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi was. The two had practically glued themselves to him upon meeting, their attitudes very intimate.

If Jin Caiwei hadn’t interrupted them, they might have clung even more closely to him.

Jin Caiwei is an ancient qiongqi, so does that mean she’s the Qilin Immortal’s wife?

The Xia Emperor remembered Jin Caiwei rejecting his recruitment offer, and he now had an explanation for it.

“None of your business!” Jiang Lianyi shielded the Everlasting Immortal Fairy behind her, acting extremely protective, as if fearing Jin Caiwei might swallow her in one bite.

Jin Caiwei gazed intently at Lu Yang’s somewhat handsome face, recalling everything that had transpired prior.

Lu Yang referred to himself as “this immortal,” so he must be an immortal.

He is more familiar with ancient history than I am and is a firsthand witness who experienced it; he’s an ancient immortal.

This indicates that Lu Yang is definitely one of the Four Ancient Immortals.

He’s familiar with ancient history, yet he admitted I was the Qilin Immortal’s third wife.

He had held me before.

I don’t dislike Lu Yang; on the contrary, I feel a natural closeness to him.

He enjoys pretending to be mysterious.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi act intimately with Lu Yang, even to the point of complying with his every word.

Then the answer is obvious.

Jin Caiwei pointed at Lu Yang, somewhat indignant, but remembering him admitting that she was the third wife, she felt more joy, her voice rising several pitches.

“A’He, it’s you!”

The Qilin Immortal’s original name was Shihe.

Chapter 856: Turning in to the Authorities

At this moment, a sudden enlightenment dawned upon Lu Yang as he received a heavenly revelation that shed light on his future and fate.

Every person will eventually die. Whether it’s by the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s hand or by the Qilin Immortal’s hand, I will end up dying.

If the Qilin Immortal were to witness this scene, Lu Yang had no idea how he could survive.

“What A’He? I’m not the Qilin Immortal.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the almighty head of the Five Ancient Immortals, conducted herself with rectitude. Impersonating the Qilin Immortal would only demean her.

“You’re not?” Jin Caiwei eyed “Lu Yang” skeptically. Do you think I’m a fool? Who are you trying to deceive?

If you’re not A’He, how could you be so intimate with Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi?

“This person is indeed not Hubby.”

Ao Ling looked down at this little one, a faint, ambiguous smile playing on her lips. “Little lass, the matters of antiquity are intricate and complex. How could you possibly understand them?”

“Don’t call me ‘little lass!’” Jin Caiwei was enraged. I hate it most when others address me this way, especially when it’s Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi!

But judging from Ao Ling’s words, could it be that Lu Yang really isn’t the Qilin Immortal?

Jin Caiwei became uncertain. Her knowledge of ancient matters was indeed not comprehensive. For instance, she was completely oblivious to affairs pertaining to the ancient Heavenly Court, whereas Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi had long been its members, clearly highlighting the disparity in information they possessed.

“If he’s not the Qilin Immortal, who else could he be?!” Among the Four Ancient Immortals, only the Qilin Immortal meets all the criteria.

If no outsiders were present, Ao Ling wouldn’t mind revealing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s identity to Jin Caiwei, but the timing now was indeed inappropriate.

Ao Ling looked toward the sole outsider present. “Who is this person?”

““He’s called Xia Tian, a subordinate I just recruited.”

“Subordinate?”

Ao Ling took a couple more glances at the Xia Emperor. I know how discerning Everlasting-jiejie’s judgement is; even recruiting underlings isn’t done casually. For Xia Tian to become Everlasting-jiejie’s subordinate, he must have unique qualities.

However, this person’s cultivation seems rather ordinary. If a real fight breaks out, even Senior Brother Lu Yang can probably defeat him. What does Everlasting-jiejie value about him?

Never mind, no need to care so much. Everlasting-jiejie naturally has her reasons for her actions.

Despite facing three half-immortals, the Xia Emperor wasn’t particularly terrified. They’re merely half-immortals; I have the Old Ancestor backing me, and I am the Old Ancestor’s spokesperson in the current era. In terms of status, I am no lower than a half-immortal.

But can I still enjoy the thrill of revealing my identity while traveling incognito among the people, right?

My eldest son gets to enjoy life when he travels out, while whenever I travel out, I’d either encounter someone clamoring to kill me or run into three ancient half-immortals. Neither is a good opportunity to reveal my identity.

“Lianyi, make these people lying on the ground go to the Ministry of Justice to turn themselves in. I have something to share.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pointed at the panic-stricken plundering cultivators.

“Alright.”

Jiang Lianyi approached the plundering cultivators. They wanted to flee, but suppressed by the dragon’s might, they couldn’t move even if they tried. She activated her Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit, imprinting each plundering cultivator with a mark, bringing them under her control.

Witnessing this scene, Jin Caiwei snorted coldly. She recalled that Jin Que also bore a mark from Jiang Lianyi’s Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit.

That was on the day before the founding ceremony of the Demon Kingdom. Chieftain Jin had inadvertently barged into an inn and bumped into Jiang Lianyi, who had recently been resurrected. To keep the matter under wraps, Jiang Lianyi had commanded Chieftain Jin not to speak of anything concerning her.

Although Chieftain Jin hadn’t mentioned it, Jin Caiwei had clashed with Jiang Lianyi more than once and recognized at a glance that the mark was Jiang Lianyi’s imprint.

“You seven, go to the Ministry of Justice and turn yourselves in; confess all the crimes you have committed. But you must not divulge anything about me, Ao Ling, or Jin Caiwei.”

Since they could become plundering cultivators, it must be because they had done this sort of thing more than once or twice.

After all, Jiang Lianyi, Ao Ling, and Jin Caiwei had special identities. If the Ministry of Justice learned that they had come to the imperial city, the Xia Emperor would inevitably find out, easily giving rise to unforeseen complications. freewebnovel.com

Better to have one less troublesome matter wherever possible.

“Yes!” The seven plundering cultivators stood up and shouted.

Ao Ling withdrew the dragon’s might. The seven plundering cultivators staggered to their feet, appearing no different from usual, but the place they were headed was somewhere they certainly wouldn't have gone before.

Naturally, they were unwilling to turn themselves in at the Ministry of Justice, but under the influence of the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit, resistance was not an option. They couldn’t even show their reluctance on their faces.

~~~

Ministry of Justice.

Ever since Xu Xin passed the hot potato that was the Fourth Imperial Prince’s matter to the Emperor, he felt that he had set down a heavy burden, and his steps became considerably lighter.

The subordinates he had trained were also capable of holding their own. During his seclusion, they had performed their respective duties, handling the Ministry of Justice’s cases in an orderly manner. Even the Body Takeover Law had been revised to its latest edition.

Xu Xin felt that he wasn’t far from the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. A joyful mood is beneficial for breaking through; this is called nurturing one’s nature through the mind. It’s an exceedingly wondrous state.

“I wonder how the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s little disciple is doing now. Speaking of which, that kid really is a talent.” Xu Xin shook his head with a wry smile.

After emerging from seclusion, he had heard many news regarding Lu Yang, such as the great battle in Luotian Forest, where he overwhelmingly crushed his peers with an unbeatable stance, and composed poetry at Lotus Blossom Brothel, where he won Ye Mengyin’s favor.

Putting aside his stubborn fixation on nine familial exterminations, this little disciple of the Taciturn Daoist Priest is much more pleasing to the eye than the Taciturn Daoist Priest himself.

Just then, the Vice Minister of Justice walked in, hesitating as the words rolled onto his tongue.

“What is it?” Xu Xin was in a good mood, his tone gentler than before.

“Your Excellency, outside the gate... Actually, never mind. Perhaps it’s best if you go see for yourself.” The Vice Minister of Justice felt that even if he said it, Xu Xin might not believe him, so it was better to let him see it in person.

“Very well.”

Accompanied by the Vice Minister of Justice, Xu Xin proceeded to the reception area, where he saw seven familiar figures.

“Shi Lei, Bai Yiwen, Zhao Tuo...”

These were all retainers of the Fifth Imperial Prince.

Shi Lei acted as if he didn’t see Xu Xin, pouring out confessions of past wrongdoings like spilling beans from a bag.

“We followed the commands of His Highness the Fifth Imperial Prince and leaked imperial examination questions for profit...

“To win over officials, His Highness the Fifth Imperial Prince instructed us to arrange for their sons and nephews to enter the imperial court...

“It was also the same case for this auction. Someone outbid His Highness the Fifth Imperial Prince for an item he desired. Even after His Highness revealed his identity, the bidder still didn’t give him face and purchased the item at a high price, humiliating His Highness. Afterward, we received orders to retrieve the item by any means necessary. Subsequently, we disguised our identities...

As the Fifth Imperial Prince’s retainers, every deed they committed was inextricably linked to him.

Xu Xin, “...”

Hold on, the Fourth Imperial Prince’s affair just ended; why has the Fifth Imperial Prince now popped out?

After seeing the Fourth Imperial Prince brought to justice, did the seven of you have a crisis of conscience and suddenly decide to collectively turn yourselves in?

“Wait a moment. Why have you all suddenly decided to turn yourselves in?” Xu Xin couldn’t help but ask. These seven don’t seem like the type to have crises of conscience.

Under the influence of the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit, Shi Lei and the others couldn’t disclose information about Jiang Lianyi and the other two ancient half-immortals. Moreover, it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy who ordered Jiang Lianyi, who then commanded the seven of them.

“It was Lu Yang who made us come and turn ourselves in.”

Chapter 857: The Gradually Growing Great Dou Dynasty

After Shi Lei and the others turned themselves in under Lu Yang’s reformative influence, old, buried cases were unearthed one by one, all of which were acts committed by the Fifth Imperial Prince to win over people’s hearts.

The Ministry of Justice became even busier than when they were handling the Fourth Imperial Prince’s rebellion case.

The Fourth Imperial Prince’s rebellion was no small matter, but it was only a single case, with at most some trouble during the arrest.

But this time, it was different with the Fifth Imperial Prince. The cases were numerous, their scope broad, involving many officials in the imperial court.

The Ministry of Justice interrogated Shi Lei and the others through the night. The good news was that Shi Lei and the others displayed a good attitude, admitting their mistakes and answering every question. Furthermore, since Shi Lei and his group were responsible for the Fifth Imperial Prince’s dirty work, they possessed a large amount of evidence, saving the Ministry of Justice considerable effort.

~~~

The First Imperial Prince, Jiang Qun, somewhat regretted disguising himself as his father to sit on the imperial throne. The endless court documents, the bitter medicinal decoctions said to slightly prolong one’s lifespan, navigating the harem and maneuvering among the elders...

“Fortunately, the Right Chancellor and Left Chancellor are not in seclusion and can share some of the load for me.”

Many less important court documents were handled by the Right Chancellor and Left Chancellor, allowing the First Imperial Prince to catch his breath a little. Although handling these court documents wasn’t difficult for him, it was boring. And now, as he was using his father’s identity, there were many things he couldn’t do.

“Traveling incognito among the people is still better. I wonder how far Emperor Father has progressed.”

Jiang Qun opened a court document from the governor of Yù Province[1], reporting traces of Great Yu’s remnants in Yù Province, suspected to include a Great Yu Transcendent Tribulation cultivator. The provincial governor had contacted the army stationed in Yù Province to jointly search for Great Yu’s remnants. But considering the remnants’ strength was uncertain, he requested reinforcements from the imperial court.

“In that case, send the Luoshui Guard to Yù Province.”

Just as Jiang Qun prepared to review the next court document, Eunuch Li came to report. “Your Majesty, the Minister of Justice, Xu Xin, seeks an audience.”

“Let him in.”

Xu Xin entered the hall with measured steps and kowtowed to Jiang Qun. “Xu Xin pays respects to Your Majesty."

“Rise, Minister Xu.”

“Yes.”

“What brings you here, Minister Xu?”

Xu Xin produced a small booklet, which Eunuch Li then presented to Jiang Qun.

Receiving the booklet, Jiang Qun was slightly baffled. “This is?”

“Your Majesty, these are the crimes committed by the Fifth Imperial Prince.”

“Who?” Jiang Qun thought he misheard.

“The Fifth Imperial Prince, Jiang Tang.”

Startled, Jiang Qun quickly scanned the booklet with his spiritual consciousness, and his eyelid twitched. The booklet clearly listed the Fifth Imperial Prince’s various crimes, explaining many of the imperial court’s long-standing unsolved cases.

“Time is tight, and this subject was worried about alerting the enemy, so only some crimes have been verified with evidence.”

Even if these were only a portion of the crimes, they were significant enough. If all the crimes were substantiated, the Fifth Imperial Prince’s fate wouldn’t be much better than the Fourth Imperial Prince’s.

The only difference was that the Fifth Imperial Prince’s crimes didn’t require the nine familial exterminations, so Jiang Qun wouldn’t need to pardon himself again.

...Wait, Old Four’s matter just settled down. Why is it Old Five’s turn to act up?

I’ve only been the interim emperor for three days, and two brothers have fallen into my hands.

Emperor Father, why didn’t you deal with anyone when you were emperor? And why have all these matters come as soon as you left?

Throughout history, imperial princes serving as regent were not uncommon, but never had an imperial prince used the regency to deal with other imperial princes.

Dealing with one is fine, but dealing with two? How would later generations view this period of history?

“How did you uncover these things?” Jiang Qun knew Xu Xin was meticulous and reliable and that he wouldn’t fabricate things to deceive him.

Besides, even if he fabricates something, he wouldn’t dare fabricate something like this.

I’m just curious.

“The Fifth Imperial Prince’s retainers, Shi Lei and the others, confessed it all.”

“Shi Lei was that honest?” Jiang Qun furrowed his brows.

“According to Shi Lei and the others, Lu Yang persuaded them to turn themselves in at the Ministry of Justice.”

Jiang Qun couldn’t help but hold his forehead. Old Four’s matter was reported by Lu Yang, and Old Five’s matter is also connected to Lu Yang. Lu Yang, are you bent on sending all my brothers into prison to clear a path to the throne for me?

“Lu Yang alone persuaded them to turn themselves in?”

“That I don’t know. However, Shi Lei and the others said that when Lu Yang persuaded them, there was also a cultivator named Xia Tian present.”

Jiang Qun, “...”

Isn’t Xia Tian Emperor Father’s damned alias?

I knew this matter wasn’t so simple! It’s indeed Emperor Father’s intention!

~~~

In Luotian Forest, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy held a meeting, sitting in a circle with Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, Jin Caiwei, and the Xia Emperor.

“It’s rare for everyone to gather together. Today’s meeting has only one objective—I intend to establish a brand-new dynasty. I’ve even thought of the dynasty’s name; it’ll be called the Great Dou Dynasty.

Ao Ling and the other three straightened their backs slightly, startled by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s words.

Some were shocked at the intention to establish a new dynasty, while others were shocked by the dynasty’s name.

“The sages said that the position of the ruler under heaven should belong to the virtuous. An innately virtuous person like me should become emperor.”

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi clapped vigorously, their eyes blazing as they gazed at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Does Everlasting-jiejie finally have the heart to vie for supremacy?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flashed a smile and lowered her hands, signalling to Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi that they didn’t need to act like this. “

“Looking across the long river of history, every change of dynasty was filled with blood and fire, with the world plunged into abject misery. This goes against my will.”

The draft for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s speech was written by Lu Yang in the mental space. While reading it, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy also improvised freely.

“I believe that establishing a brand-new dynasty doesn’t necessarily have to involve war; it can be achieved through peaceful means.

“For example, I once collaborated with the Fourth Imperial Prince and reported him for rebellion, planning to cause the Jiang Family to collapse by itself through the nine familiar exterminations.

“However, I didn’t expect the Jiang Family ancestor to have some methods, setting up a pardon system in advance and thwarting my plan. Truly an intractable opponent!

“But that’s fine. Nothing is smooth-sailing. The process of founding an enterprise is always arduous. I believe that as long as we’re united, no difficulty is insurmountable!”

Standing on the table, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy raised her hand and yelled, “Everyone, are you willing to follow me in establishing a new dynasty?!”

“I’m willing!”

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi went without saying; whatever the Everlasting Immortal Fairy did, they would support her unconditionally.

“Good, then I shall appoint you two as grand generals.”

After shouting, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hopped down from the table and looked at Jin Caiwei. “Little Tiger, what about you?”

Jin Caiwei had no particular thoughts about establishing a new dynasty. But since Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi supported it, if she didn’t, she felt that she would lose face, something she couldn’t tolerate.

“I am also willing!”

“I shall also appoint you as a grand general.”

The four women simultaneously turned their gazes toward the Xia Emperor. Their eyes seemed to say, “And what about you?”

The Xia Emperor felt his scalp tingle under their stares. You’ve all agreed; if I disagree, wouldn’t that make it seem like I don’t fit in?

He had no choice but to slowly raise his hand. “I also agree.”

“I shall appoint you as Prime Minister.”

The Transcendent Tribulation cultivator responsible for secretly protecting the Xia Emperor witnessed this scene and clicked his tongue in amazement. Despite having lived several thousand years, he had never encountered something like this.

Chapter 858: Scheme for Power and Usurp the Throne

The Transcendent Tribulation cultivator secretly protecting the Xia Emperor found the situation quite good. Teaming up with three half-immortals guarantees absolute safety; there is practically nothing left for me to do.

Anyway, my responsibility is to protect His Majesty; everything else is none of my concern.

Below, the three newly appointed grand generals successively volunteered to embark on campaigns, eager to prove their worth.

Ao Ling declared, “I possess the Natural Selection Incipient Dao Fruit, which can temporarily elevate me to the level of an immortal’s body, allowing me to hold my own with the Jiang Family immortal for a while.” In terms of combat power, Ao Ling was the strongest. By enduring attacks from others, she could reach the state of an immortal’s body before fighting the Jiang Family immortal.

Jiang Lianyi was always ready to help others; she most enjoyed assisting Ao Ling. “I possess the Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit, which can control others, turning everyone in the imperial palace into our people. We’ll attack from within and ambush the Jiang Family!”

Little Tiger Jin Caiwei was not to be outdone. “I possess the Planarity Incipient Dao Fruit, which can compress objects into two-dimensional planes. If I form a complete Dao Fruit, the entire world could be turned flat!”

The three grand generals looked at the Prime Minister, wanting to know what capabilities he possessed to be regarded so highly by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“...I can commit suicide.”

Ao Ling, “?”

The Xia Emperor felt that with his mere Divine Transfiguration Stage cultivation, he was certainly useless for rebellion. It seems the only way is through suicide, which makes the throne vacant, thereby creating an opportunity for the Great Dou Dynasty.

“Alright, alright, we’ve said we will be using peaceful methods. Look at you all, using Incipient Dao Fruits and committing suicide.”

“Then how do we use peaceful methods to overthrow the Great Xia Dynasty?” Ao Ling was puzzled. She was already prepared to fight the Jiang Family immortal.

If one relied solely on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it would be difficult to conceive of any effective method. Fortunately, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was never alone—she had the old kid Lu Yang strategizing for her in the mental space.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy laid out her plan. “As the saying goes, ‘scheme for power and usurp the throne.’ To overthrow Great Xia, one must accomplish these two steps. I believe we should usurp the throne first, then scheme for power.

“What is usurping the throne, you may ask? Naturally, it’s seizing that throne in the imperial court!

“The importance of the throne is self-evident. Several imperial princes are breaking their heads just for that throne, aren’t they?

“Once we seize the throne, we would naturally have overthrown half of Great Xia.”

She continued earnestly, “Therefore, I believe we should go to the imperial palace and steal that chair!”

“Great idea!” Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi clapped simultaneously with much force.

In the mental space, Lu Yang exhaled a sigh of relief. Through my calculations, I have finally reduced the death penalty to a fixed-term imprisonment.

It would be best if the Everlasting Immortal Fairy gets caught and spends a year in prison. Things would quiet down then.

Perfidious minister Lu Yang harbored intentions of rebellion, his treacherous heart and crime deserving death a thousand times over.

“Xia Tian, what do you think of this idea?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked.

“It's a good idea.”

The Xia Emperor finally became useful for once.

“I'm very familiar with the imperial palace. Let me plan the route.”

~~~

In the dead of night, five figures stealthily sneaked into the imperial palace.

Although the First Imperial Prince was at the Fusion Stage and needed no sleep or rest, he wasn't a mule either, needing to work from day to night and night to day.

Furthermore, Jiang Qun was impersonating his father now. Slogging away at work tirelessly didn't match the sickly, wan appearance of the Xia Emperor.

It was with this method that he escaped from the harem in the rear palace.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy reminded, “Everyone, be careful not to use your spiritual consciousness, lest we alert the enemy.”

According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy's reconnaissance over the past few days, the Jiang Family immortal resided in the forbidden ground, the deepest part of the imperial palace, and wouldn't involve himself in matters of the imperial palace. However, if someone with high cultivation like Ao Ling and the others probed with their spiritual consciousness, it would easily draw the Jiang Family immortal's attention.

“Alright,” the Xia Emperor whispered.

He was the worst at using spiritual consciousness. Most of the palace bodyguards had higher cultivation than him. If he activated his spiritual consciousness, the palace bodyguards would discover him immediately.

The five of them were literally “shadowy figures.” Jin Caiwei had activated her Planary Incipient Dao Fruit, turning the other four into a planar state, allowing them to traverse along the ground.

This was mainly to accommodate the Xia Emperor and Lu Yang. Their cultivation levels were too low, and they could easily be detected while infiltrating the imperial palace.

“This Incipient Dao Fruit of yours strips away the concept of ‘height,’ leaving only ‘length’ and ‘width?’” Ao Ling asked, looking at Jin Caiwei with newfound respect.

She had assumed that Jin Caiwei was like her father, possessing the Soul Incipient Dao Fruit. She hadn’t expected it to be a completely new type of Incipient Dao Fruit. This creativity is not to be underestimated. Even I would be caught off guard if I’d encountered Jin Caiwei’s Incipient Dao Fruit for the first time.

“You still have some discernment.” Jin Caiwei snorted coldly, quite smug. She had expended tremendous effort to condense this Incipient Dao Fruit.

Turning into a planar state didn’t make them invisible; it just made them less likely to be noticed.

Nevertheless, it wasn’t a problem even if they were discovered. Jiang Lianyi could use her Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit to control the person who spotted them, making them ignore the group’s presence.

In the mental space, Lu Yang thought, You’re just stealing a chair. Is it really necessary to use Incipient Dao Fruits one after another like this?

Back when the Second Imperial Preceptor sneaked into the Dao-Seeking Sect, he only used one Incipient Dao Fruit.

With the help of two Incipient Dao Fruits, the five figures and six souls smoothly reached their destination—the Grand Brilliance Hall (Daming Hall).

The Grand Brilliance Hall was silent, empty, and pitch-black, but this was no hindrance. Even Lu Yang, who had the lowest cultivation, and the Xia Emperor, who had the lowest combat power, could discern the hall’s layout with the aid of the faint moonlight, let alone the three ancient half-immortals.

It wasn’t Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s first time here. The previous conference of righteous path leaders had been held here, and the previous beatings of the four great immortal sect leaders had also occurred here.

Before the Grand Brilliance Hall was a dragon tail path, with stairs and ramps alternating, its surface paved with patterned bricks. Under the eaves were dense bracket sets. Both interior and exterior beams were adorned with painted designs, and the upper parts of doors and windows were inlaid with rhombus-shaped latticework, every detail carrying symbolic meaning.

And the most conspicuous was the prized seat at the far end of the hall—the imperial throne revered by all, representing the ruler of Great Xia.

“We’re finally here,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy cheered softly as she took large strides and happily sat in the chair.

Jiang Lianyi’s eyes lit up. She immediately took out the four treasures of the study and swiftly painted this scene.

In the black-and-white painting, Lu Yang sat high on the throne, hands on the armrests. His eyes resembled those of dragons, and he exuded a majestic and awe-inspiring aura, the very image of a ruler under heaven. Above his head was a plaque inscribed with the characters “Upright and Illustrious,” with the Qin Mirror suspended high overhead,[1] demonstrating his impartiality.

If one looked carefully, they could also spot the signature in the corner of the plaque—Meng Junzi.

“Immortal Fairy, how does it feel sitting on the throne?” Lu Yang asked.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shifted in her seat, not very satisfied. “This doesn’t cut it. It's not as comfortable as the chair Zhu Tian made.”

After all, the chair symbolizing imperial authority was crafted by mere artisans with some cultivation. How could it compare to the monarch chair personally created by Zhu Tian?

1. It is said that the Qinshihuang had a mirror that could distinguish good and evil. The phrase “Qin Mirror suspended high overhead” describes an official’s impartiality when handling cases. ☜

Chapter 859: The Icy Throne is Gone

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sat on the icy throne and sighed softly.

“This chair is hard and cold. This person had become the ruler of the Central Continent, yet he couldn’t even get himself a proper chair.”

The Xia Emperor, “...”

I originally thought sitting on the throne was fine, but why do I sound so pitiful when you put it that way?

“I've got to give it to Zhu Tian for knowing how to enjoy life. The monarch chair he made is much more comfortable than this.”

Zhu Tian’s interests were wide-ranging, including but not limited to dancing and crafting furniture. Every piece of furniture in the Demon Kingdom’s imperial palace was crafted by Zhu Tian himself.

From this perspective, the Demon Kingdom’s imperial palace was much more ostentatious than Great Xia’s imperial palace, for it was the creation of a half-immortal. Even the furniture in the abodes of the Five Ancient Immortals was crafted by Zhu Tian.

Jin Caiwei had heard that even her father’s coffin was made by Zhu Tian. In terms of craftsmanship in this field, First Elder couldn’t compare to Zhu Tian—he was not even close. This was the gap between a Fusion cultivator and a half-immortal; no skill could bridge it!

“Where is the imperial jade seal?” Even while sitting on the throne, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was restless, groping around.

“What do you need the imperial jade seal for?” Lu Yang asked. This isn’t part of the plan.

“Just to see what it looks like. Isn’t it said that emperors must have an imperial jade seal? As the First Dou Emperor, I should see what Great Xia’s imperial jade seal looks like so that I can create one accordingly.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was particular about details. An emperor must have the demeanor of an emperor.

Lu Yang looked at the imperial robe the Everlasting Immortal Fairy donned. The front was embroidered with the smiling face of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, while the back was sewn with the frosty, dashing face of Yun Zhi.

He felt that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy needn’t be overly particular about the imperial jade seal. After all, even if she holds the imperial jade seal, she won’t look like an emperor.

It was everyone’s first time being thieves, so they lacked experience and were unsure what to do now.

Ao Ling leisurely admired the murals in the Grand Brilliance Hall. The murals depicted how the Jiang Family rose to prominence during the late Great Yu era, rapidly growing into one of the major factions vying for the world; how the Jiang and Meng families joined forces to battle the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord; and how the two families parted ways, drew swords against each other, and contended for the position of the world’s hegemon.

“The pigments used in these murals aren’t cutting it; they’re already starting to fade,” Ao Ling critiqued. “Back then, the murals in our home were all blessed by the Epoch Immortal, so they were impervious to the erosion of time, eternal and long-lasting.”

“Also, the quality of these magical treasures is rather ordinary; they just look nice.” Jiang Lianyi pointed near the wall where there was a row of magical treasures serving as decorations.

“The magical treasures in our house were refined by the Heaven Mandate Immortal, all at the immortal-grade.”

The Xia Emperor, “...”

Don't go overboard. First the Epoch Immortal, then the Heaven Mandate Immortal. No matter what, this Grand Brilliance Hall was constructed under the supervision of our ancestors. Please give them some face.

Jiang Ping’an wasn't an expert in artifact refinement. How was he supposed to find so many magical treasures to keep up appearances?

At least, Jin Caiwei hadn't seen much of the world and didn't go around finding fault with everything.

Her searing gaze landed on the throne. “How much can this throne be sold for?”

Our Qiongqi Tribe is currently in need of spirit stones. If we can sell the throne, this trip wouldn't be in vain.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy kindly answered, dispelling Jin Caiwei’s notion. “It’s just a showpiece, hardly worth anything.”

While stealing the throne, the group also took the opportunity to tour the Grand Brilliance Hall.

“How do we move this throne?” Jiang Lianyi asked. This throne has an owner and can't be stowed away in a storage ring. But if we carry it off directly, it'll be way too obvious.

“Let me.” Jin Caiwei volunteered, activating her Planarity Incipient Dao Fruit. She extended both palms, one above and one below, sandwiching the throne perfectly between them.

She clapped her hands lightly, and the throne suddenly vanished, replaced by a piece of paper.

“Done.”

Jin Caiwei compressed the throne into a plane, rolled it into a scroll, and held it in her arms, greatly reducing its size and making it less conspicuous.

“This Incipient Dao Fruit of yours is pretty nifty.”

“Of course, forget about a mere throne, I can even compress the entire imperial palace into a plane.” Jin Caiwei preened herself on her ability.

“Alright, alright, let's quickly leave.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged everyone.

Jin Caiwei compressed the group into planes, and they left the imperial palace using the same techniques.

~~~

The next morning, Jiang Qun stared dumbfounded at the completely empty spot.

“Where is the chair?”

I did say the chair was uncomfortable, but that doesn't mean you had to carry it off.

~~~

Recently, two shocking events occurred in the imperial city.

The first news was that the Fifth Imperial Prince's crimes were exposed. His accomplices were arrested one after another, sending shockwaves across the court and leading to the dismissal of many officials.

When the Second Imperial Prince heard the news, tumultuous waves surged in his heart.

Only days after Fourth Younger Brother's incident, only Big Brother and I remain.

Considering Lu Yang’s significant role in this process, any slip-up could easily lead to retaliation from the Fifth Imperial Prince's remnants. Therefore, the Ministry of Justice didn't publicize Lu Yang's contributions.

The second news was that an audacious thief had stolen the throne. Rumors said that on that day, the Xia Emperor had stood during the morning court assembly, just like the ministers, earning effusive praise from them.

The throne had been in the Grand Brilliance Hall for a hundred thousand years, never moving from its position. People wondered what kind of person dared to commit such a treasonous act.

Some suspected it was the long-vanished Thief Ancestor, while others suspected it was the long-silent Thief King, and there were also those who claimed that it was their successors stepping into the world and making a name for themselves.

Theories abounded, but there was no definitive conclusion.

Xu Xin arrived at the imperial palace with a frown, his steps heavy as lead. He didn't care what the world said. They're all rumors and hearsay anyway, so they can say whatever they like.

But I can't. His Majesty has issued a peremptory command for me to track down the throne’s whereabouts.

Actually, the best method would be to directly ask the throne’s owner where the throne was. In fact, the best method was to ask the throne’s owner directly where it was, but the throne belonged to Jiang Ping’an. The First Imperial Prince dared not trouble the old ancestor in the forbidden ground over a matter like this.

Then Minister Xu will just have to suffer a bit.

“How is the investigation going?” Xu Xin brought a group of capable subordinates to the Grand Brilliance Hall. These subordinates were all famous master detectives from the Ministry of Justice; no clue could escape their eyes.

But this case was about to be their undoing.

“Your Excellency, the perpetrator was extremely cunning, leaving behind no evidence whatsoever.” The subordinates had conducted investigations from the outer perimeter of the imperial palace to the Grand Brilliance hall, yet not a single useful clue was found.

“Could it have been someone with concealment abilities?” Xu Xin furrowed his brows. He himself was also a master detective, but after becoming the Minister of Justice, he hadn’t personally solved cases for a long time.

The Vice Minister of Justice shook his head, spreading out a map covering the entire table; it was an exceedingly detailed map of the imperial palace. “Your Excellency, take a look. There are multiple detection arrays and palace guards on patrol in the imperial palace. Unless it was the work of an immortal, something should have been left behind.

“But immortals wouldn't possibly be so bored as to steal something like this.”

Immortals have already cultivated to the limit. Even if they're drunk, they wouldn't go to the imperial palace to steal a chair.

Xu Xin sighed and presented another possibility. “The perpetrator was extremely familiar with the imperial palace’s layout; it was an inside job.”

Chapter 860: No One Escapes the Vast Net of Justice

“It was stolen by someone from the palace?!” The Vice Minister of Justice verified through an auditory message, not daring to speak aloud.

This is no small matter. If we dig deeper, who knows what we may uncover?

Has our Ministry of Justice recently decided to pick a fight with the imperial family? Two princes have already fallen into our hands—an unprecedented situation in history.

“Most likely. Right now, there are only two possibilities—either an immortal intervened, or it was stolen by someone from the palace.”

But neither possibility makes sense. There’s no motive for the crime.

Do they have nothing better to do than steal the throne? To make His Majesty stand during court assemblies?

By that logic, practically every minister has a motive.

“Go and compile a list. Check who is familiar with the arrays in the palace.”

“Understood.”

The Vice Minister of Justice was efficient. He soon produced a lengthy list filled with names from the imperial family, at the very top of which was the Xia Emperor.

Xu Xin smacked the Vice Minister of Justice on the head. “Are you stupid? Why did you put His Majesty on the list? How could it be His Majesty who stole it?”

The Vice Minister of Justice hurriedly removed the Xia Emperor’s name.

The Xia Emperor had nine sons and seven daughters. With the Fourth Imperial Prince and the Fifth Imperial Prince apprehended, two suspects were eliminated. Naturally, apart from the imperial princes and princesses, suspects also included individuals like Chief Eunuch Li, the Xia Emperor’s personal attendant.

After obtaining Jiang Qun’s approval, the Ministry of Justice swiftly launched its investigation.

“Minister Xu, how is the investigation going?” Jiang Qun summoned Xu Xin to the Mental Cultivation Hall, anxiously hoping to learn about the throne’s whereabouts.

Otherwise, when Emperor Father returns to find his seat missing, it’ll be terribly awkward.

“Your Majesty, after these past two days of investigation, we have discovered that none of the imperial princes or princesses are under suspicion, except for one.”

“Oh? Who is it?”

Chapter 862: Your Exalted Majesty’s Talent is Immense

You didn’t tell me there was also someone named Xia Tian.

Chapter 863: Lu Yang, You Brat, Your Heavenly Luck With Women

Immortal Fairy, why don’t you continue managing my body? This is a situation I can’t handle.

Then, to his astonishment, he saw Lu Yang's heavenly luck with women, encircled by two peerlessly beautiful women and one young girl.

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes were about to burn with envy, but having just emerged from seclusion, his mind was still foggy. Witnessing this scene sent a rush of blood to his head, but he quickly sobered up, remembering that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had taken over Lu Yang’s body. He immediately felt much better.

“Don’t speak nonsense. There’s no such thing; it’s all rumors,” Lu Yang hurriedly denied.

Realization instantly hit Meng Jingzhou. This tone is unmistakably Lu Yang’s!

“Lu Yang, you brat, your heavenly luck with women—”

Lu Yang immediately delivered a kick, sending Meng Jingzhou flying out of the room and cutting off his remaining words.

If the Qilin Immortal were to hear this, it would be disastrous.

Chapter 864: Immortal Peach

After being kicked by Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou returned to Lu Yang’s room. Only then did he get a clear look at the three women. He instantly broke out into a cold sweat.

While he didn’t recognize Jin Caiwei, he had seen both Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi. Lu Yang, you brat, what have you done? Why have you brought these two great figures into our home?

“Seniors, please forgive us for failing to welcome you to our Meng Estate.” Although he didn’t recognize Jin Caiwei, judging by her aura, she didn’t appear far behind Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi. She must also be a senior.

“Ah, it’s the boy from the Meng Family.” Ao Ling’s memory of this young cultivator who had pioneered the Double Infants Stage remained fresh.

Originally, she had assumed it was the current trend for cultivators to form two nascent souls. It was only after leaving the Dao-Seeking Sect and touring the modern cultivation world that she realized Meng Jingzhou was an exception.

“Meng Jingzhou pays his respects to Senior Ao Ling, Senior Jiang Lianyi, and this little senior.” The “little senior” naturally referred to Jin Caiwei.

Jin Caiwei held a favorable impression of the Meng Family. The Qiongqi Tribe often took out loans from the Meng Family, which had helped the tribe tide over several crises. Most importantly, their interest rates weren’t high.

“I am Jin Caiwei from the Qiongqi Tribe. I have been slumbering since the ancient era until now.”

Meng Jingzhou inhaled a sharp breath of cold air. I knew someone who hung out with Lu Yang couldn’t possibly have an ordinary background. See, here’s another ancient immortal beast popping up—and from the Qiongqi Tribe, no less.

“There’s no need to disclose matters concerning the three of us, especially to your Meng Family,” Ao Ling instructed, not wishing to cause trouble.

If the three of them could evade the Ministry of Justice’s search, they could naturally also hide from Meng Jingzhou. They hadn’t concealed their auras because he was Lu Yang’s good friend.

~~~

Two more days passed.

The Meng Family received a piece of unverified news: the Xia Emperor’s end was near, and he had fallen into a coma. The imperial palace was under strict lockdown, with no one permitted entry or exit. According to Meng Jingzhou’s father, this rumor was likely true.

Lu Yang hadn’t expected the Xia Emperor’s condition to deteriorate to this extent. When they parted two days ago, the Xia Emperor had appeared to be full of vigor.

Just as Lu Yang grew anxious and prepared to wake the Everlasting Immortal Fairy up to see if she could devise a solution, an unexpected guest visited the Meng Family.

“Junior Brother Man, what brings you here?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou went out together to greet him. At the main gate, they saw Man Gu standing there in a daze, a cloth bundle strapped to his back.

Man Gu had never seen such an imposing gate before.

“Don’t just stand at the gate. Come in, come in.” Lu Yang acted like the host and ushered Man Gu inside, nudging Meng Jingzhou aside.

It was Man Gu’s first time at the Meng Estate, and he felt rather embarrassed.

Seeing Lu Yang, Man Gu recalled the stories he had heard on his journey and looked at him with worshipful admiration. “Brother Lu, you’re so amazing! I heard you composed a poem on the spot at Lotus Blossom Brothel, and it was hailed as the number one ci poem of the Shangyuan Festival!”

As a Confucian cultivator himself, Man Gu never imagined Lu Yang’s mastery of the Confucian Dao to far surpass his own. Especially after hearing Green Jade Salver: Lantern Festival, he felt that Lu Yang was practically a divine adept!

Lu Yang gave an awkward smile, too embarrassed to admit it was plagiarized and to confess that it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy showing off on his behalf.

Upon hearing Man Gu had arrived, Meng Potian immediately ordered spirit dishes to be served.

“Your chieftain and I are old acquaintances. How has he been lately?” Meng Potian laughed heartily without the airs of a senior as he inquired about the Barbarian Tribe Chieftain’s well-being.

“The chieftain is doing well. I saw him just half a month ago,” Man Gu replied with a candid smile, not quite accustomed to Meng Potian’s enthusiastic hospitality.

“Junior Brother Man, you went home?”

“Mmm, I just went back for a visit. It was our Barbarian Tribe’s Ancestor Worship Day half a month ago. I wasn’t particularly keen on returning, but I couldn’t refuse when the tribe insisted that I must attend.”

Meng Jingzhou nodded repeatedly. “I can understand. After all, you’re an Ancient Barbarian. Even if others don’t go, you have to.”

Man Gu shook his head, revealing a rare, bashful expression. “Actually, that’s not the reason. It’s mainly because my nascent soul is the Ancestral Assembly Nascent Soul. During the worship ceremony, the tribe elders insisted on placing me on the platform, summoning my nascent soul, and having the tribesmen worship me.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

He imagined Man Gu sitting on the platform, with tens of thousands of barbarians below bowing and singing to him in unison. Who could possibly endure that?

“Doesn’t your nascent soul randomly summon ancestors?”

“That’s why the elders decided to worship them randomly. They figured that since they’re all ancestors, it doesn’t matter who they pay their respects to.”

Lu Yang thought, As expected of the Barbarian Tribe. Freed from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Tame Head Curse, their thinking has become much more flexible and adaptable. It’s a good thing.

“Uncle Meng, may I ask if you are very familiar with our chieftain?”

“Oh? Has he never told you? Your Barbarian Tribe and our Meng Family have maintained ties for a hundred thousand years. You could say that our relationship spans generations.”

“That long?” Man Gu was astonished. Why has the Chieftain never mentioned this to me?

“Absolutely! Back in the days of contending for supremacy, your Barbarian Tribe ancestors followed the Jiang Family. They were a key general under the First Xia Emperor, Jiang Ping’an, and were often trounced by our Meng Family, covering their heads and fleeing like rats!”

Man Gu, “...”

“Of course, all that is ancient history and has long passed. Our Meng Family is no longer the same one that vied for supremacy. Now we just want to earn money honestly.”

“By the way, Junior Brother Man, what’s in your cloth bundle? It smells quite fragrant.” Lu Yang sniffed the air. Man Gu’s cloth bundle emitted a refreshing, soothing aroma that was even more enticing than the spirit dishes on the table.

“I don’t know either. After the ancestor worship ended and I returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect, Big Senior Sister gave me this cloth bundle and told me to take it to the imperial city to deliver it to you. She said you would understand upon seeing it and strictly instructed me not to open it.

“Speaking of which, this is strange. The cloth bundle had no smell when I set out. It was only when I was about to reach the imperial city that a fragrance started to waft out.

“Here.”

Hearing it was from Yun Zhi, Lu Yang took the cloth bundle. Without caring for his meal, he said goodbye to Meng Potian and Meng Jingzhou and hurriedly returned to his room.

~~~

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, what’s wrong? Why the rush?” In his room, Ao Ling and the other two ancient half-immortals were studying the applications of the Planary Incipient Dao Fruit.

“What a familiar scent.” Jiang Lianyi’s gaze drifted toward the cloth bundle in Lu Yang’s hand.

Lu Yang placed the cloth bundle on the bed and unwrapped it, revealing a familiar wooden box. He lifted the lid of the box to find a large, tender, pink peach resting peacefully inside.

It was the peach’s subtle fragrance that had wafted out from the wooden box.

“No wonder it was so familiar! It’s an immortal peach from the natural spiritual root!” Jiang Lianyi chuckled, recognizing the peach’s origin.

Lu Yang remembered seeing the immortal peach before leaving for the imperial city. At the time, it was unripe and green. Judging by its current state, it had likely ripened.

“It’s an immortal peach, and one that has just ripened.” Ao Ling and Jin Caiwei also recognized it.

All three women had eaten immortal peaches during the ancient era, especially Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi, who frequently consumed them.

Immortal peaches were something only those from ancient times could recognize. During the great battle between the Four Ancient Immortals and the mastermind behind the scenes toward the end of the ancient era, that particular World Natural Spiritual Root had retreated into a peach blossom secret domain and never emerged again.

Hence, people born after the ancient era were unfamiliar with immortal peaches.

Chapter 865: Interception

“The Xia Emperor needs this immortal peach now more than ever. We must deliver it swiftly!”

The Xia Emperor’s condition was not optimistic; he likely only had a few days left. This was precisely the time to consume the immortal peach.

The only thing that puzzled Lu Yang was why Yun Zhi hadn’t simply instructed Man Gu to deliver it directly to the imperial palace, but instead had Man Gu pass it to him to deliver it.

Given the urgency of the situation, Lu Yang couldn’t dwell on the possible reasons, preparing to set off immediately.

To be safe, Lu Yang also informed Meng Potian about the immortal peach, hoping the Meng Family would dispatch someone to accompany him to the imperial palace.

The identities of Ao Ling and the other two were special. If they intervened, it would be difficult to explain why they were helping Lu Yang. It was best if they refrained from taking action.

“Unaffected by the threshold of lifespan and capable of further extending it—such an immortal item exists in this world?” Surprise spread across Meng Potian’s countenance. Even with the Meng Family’s vast wealth and influence, he had never heard of the immortal peach’s existence.

“Since it was Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi who spoke of it, it must be genuine. Let’s go. I’ll personally accompany you to the imperial palace!”

Meng Potian understood the importance of this matter. While Lu Yang was unfamiliar with the current state of the imperial city, he was acutely aware. As the Xia Emperor’s lifespan dwindled, many factions were becoming restless again, seeking to profit from the situation.

The existence of the immortal peach would undoubtedly be viewed as a thorn in their side! Furthermore, the immortal peach’s ability to extend lifespan would attract the attention of countless old monsters whose own lifespans were nearly spent.

Although people today might not recognize the immortal peach as a product of the World Natural Spirit Root, accomplished cultivators could determine it was a lifespan-extending treasure merely by its scent.

Meng Potian suspected that when Man Gu brought the immortal peach into the imperial city, its fragrance had wafted along the route from the city gates to the Meng Estate. It was highly likely that interested parties had already taken note.

He attempted various sealing methods to contain the immortal peach, but none could lock in its scent. Even inviting the Meng Family’s Transcendent Tribulation cultivators from the mountain to intervene proved futile.

Lu Yang and Meng Potian had no choice but to carry the scented immortal peach toward the imperial city. Accompanying them were several Fusion cultivators and one Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the Meng Family.

On the surface, the imperial city appeared as bustling and prosperous as ever, with cultivators everywhere. But Meng Potian knew this was merely an illusion. In reality, all factions were as tense as a taut string, their attention fixed on the movements within the imperial palace.

Everyone wanted to know whether the First Imperial Prince or the Second Imperial Prince would ultimately inherit the throne.

The imperial city was bisected by a river several hundred zhang wide, divided into the northern and southern cities. The imperial palace was located in the northern city, while the Meng Estate was in the southern city. One had to cross the Gold Sand River to travel from the Meng Estate to the imperial palace.

When Lu Yang’s group was halfway across the bridge, a formidable contingent approached from the opposite direction. Their leader rode a tall steed, halting before the two.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, Uncle Meng, where are the two of you headed?” He dismounted and inquired politely.

Lu Yang watched the other party warily, subtly retreating two steps. “We shall not concern you with that, Second Imperial Prince.”

The Second Imperial Prince’s eyes narrowed slightly, his gaze darting toward the box Lu Yang carried on his back.

“If my guess is correct, Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, you must be carrying an item capable of extending lifespan. Hand it over to me, Lu Yang. Once I become the emperor, I can give you everything you desire.” The Second Imperial Prince’s eyes burned with fervor, gazing at the box on Lu Yang’s back as if he was beholding the form of a peerless beauty.

Among his supporters was a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator named Cang Mingzi, whom Lu Yang had encountered during his journey to the East Sea. Cang Mingzi had informed the Second Imperial Prince that Lu Yang possessed an item capable of saving the Xia Emperor’s life.

In the Second Imperial Prince’s life, this wasn’t a life-saving item for his father. It was a supreme immortal treasure that would compel his father to hand the throne to him! As long as I obtain this life-saving treasure and use it to rescue Emperor Father, he will definitely pass the throne to me!

Meng Potian stepped in front of Lu Yang, his voice cold. “Step aside. His Majesty is in critical condition. Every second counts. Do not waste time on such matters.”

The Second Imperial Prince was reluctant to offend the Meng Family and the Dao-Seeking Sect. However, he knew this was his only chance to secure the throne. According to sources in the imperial palace, Emperor Father has already prepared an edict to pass the throne to Big Brother. It's just that Emperor Father has fallen into a coma at this juncture.

Once Emperor Father awakens and issues the succession edict, I’ll have no more opportunities to contend for it!

Success or failure all comes down to this! I have to go all out!

To seize the throne, he had drawn in too many people and struck too many bargains. If he conceded now, neither he nor the powers backing him would accept it.

“What if I refuse to step aside?!”
