“Then get lost!” When Meng Potian roamed the cultivation world with the old horse and Steward Xu in their youth, he possessed the temperament of a fierce bandit. It was only after becoming the family head that his character had mellowed.

Now that things had come to this, he decided to throw away all pretense.

“Attack together!”

At Meng Potian’s command, the Meng Family elders acted simultaneously. The power of the five elements swirled, and the dual energies of yin and yang surged forth.

But the Second Imperial Prince’s entourage was no pushover either; they also had several Fusion cultivators among them.

Boom!

The two sides clashed above the Golden Sand River. The bridge collapsed with a thunderous roar, crumbling into massive stones that plunged into the river with loud splashes.

Fortunately, pedestrians who had been crossing the bridge sensed the hostile atmosphere and had long since sought refuge at a distance.

Faced with the melee of Fusion combatants, Lu Yang couldn’t offer any assistance and could only take cover at the side.

However, he held the immortal peach, the focal point of the battle. From beneath the river’s surface, a shadow locked onto Lu Yang, rapidly closing in.

The river’s surface boiled, mist rising in spirals. The mist coalesced into chains that shot through the air toward Lu Yang.

“Cang Mingzi, you have some nerve!” A deafening roar echoed above Lu Yang’s head, imbued with the true intent of a lion’s roar, shattering the chains.

Cang Mingzi flew out of the war. Seeing the person who had shattered his chains, his pupils constricted sharply.

“Meng Kuang, since when did you reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage?!”

Meng Kuang was Meng Jingzhou’s grandfather, a good friend of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, a formidable adversary to both the Left Chancellor and the Right Chancellor, and the family head of the Meng Family.

“Why does this old man need to report that to you?”

Meng Kuang wielded a large saber. He drew his palm across the blade, letting blood flow over its surface before it was quickly absorbed. The entire saber turned crimson and wrapped around Meng Kuang’s wrist, as if it had become one with him.

“To prop up this second son of the Jiang Family, you even dared to rob a junior? Do you have no shame?” Meng Kuang’s crimson saber stirred up a gale of blood and carnage.

Witnessing this, Cang Mingzi’s expression changed drastically, and he cried out involuntarily, “Major mastery in the Battle Saber Technique! How is that possible? The Battle Saber Technique requires one to be tempered by battles, attaining enlightenment and breaking through mid-battle. There hasn’t been a large-scale war in nearly a millennium. Where did you get the chance to cultivate it?!”

Meng Kuang laughed uproariously and unleashed a saber strike at Cang Mingzi. “Fool, aren’t trade wars also a form of war? How many trade wars did the Meng Family go through when I was the family head?!

“Behold this move: Battle Saber Technique—Wealth Flows in Torrents!”

Cang Mingzi transformed into a water form. The highest virtue was like water, using softness to conquer hardness. As a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator adept at controlling water, he countered saber and sword cultivators.

Meng Kuang’s saber cleaved Cang Mingzi, splitting him into two masses of water. The water spheres merged back together, leaving Cang Mingzi unscathed.

“What can you do, old ghost Meng Kuang? Don’t think that just secretly cultivating to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage makes you my match!” Cang Mingzi taunted.

Meng Kuang chuckled, producing a big cloth sack from behind him. It was stuffed with top-grade spirit stones.

Noticing the big cloth sack, Cang Mingzi’s face went through a spectacular array of expressions. He hastily felt for his storage ring, only to discover that all the top-grade spirit stones inside were gone!

“What kind of move is this?!” Cang Mingzi was furious. Those are my spirit stones!

“I told you, it’s called Battle Saber Technique—Wealth Flows in Torrents.”

“Bullshit! The Battle Saber Technique has no such move.”

“Trade wars are all about turning your money into my money. Isn’t it perfectly normal for this old man to comprehend such a move from trade wars?”

Chapter 866: Great Yu's Scheme

Having suffered a significant loss, Cang Mingzi dared not directly block Meng Kuang’s moves again. If he got hit a couple more times, he would undoubtedly go bankrupt.

Cang Mingzi kept dodging and weaving through the attacks, attempting to find an opportunity to seize the immortal peach from Lu Yang’s grasp.

But when it came to experience in snatching things, how could Cang Mingzi possibly compare to Meng Kuang? The moment Cang Mingzi’s finger twitched, Meng Kuang saw through his intentions and preemptively cut off his routes.

With his moves predicted and unable to withstand the great saber head-on, Cang Mingzi quickly found himself at a disadvantage.

~~~

Center of the river.

Although Meng Potian cultivated for less than two millennia, shorter than the elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect, his talent for cultivation and combat was extraordinary—evident from Meng Jingzhou’s prowess. At the Fusion Stage, no one was a match for Meng Potian, unless they were an anomaly like a Half-Step Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

Those on the Second Imperial Prince’s side were all masked, concealing their identities. Otherwise, if word got out, they would be finished.

“Kong Yuan, even you, the Grand Governor’s Office Chief Secretary, have taken action?” Meng Potian deduced the other person’s identity through their brief exchange of blows.

He frequently made enemies, and it wasn’t uncommon for him to be ambushed by masked assailants and given a beating. Fortunately, his cultivation was exceptional, and he suffered no serious harm.

Having been ambushed by masked assailants numerous times, he had naturally developed a skill for guessing their identities.

“Nonsense! Who is Kong Yuan? I don’t know him!” Kong Yuan flatly denied it. I absolutely mustn’t admit it.

Meng Potian kicked Kong Yuan, sending him flying across the river.

Kong Yuan vomited blood, and the mask on his face fell off. He tumbled a few times on the ground, rolling right up to the feet of a group of people observing the battle. They hadn’t expected someone to land near them.

Kong Yuan inwardly cursed. I absolutely mustn’t let anyone see my face!

“Die!”

Collateral damage during a clash between Fusion cultivators was perfectly normal.

However, one person from the group squatted down and punched Kong Yuan squarely, leaving him dazed.

“The public security in the imperial city is really not up to par.” Mu Baiyi clicked his tongue disapprovingly, then delivered another punch to Kong Yuan.

The Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the Radiant Sun Creed had come to the imperial city to assess the business environment. They had only been here for a few days, yet had already run into a melee involving Fusion-stage cultivators, one of whom had even tried to kill them.

Kong Yuan hadn’t stopped to think: how could those who dared to spectate the battle at such a time be ordinary civilians?

“Who’s next?”

“Me, me.”

The upper-ups of the two great diabolic creeds volunteered themselves one after another. Opportunities to retaliate against imperial court officials didn’t come often.

Casualties from two sides during a clash between Fusion cultivators were perfectly normal.

“Lu Yang, get moving, quick!”

Although Cang Mingzi was suppressed by Meng Kuang, the latter couldn’t easily take him down either. The most urgent matter now was to deliver the immortal peach to the imperial palace swiftly.

Meng Kuang grabbed Lu Yang by the collar, rotated his wrist two times, and hurled Lu Yang straight to the opposite bank of the river—the northern city, where the imperial palace was located.

Lu Yang tumbled head over heels upon landing. After stabilizing himself, he immediately summoned the Sword-Cleansing Pond and flew toward the imperial palace.

With how chaotic the imperial city was, the higher-ups of the two diabolic creeds figured it would be more interesting to follow Lu Yang, the epicenter of the chaos. They temporarily spared the unconscious Kong Yuan and stealthily trailed after Lu Yang.

After flying across nearly half of the northern city, Lu Yang suddenly sensed his Unbeatable Nascent Soul stir in an attempt to flee. He hastily pushed off with all his might, leaping to the side.

Boom!

A pillar of fire crashed down, striking precisely where the Sword-Cleansing Pond had been. If Lu Yang had been hit by it, it would have meant certain death.

“Oh, a mere Nascent Soul junior could evade this venerable one’s strike? It seems the Dao-Seeking Sect highly values you, giving you a life-preserving treasure.”

From within the towering flames, a figure slowly emerged. The man was as handsome as jade and clad in black robes, resembling a young master from some reclusive clan. A frivolous smile hung on his lips.

“Who are you?!” Lu Yang warily watched the figure within the flames.

“Me? You may address me as Young Master Yu.”[1]

Lu Yang’s pupils contracted. “That General Yu? The General Yu who annihilated the remnants of the Great Qian army, completely overthrew the Great Qian Dynasty, achieved victory in all his battles, with the only defeat at the hands of the Nightmare Supreme Lord and Wu Yao, and subsequently submitted to Wu Yao?!”

Who was the Nightmare Supreme Lord? He was a powerful venerable who nearly seized the world despite having Wu Yao and the first Imperial Preceptor as his opponents. Losing to the Nightmare Supreme Lord was absolutely not a disgrace; it could even serve as a credential to spread one’s fame in later generations.

Besides, since General Yu only lost to the Nightmare Supreme Lord and didn’t die, it’s very likely that he’s also a half-immortal!

“You, junior, aren’t completely ignorant, it seems. I’ll make your death a little less painful later.” General Yu chuckled. In his eyes, Lu Yang was already a dead man.

“How dare a Great Yu half-immortal appear in the imperial city? Aren’t you afraid of the Jiang Family Old Ancestor taking action?!”

Even if the Second Imperial Prince seizing the immortal peach can be considered an internal strife and doesn’t warrant the Jiang Family Old Ancestor’s intervention, a Great Yu half-immortal acting within the imperial city certainly warrants the Jiang Family Old Ancestor's intervention.

Is General Yu not afraid of death?

“Oh? It seems you know quite a bit.” General Yu regarded Lu Yang more highly. Knowing the secret that the Jiang Family Old Ancestor is an immortal confirms that Lu Yang’s status is indeed as lofty as the rumors claimed—designated by the Dao-Seeking Sect as their next sect leader.

But so what? The Dao-Seeking Sect isn’t worthy of my attention.

General Yu looked at Lu Yang with an ambiguous smile. Perhaps because he already saw Lu Yang as a dead man, he was willing to share a bit more. “Yù Province is quite a distance from the imperial city. The news hasn’t arrived here yet.

“We deliberately exposed our traces in Yù Province to lure your Great Xia imperial court into dispatching the Luoshui Guard as reinforcements.

“But what Great Xia couldn’t have anticipated is that we also stationed a half-immortal in Yù Province. He has sealed off nearly half of Yù Province. The Luoshui Guard, Yù Province army, the Yù Provincial Governor, and other key officials, along with several billions of Yù Province civilians, are all trapped there.”

Lu Yang’s pupils constricted sharply. Another Great Yu half-immortal?

Lu Yang understood all too well how terrifying half-immortals were. Although they only had an extra Incipient Dao Fruit compared to a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, it conferred an overwhelming advantage. For example, if the Second Imperial Preceptor activated his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, Transcendent Tribulation cultivators would be powerless to fight back before him.

Among the cultivators sealed within, none could defeat a half-immortal. To resolve the crisis in Yù Province, an immortal must step in!

Sure enough, General Yu added, “Jiang Ping’an has already headed to Yù Province to resolve the matter. He won’t be back for at least half a day.”

In the past, whenever Lu Yang encountered a half-immortal within Great Xia’s borders, Jiang Ping’an should have been the one to take care of it. However, every time Lu Yang was present, the half-immortals would be taken care of successfully, leaving no chance for Jiang Ping’an to step in.

But this time, Lu Yang was not in Yù Province.

The Great Yu cultivators had been plotting for this day for a long time.

“Alright, that’s enough. Why am I wasting so many words on a dead man?” General Yu said lazily. Behind him, countless purple fireballs materialized, their terrifying heat warping the space around them.

His objective wasn’t to seize the immortal peach but to destroy it, causing the Xia Emperor to die of old age upon his sickbed.

Suddenly, a strange, demonic wind swept in from all directions, emanating an aura of decay and death, extinguishing the terrifying purple fireballs.

“This immortal peach is something our Heavenly Court has set our sights on. Let me see who dares touch it!”

“Who goes there?!” General Yu jerked his head up, only to see a vast expanse of brilliant white that blinded his eyes. Focusing his gaze, he saw a colossal, white qiongqi flapping its bone wings, its golden, resplendent tiger eyes particularly conspicuous amidst the sea of white.

“One of the Four Regents of the Heavenly Court, the Northern Great Emperor of Wealth.”

1. The “yu” here means jade. ☜

Chapter 867: Northern Great Emperor of Wealth

When Jin Caiwei first came to Great Xia, she had intended to establish a cooperative relationship with the Dao-Seeking Sect. However, after Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi informed her about the matters of the Heavenly Court while staying at the Meng Estate, she decided to join the Heavenly Court as well.

After all, joining the Heavenly Court essentially made her half a Dao-Seeking Sect member, which wasn’t too far from her original goal.

The title “Northern Great Emperor of Wealth” was one Jin Caiwei had chosen for herself, embodying her fondest hopes and aspirations.

“Northern Great Emperor of Wealth?”

Jin Caiwei’s sudden appearance instantly attracted the attention of everyone in the imperial city.

“Why has the ancient Heavenly Court also come to the imperial city?”

“Who is this qiongqi from the ancient era? According to records, the qiongqi among the half-immortals was male.”

“No one seems to match.” The crowd couldn’t come up with a corresponding ancient half-immortal.

“Don’t bother about that now. Judging by the title, this great emperor oversees wealth and fortune. Do you think paying respects could bring prosperity?”

“That seems to make sense. Should we give it a try?”

~~~

“It’s you again, the Heavenly Court?” General Yu’s smile faded, the roguish grin vanishing from his face. “Wu Youdao’s operation in Wilderness Province failed because of your Heavenly Court. And now you wish to stick your oar in again?”

“Stick our oar in?” The white qiongqi revealed a mocking smile. “This immortal peach originates from the sole World Natural Spiritual Root between heaven and earth. Consuming one leads to boundless marvels; it’s far more than simply extending one’s lifespan.

“The ancient immortals partook of it. That World Natural Spiritual Root originally belonged to our Heavenly Court. It is a pity that it was lost during the immortal battles at the end of the ancient era.

“Now that the immortal peach has reappeared, this is our opportunity to search for that World Natural Spiritual Root again.

“You Great Yu cultivators are blind and ignorant, unable to recognize an immortal treasure. To think you tried to destroy this immortal peach—utterly ignorant!”

“The sole World Natural Spirit Root between heaven and earth?” General Yu was startled by this title. The name alone implies how extraordinary the immortal peach must be.

Indeed. Aside from the legendary immortality elixir, only such an immortal treasure could possibly rescue the wizened Xia Emperor from the brink of death.

“What’s the point of wasting so many words with a country bumpkin from later generations like you? Dao-Seeking kid, pass me the immortal peach!” A gigantic white tiger paw that resembled a small mountain reached toward Lu Yang.

Lu Yang stood dumbfounded in place, frightened by the ancient qiongqi’s terrifying oppressive pressure.

“First come, first served. This immortal peach rightfully belongs to our Great Yu!” General Yu unleashed a fiery spirit saber that seared spirit energy, deflecting Jin Caiwei’s paw.

General Yu had figured things out. The Xia Emperor is protected by national fortune and can’t be easily killed; we can only wait for him to die of old age. My mission is to prevent the immortal peach from reaching the imperial palace. Whether the immortal peach is destroyed or becomes mind makes no difference.

In that case, we will follow the rules of the jianghu: whoever has the stronger fist will claim the treasure!

Innumerable rare spirit metals were smelted into metal plates within the flames. These metal plates flew out and attached themselves to General Yu’s body, forming a full suit of armor.

This was the attire he wore during the campaigns at the end of the Great Qian era. Back then, he commanded vast armies, brimming with vigor and ambition—a formidable lord worthy of contending for supremacy.

General Yu gripped a fire-tipped spear as he charged at Jin Caiwei.

“Courting death!” The golden tiger eyes turned icy. The qiongqi governed slaughter and warfare. Her father had carved out a fearsome reputation through carnage in the ancient era. As the Old Qiongqi’s little daughter, how could she be weak?

The qiongqi roared and flapped its bone wings as though countless vengeful spirits were wailing, shattering the surrounding space.

General Yu tread upon the space fragments, lunging straight toward Jin Caiwei.

The white qiongqi opened its maw and directly clamped down on the head of the fire-tipped spear. With a violent twist of her head, she flung both the spear and General Yu away.

Noticing the imprint of a tiger’s tooth on the fire-tipped spear, General Yu’s expression changed. This fire-tipped spear had accompanied him through numerous battles over the years. Even when facing enemies like the Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Yu Emperor Wu Yao, it didn’t sustain a single scratch. Yet, a single bite from this ancient qiongqi had damaged it.

With these two ancient figures in combat, Lu Yang dared not get involved. He hastily clutched the immortal peach and fled.

“Dang, he’s coming this way!” The higher-ups of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed and the Radiant Sun Creed had been enjoying the spectacle when they saw Lu Yang running toward them and were scared out of their wits.

As Fusion cultivators, their running speed exceeded Lu Yang’s. Hence, they had run ahead of him to get a better view of the spectacle. Now that Lu Yang was trying to break free from the battlefield and make his way to the imperial palace, he was naturally headed in their direction.

But the problem was that while Lu Yang wanted to leave the battlefield, the two half-immortals in the sky wouldn’t allow it!

No matter how strong the higher-ups of the two diabolic creeds were, they dared not observe a half-immortal battle at close range.

General Yu didn’t dare to engage Jin Caiwei head-on again. He activated his Incipient Dao Fruit. A black-red flame appeared in his right palm, causing Creed Leader Chi’s eye to twitch.

He sensed that the temperature of the flame in General Yu’s hand was even higher than the surface of the sun. This is a heat capable of incinerating Fusion cultivators and severely burning Transcendent Tribulation cultivators!

In General Yu’s left hand, a hovering block of ice materialized. The surrounding temperature plummeted rapidly. Countless icicles condensed in the air, and the trees below froze into brittle lumps of ice that would shatter at a touch.

Extreme heat and extreme cold were simultaneously controlled by General Yu. The two opposing forces treated him as their boundary and didn’t interfere with each other, coexisting peacefully. freewebnovel.com

Jin Caiwei recognized General Yu’s Incipient Dao Fruit at a glance. “Controlling dual extremes. It appears you possess a Yin-Yang Incipient Dao Fruit.”

Although Jin Caiwei hadn’t lived through the Battle of the Great Era in ancient times, she had often heard her father recount tales from that time, including the Nine-Layers Immortal’s Yin-Yang Dao Fruit.

“If it were the Nine-Layers Immortal at the Half-Immortal Stage, I indeed wouldn’t be a match. But you? You’re far from it!”

“Arrogant! Today, I’ll make you understand that the past is inferior to the present!”

The black-red flames and dark icicles shot toward Jin Caiwei. The flames spread with a momentum threatening to incinerate space itself. While the dark icicles couldn’t match the level of cold achieved by the Nine-Layers Immortal—which could even freeze time—it could still slow its flow and impede movement!

Jin Caiwei extended her tiger paw and pressed gently downward. Subjected to pressure from above and below, the black-red flames and dark ice were compressed into a plane. From the front, one would only see a black line without any height.

At first, General Yu thought nothing much of it, trying to control the direction of the flames and ice, but he soon realized something was wrong. He could only adjust their movement forward, backward, left, and right, but not up and down. It was as if the flames and dark ice were trapped within an invisible plane, having lost the ability to move vertically.

Even the emitted heat and cold could only be sensed within that plane.

The flow of time returned to normal.

In reality, once struck by the Planary Incipient Dao Fruit, one could only move parallelly, unable to flip over any obstacles. When everyone had transformed into planes to infiltrate the imperial palace, Jin Caiwei allowed them to move at will.

“What is this Incipient Dao Fruit of yours?!” General Yu demanded.

Jin Caiwei naturally wouldn’t answer such a foolish question. Her response to General Yu was another tiger’s roar.

The roar formed sonic waves, crashing upon him unceasingly like colossal waves. Under the assault of these layers of sonic waves, General Yu was pinned in that space, unable to move.

Jin Caiwei activated her Planary Incipient Dao Fruit once more, planning to compress General Yu into a plane.

General Yu knew he absolutely must not be hit and yelled, “Yin-Yang Swap!”

General Yu exchanged places with his own shadow. The shadow became a plane, unable to move vertically, while he himself escaped disaster and was left reeling from the trauma.

Chapter 868: Passed Away

With two half-immortals fighting over the immortal peach, the battle between the Second Imperial Prince’s faction and the Meng Family had become utterly inconsequential.

Meng Potian stepped on a masked acquaintance, gazing anxiously at the armored adept and the ancient qiongqi battling above the imperial city. Suddenly, he recalled the old horse’s assessment of Lu Yang.

“Your Meng Family can buy half the imperial city, right? Lu Yang’s luck can destroy half the imperial city.”

No matter how sturdily the imperial city was built, it could not withstand the full force of two half-immortals in combat.

Fortunately, these two half-immortals’ Incipient Dao Fruits had yet to reach their pinnacle; otherwise, the imperial city’s destruction would have been even faster.

“Big Dipper Inverted, Truth Shadow Swapped!” General Yu pointed a finger at Jin Caiwei. Her shadow gradually swelled and took her form, though it was only an outline with no details.

Not only could General Yu use his own shadow to evade mortal peril, but he could also control the shadows of others, making them attack their owners.

“Troublesome!” Jin Caiwei frowned. She had heard from her father that the Nine-Layers Immortal had often used this move to exhaust his opponents’ stamina during his half-immortal days. By the time the opponent defeated the shadow, their energy would be mostly depleted. This was an intractable move to deal with.

But that is for others.

“Get back!” Jin Caiwei activated her Planary Incipient Dao Fruit, compressing the bulged shadow back into a flat plane, suppressing it temporarily. She would deal with her own shadow slowly after the battle concluded.

With a pat of her storage ring, countless bone fragments flew out. These fragments were ground until they were extremely sharp, capable of slicing through hair.

“Go!”

The reason she had chosen bone fragments was that cultivators at this level typically mastered control over metals. Using special materials such as bones for weapons could prevent them from being manipulated.

Countless bone fragments streaked through the air, leaving shocking gashes in the surrounding space.

General Yu twirled his spear. Though the bone fragments were numerous, he had faced even more attacks from hair-slicing flying daggers. This level of assault was nothing to him.

However, the moment the fire-tipped spear touched a bone fragment, it was cleanly sheared in two. Startled, General Yu dared not block directly and instead dodged frantically.

How could there possibly be such sharp bone fragments in the world?!

General Yu didn’t know that these bone fragments had long been compressed into planes, devoid of the concept of height. For a weapon to become sharp, its edge must be as thin as possible. At the ultimate thinness, it would become a plane without height.

Without an immortal artifact, no matter how excellent the material of one’s weapon was, it would be severed upon contact with these bone fragments.

“Taking so long just to seize a peach.”

Accompanied by a phoenix’s cry, a five-colored phoenix soared across the sky, looking down at the two half-immortals battling below.

Among all birds, the phoenix reigned supreme, and among phoenixes, the five-colored phoenix reigned supreme. This five-colored phoenix was naturally none other than Jiang Lianyi, one of the Heavenly Court’s Four Regents.

“It’s the Southern Great Emperor of Nirvana, Jiang Lianyi!”

The half-immortal battle was visible to the entire imperial city, and Jiang Lianyi had made her entrance before everyone’s eyes. Anyone who paid even the slightest attention to the Demon Region could recognize Jiang Lianyi.

“Two of the Four Regents have appeared. Is this the world about to get turned upside down?” freewebnovel.com

“Speaking of which, the Heavenly Court’s Four Regents have never had more than one appearing at the same time.”

Compared to the relatively unknown Jin Caiwei, Jiang Lianyi was far more widely recognized. Although General Yu was also a legendary existence for cultivators, his fame still fell short of Jiang Lianyi’s, which had resounded throughout the lands since ancient times.

The crowd marveled. Three half-immortals had appeared simultaneously above the imperial city! Since the founding of Great Xia, a battle of such magnitude had never occurred, especially right in the imperial city.

“Space, seal.” Jiang Lianyi activated her Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit right from the outset, locking the space around General Yu.

Since Jiang Lianyi could shatter space, it meant that she herself was stronger than space. Therefore, she could employ a portion of spatial power.

In the ancient era, Jiang Lianyi had sparred with the Nine-Layers Immortal before he became an immortal. She was far more familiar than Jin Caiwei with how to counter the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit.

Against a Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, attacks of the Five Elements were ineffective. If one attacked with fire, the opponent could counter with water, completely negating the attack. A better method was to use physique cultivation methods or direct weapon attacks. However, the most effective way was undoubtedly to employ spatial or temporal means.

General Yu was locked in place, and several bone fragments pierced through his waist, cleaving him in half.

Jin Caiwei pouted. I had already gained the upper hand, yet Jiang Lianyi just had to pop up out of nowhere to steal my thunder. How infuriating!

While the three half-immortals battled, Lu Yang ran himself ragged, traversing through most of the imperial city. At last, he caught sight of the imperial palace.

~~~

Within the imperial palace, the Xia Emperor lay on his sickbed. He was emaciated to skin and bones, his lips parched. Manifold spiritual pills, wondrous elixirs, and natural treasures that seemed capable of prolonging one’s lifespan were piled up beside the bed.

But for the Xia Emperor, whose lifespan was almost depleted, they were pointless.

His eyes were clouded. He seemed to sense the battle of the three half-immortals outside the palace and Lu Yang rushing toward him, carrying the immortal item that could save his life.

He tried his best to turn his head, but in his current frail state, he couldn’t even manage that. He could only move his eyes.

He knew Lu Yang very much wanted to save him, but he also knew he couldn’t hold on until then.

“This emperor...I...still have so many things not yet done...”

I still haven’t universalized education, haven’t reduced medical costs, haven’t cleansed officialdom, haven’t eradicated diabolic cultivators, haven’t eliminated the archaic cultivators...

Most importantly, I haven’t appointed a successor.

~~~

At this very moment, Lu Yang’s heart raced. And it wasn’t just Lu Yang’s—the heartbeats of all Great Xia’s citizens inexplicably quickened, as if something terrible had happened, tugging at everyone’s heartstrings.

A red beam of light shot up from the imperial palace into the sky. The light appeared as a ribbon, drifting in the air like a person who had lost their way, in search of a direction for their future.

Lu Yang wore a bewildered expression, not understanding what had occurred.

Meng Potian and Meng Kuang witnessed this scene from afar. They experienced the same sensation as Lu Yang, the difference being that they knew what had happened.

The Xia Emperor had passed away. Without him naming a successor, and without Jiang Ping’an present to pacify the national fortune, that power had lost all control and restraint.

To regain control of the national fortune, they would either have to wait for Jiang Ping’an to return or have an imperial prince ascend the throne.

However, neither method was feasible now.

Because an immortal had appeared.

“Finally...finally, this opportunity has come.”

A deep, resonant laughter reverberated through the clouds. The laughter alone was enough to disperse the dark clouds above the imperial city and halt the flow of the Golden Sand River that bisected the city.

An elderly man with a weathered face walked through the air, hands clasped behind his back. Arriving above the imperial palace, he paid no heed to the fearful or furious gazes below. Instead, he looked at the confused national fortune with a beaming smile, utterly enchanted.

Lu Yang and Jin Caiwei were extremely familiar with this elderly man. They had just met him together not long ago.

It was Qi Xiuya, the Dean of the Imperial Taixue Academy.

And he had an even more resounding identity and name—Great Yu’s First Imperial Preceptor, Guan Shanhai.

Chapter 869: Guan Shanhai

Seeing the national fortune floating in the air, seemingly having become masterless, Lu Yang recalled the knowledge Meng Jingzhou had previously imparted to him.

The separation of the national fortune from the Xia Emperor’s body can only mean one thing—the Xia Emperor has passed away!

I was still a step too late!

Lu Yang instantly recognized the figure standing in the skies above the imperial palace, who radiated the bearing of a monarch ruling all under heaven. He had seen this elderly man before at the Imperial Taixue Academy—Dean Qi Xiuya, one of the most accomplished historians.

“Why is Dean Qi here?!”

Lu Yang remembered that Qi Xiuya’s cultivation was only at the Fusion Stage. The national fortune concerned the very foundation of Great Xia. It was absolutely not something a Fusion cultivator could meddle with! Even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators wouldn’t dare touch such a thing!

“And this oppressive pressure...”

Originally, Qi Xiuya had his cultivation contained, appearing like an ordinary old man. Perhaps because he had finally obtained the national fortune, he involuntarily released some of his oppressive pressure.

The oppressive pressure that leaked out merely due to his emotional fluctuations enveloped the imperial city and eight nearby cities! Even a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator couldn’t achieve this by releasing their full oppressive pressure.

“An immortal!” Lu Yang was the first to make his judgment.

“Imperial Preceptor, save me!” Seeing the national fortune finally leave the Xia Emperor’s body and Qi Xiuya making his entrance to reap it, General Yu couldn’t help but cry out for help. He was utterly powerless to fight back against the joint attacks of Jin Caiwei and Jiang Lianyi.

“Imperial Preceptor?!”

The only individual whom General Yu would willingly address as “Imperial Preceptor” was the First Imperial Preceptor, Guan Shanhai, who was both teacher and friend to the Yu Emperor Wu Yao and co-founded the Great Yu Dynasty. freewebnovel.com

He was also one of the only two immortals of the Great Yu Dynasty.

The moment the Imperial Preceptor’s identity was confirmed, Lu Yang roughly deduced Great Yu’s scheme.

To seize the power of the national fortune, Guan Shanhai took advantage of the Xia Emperor’s critical condition by instigating turmoil in Yù Province, luring the Jiang Family’s Old Ancestor away to provide aid. This way, he could become the only immortal in the imperial city and could act as he pleased.

If an immortal wished to conceal their identity, they could suppress their cultivation, alter their appearance, and start growing from an infant’s body. With increasing age, they could gradually release the seals on their cultivation.

That way, every step of their growth would leave a traceable record. Even if Great Xia wanted to investigate, they wouldn’t find anything amiss.

It was unknown how long Guan Shanhai had lived incognito in the imperial city. Even his identity as Dean Qi had been used for over a thousand years.

Dean Qi’s students were scattered throughout the world. It was probable that he viewed them as sources of intelligence. For instance, someone like Ye Gu, who served as a private tutor for the Meng Family, could share information about the Meng Family with him.

I knew there was something fishy with Dean Qi. A Fusion cultivator with no grudge against Shifu? Could that be an ordinary person?

“It’s the Great Yu Imperial Preceptor?!” General Yu’s loud cry was heard clearly by more than half the imperial city’s populace. Astonishment spread, and panic instantly ensued.

Although they didn’t know what the national fortune was or why the Great Yu Imperial Preceptor had come, the appearance of an archaic immortal in the imperial city was itself an extremely dangerous sign!

Guan Shanhai ignored the panicked expressions of the imperial city’s inhabitants and General Yu’s shouts. He trod upon the air, approaching the crimson national fortune step by step.

As he neared the national fortune, his appearance also transformed, turning into a middle-aged man with a goatee and sunken cheeks, gradually overlapping with the portraits of him in historical texts.

The national fortune seemed to sense Guan Shanhai’s malicious intent. It swayed restlessly, emitting fluctuations potent enough to make a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s heart palpitate.

But Guan Shanhai simply smiled and reached out to grab the national fortune. It was like a snake catcher seizing a serpent by its vital spot; no matter how the snake writhed, escape was impossible.

“Jiang Ping’an really has some skill to have created something like the national fortune.”

The national fortune was something Jiang Ping’an created after the founding of Great Xia and was thus considered an immortal’s creation. However, unlike the Mother-Child River or the Twins River, the national fortune was directly forged by Jiang Ping’an with the authority of his Dao Fruit. It bore the aspirations of Great Xia’s myriad citizens and was the very foundation of the nation.

After all, it was something Jiang Ping’an had expended immense effort to create. Even if Guan Shanhai wanted to fully obtain the power of the national fortune, he couldn’t accomplish it in a short while.

Nevertheless, Guan Shanhai didn’t need to fully obtain it either. What he valued was the connection between the national fortune and the myriad citizens. Relying on this link, he could transform Great Xia into Great Yu!

The moment he grasped the national fortune, he had already begun refining it.

Refining the national fortune wasn’t particularly difficult but was time-consuming. While refining it, he slowly turned his head to look at General Yu, who had been flattened into a plane and sliced to countless pieces, and then at Jiang Lianyi and Jin Caiwei, who regarded him as a formidable enemy.

“Fellow Daoist Jin, it has been but a few days since we parted at the Imperial Taixue Academy. I didn’t expect us to meet again under such circumstances.” Guan Shanhai smiled without the slightest overbearing presence.

“Fellow Daoist Jiang, the reputation of the Phoenix Ancient Ancestor precedes you. Now that I’ve seen you today, you are indeed extraordinary. Had there not been anyone above you, you would also likely be an immortal.”

Even if Guan Shanhai was sufficiently polite and willing to treat Jiang Lianyi and Jin Caiwei as peers despite his immortal status, it still provoked hostility from both women.

Guan Shanhai acted as though he didn’t see the hostility in their eyes and cupped his hands toward an empty spot.

“And Fellow Daoist Ao Ling, you’ve been hiding here for so long; it’s time you revealed yourself.”

Space rippled in concentric circles. With a grim face, Ao Ling emerged from the space and stared fixedly at Guan Shanhai. Even with her unparalleled concealment abilities, she had nowhere to hide before an immortal’s spiritual consciousness.

“I must ask you three fellow Daoists to release General Yu.” Guan Shanhai’s tone was placid, as if he was discussing a minor matter.

Ao Ling stared at Guan Shanhai for a moment, then slowly exhaled. She understood all too well the gap between an immortal and a half-immortal. This is not an opponent we can defeat.

“Release General Yu.”

Jin Caiwei obediently complied, deactivating her Planary Incipient Dao Fruit and allowing General Yu to regain his three-dimensional form.

However, General Yu was now in numerous small fragments. He would have to rely on his own efforts to reassemble them into his original form.

“Guan thanks you three fellow Daoists. I came to the imperial city solely for the national fortune. I never imagined I would have the opportunity to meet the Qilin Immortal’s three wives. It is truly lucky.” Guan Shanhai hadn’t become the Imperial Taixue Academy’s dean merely to conceal his identity and gather intelligence; he genuinely enjoyed studying history.

Especially ancient history.

“Three wives?”

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi looked at each other. Since when did Hubby have three wives?

Guan Shanhai was also taken aback. “It was Fellow Daoist Jin who told me. Could it be mistaken?”

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi simultaneously turned their heads, fixing their gazes on Jin Caiwei.

Guan Shanhai didn’t dwell on the matter but cupped his hands and continued, “I must trouble the three of you to inform me of the Qilin Immortal’s whereabouts. I have some matters I wish to inquire about with him.”

Ao Ling shook her head. “None of us know where Hubby is.”

Guan Shanhai narrowed his eyes, not believing the three’s words. His tone turned slightly unfriendly. “I believe I have been courteous enough to you three fellow Daoists. Do not mistake my kindness for weakness!

“Tell me the Qilin Immortal’s location, or else you three fellow Daoists will have to remain here today and wait for the Qilin Immortal to come retrieve you!”

Chapter 870: Guan Shanhai’s Bizarre Methods

Unlike Wu Yao, who was single-mindedly focused on leaving the cultivation world for the external world, Guan Shanhai had poured an immeasurable amount of effort into establishing the Great Yu Dynasty.

Yet in the end, the Great Yu Dynasty was destroyed, and Wu Yao even personally sacrificed the dynasty to facilitate his departure from the cultivation world.

Ever since then, he and Wu Yao went their separate ways, never meeting again.

Although Wu Yao had left the cultivation world as he wished, Guan Shanhai had always harbored lingering resentment over the destruction of Great Yu.

When the Great Yu Dynasty fell, the Qilin Immortal had also made an appearance. However, Guan Shanhai was unclear about the role the Qilin Immortal played in its destruction. I must meet the Qilin Immortal and get a clear answer!

Previously, only Jin Caiwei was present, and he wasn’t certain of Jin Caiwei’s standing in the Qilin Immortal’s heart. Acting then would have alerted Jiang Ping’an, preventing him from seizing the national fortune.

But now, all three of the Qilin Immortal’s wives are here. I refuse to believe that the Qilin Immortal won’t show himself if the three of them are captured!

The right time, the right place, and the right people—all three are on my side.

“Since you are unwilling to tell me, you shall all remain here!”

Guan Shanhai shed his previous respectful demeanor, his expression turning cold like a sovereign wielding power over life and death, before whom everyone was but a straw dog. Although he was reluctant to offend the Heavenly Court, he absolutely needed to obtain information about the Qilin Immortal.

Jin Caiwei repeated her tactic, sending forth countless bone fragments compressed into planes. They blotted out the sky and covered the earth, leaving no room for evasion.

Guan Shanhai walked unhurriedly toward Jin Caiwei, allowing the bone fragments to strike him. The bone fragments that had sliced General Yu into pieces couldn’t inflict the slightest injury upon Guan Shanhai.

“If I am not mistaken, you wield a spatial type Incipient Dao Fruit that can eliminate the concept of ‘height.’ Compressing the bone fragments into planes is a clever idea. Unfortunately, you are unaware of the might of an immortal’s body.” freewebnovel.com

Guan Shanhai didn’t even need to activate his Dao Fruit; his immortal body alone could block all the bone fragments.

An immortal was an existence on an entirely different level. Half-immortals, after all, hadn’t completed their metamorphosis and were still considered mortals. Those capable of harming an immortal with mortal means were exceedingly rare.

“Let’s capture one first.” Guan Shanhai approached Jin Caiwei. His steps appeared slow, but in reality, every step employed Close Horizon From Cliff. He loomed like a towering mountain, frightening Jin Caiwei so much that she didn’t dare to budge an inch.

“Dream on!” Ao Ling growled, transforming into a black true dragon. With her indestructible dragon horns, she rammed into Guan Shanhai, sending him flying.

“Interesting. Intelligence gathered from the East Sea mentioned that you could temporarily attain an immortal’s body. There is some substance to it.”

Ao Ling had prepared thoroughly. Before Lu Yang set out to deliver the immortal peach to the imperial palace, she had Jiang Lianyi beat her up, allowing her to rapidly elevate to an immortal’s body.

Now it seemed fortunate that she had prepared adequately.

Facing an immortal foe, the three women didn’t dare be negligent. All three revealed their true forms: a white qiongqi, a five-colored immortal phoenix, and a jet-black true dragon. The three immortal beasts were colossal, several times larger than the imperial city’s mountains. They blotted out the sky and sun, as if ancient legends had been reborn.

Sensing the oppressive pressure of the immortal beasts, the cultivator below in the imperial city trembled like chaff in a sieve, unable to stand steadily.

“Heh, do you think having an immortal’s body can protect the other two?” Guan Shanhai chuckled softly and retrieved a corpse that no one recognized from his storage ring. The only thing certain was that the deceased had been a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.

The corpse had a middle-aged appearance. However, as Guan Shanhai placed his hand over the corpse’s face, its form gradually changed, transforming from a middle-aged man with only a few lines on his face into an elder with a face full of wrinkles.

Ao Ling furrowed her brows, unable to discern what Guan Shanhai was doing.

What no one expected was that the deeply wrinkled old man suddenly opened his eyes and awoke!

Before long, someone below recognized the identity of the wrinkled elder, their voice quivering. “He is...the Second Imperial Preceptor of Great Yu!”

Great Yu’s Second Imperial Preceptor was a pivotal figure who shaped the course of Great Yu’s history, and his portrait was widely circulated.

He was also once killed by the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“What kind of technique is this?!” Jin Caiwei was astonished. The deceased resurrecting? But the revived person doesn’t even look like he did when he was dead. It’s not even the same person.

“Shifu, where am I?” The Second Imperial Preceptor looked at Guan Shanhai with a bewildered expression, equally clueless about what had happened.

Guan Shanhai affectionately caressed his disciple’s head. He offered no further explanation, simply pointing at Jin Caiwei and Jiang Lianyi. “Go and capture those two. You may injure them, but you must keep them alive.”

“As you command!” Out of trust in his shifu, the Second Imperial Preceptor didn’t hesitate, vanishing before everyone’s eyes.

Everyone forgot his existence. Even Ao Ling and the other two were only warily watching Guan Shanhai, completely forgetting what had just transpired.

Suddenly, Jin Caiwei felt a heavy blow strike her back—a spirit blade was embedded in her back.

Only then did everyone remember the existence of the Second Imperial Preceptor and recall the earlier events.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi remembered what Lu Yang had once shared with them. Great Yu’s Second Imperial Preceptor possessed the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, allowing him to erase his own karma. If not for encountering the Everlasting Immortal Bu Yaolian the last time, who happened to counter him, even other half-immortals would have found him difficult to deal with.

None of the three women had witnessed this move of Guan Shanhai’s. It was a Dao Fruit that hadn’t appeared even in the ancient era, including its incipient form!

Jiang Lianyi released a five-colored divine light, which enveloped Jin Caiwei to heal her injuries.

Guan Shanhai smiled as he looked at Ao Ling’s grave countenance. “Now, what will you do? And how long can your immortal body last?”

Ao Ling’s expression changed. Indeed, I can’t maintain my immortal body indefinitely. Guan Shanhai’s methods are bizarre and hard to counter. Even escaping is impossible. This is a deadlock.

Witnessing this scene from below, Lu Yang grew extremely anxious. He hastily shook the sleeping Everlasting Immortal Fairy awake.

“Immortal Fairy, wake up! Something big has happened!”

Within the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy woke up from the broad, comfortable throne, grumbling twice before reluctantly rousing.

“What’s the matter, waking this immortal up? Has the boring play-acting ended?”

“The Xia Emperor is dead!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy yawned widely, unsurprised by the news. “Then that just means the play-acting has ended.”

Lu Yang was taken aback.

Suddenly, a hearty laugh resonated across the skies above the imperial city. The sound seemed both near and far, elusive and unpredictable. Guan Shanhai was about to capture the three women when he stiffened abruptly.

“Fellow Daoist Guan, how is the refinement of the national fortune coming along?”

Guan Shanhai searched everywhere for the voice’s owner. He had heard this voice before, though he couldn’t immediately recall where. Seeming to sense something, his gaze traversed from the north of the imperial city to the south, where the Meng Estate was located.

Above the Meng Estate, a young man’s figure smiled as he looked at Guan Shanhai, even waving his hand as if greeting an old friend he hadn’t seen in ages.

Guan Shanhai’s memory was pulled back a hundred thousand years. At that time, it was a chaotic era after the fall of Great Yu. Two major factions rose to contend for supremacy—one whose surname was Jiang, and the other whose surname was Meng.

For the final battle for supremacy, the two abandoned an army-on-army confrontation and instead chose to determine the future emperor through a one-on-one duel.

In that battle, Jiang Ping’an became an immortal.

And the man surnamed Meng had also left a deep impression on Guan Shanhai.

“Meng Junzi!”

Chapter 871: An Act

Guan Shanhai’s voice reverberated throughout the entire imperial city, from aristocrats and ministers down to commoners. Upon hearing the name “Meng Junzi,” everyone shuddered involuntarily. Even children learning to read and write in private schools had heard of the name.

The Meng Family’s Old Ancestor had once contended for supremacy against the Jiang Family. Although the Jiang Family ultimately triumphed and established Great Xia, the Meng Family was unlike the vanquished clans of previous dynastic struggles that were purged and wiped out. On the contrary, the Meng Family had flourished, becoming the number one ancestral clan of Great Xia.

While this was in part due to the Jiang Family’s Old Ancestor cherishing past ties, more importantly, it was because the Meng Family held deep foundations.

The Meng Family originated from the Great Yu era, but at the time, they were merely an ordinary ancestral clan. The one who truly led the Meng Family to greatness and glory, amassing their rich heritage, was Meng Junzi, who became the family head toward the end of the Great Yu era.

“Fellow Daoist Guan, such intense hostility isn’t nice.” Meng Junzi stood with his hands clasped behind his back, emanating an upright and tranquil aura that dispelled the immortal’s oppressive pressure shrouding the imperial city.

“You really did become an immortal!” If Guan Shanhai had been skeptical before, Meng Junzi’s display now confirmed he was an immortal just like himself.

Meng Jungzi’s appearance shocked everyone, including Meng Jingzhou.

Meng Jingzhou stared wide-eyed at the old ancestor standing above him, his jaw dropping in astonishment. Wait, Old Ancestor, so you did become an immortal.

Man Gu was also quite taken aback. I have only been in the imperial city for two hours and have already encountered two immortals. I knew following Brother Lu and Brother Meng would broaden my horizons.

Meng Junzi had only made an appearance right after the founding of Great Xia. Since then, he had never been seen again. People speculated that after losing to Jiang Ping’an, he became disheartened and sealed himself away.

Guan Shanhai had thought the same. Jiang Ping’an and Meng Jungzi—these two prodigies from later generations are too brilliant to ignore. Otherwise, I wouldn’t have used my identity as Imperial Taixue Academy Dean to send a student to teach at the Meng Estate’s private school.

Back then, I had personally witnessed Meng Junzi seal himself and instruct his descendants to bury him within the Meng Estate’s mountain.

Now it seems that his self-sealing was an act performed for me.

Why would an immortal need to seal themselves?!

Guan Shanhai glared fixedly at Meng Junzi, trying to recall when Meng Junzi had become an immortal right under his nose and where the Immortal Ascension Tribulation had taken place.

Suddenly, he understood. Meng Junzi had already become an immortal a hundred thousand years ago.

“Back then, Wu Yao and I simultaneously achieved immortality at the nation-founding ceremony. You and Jiang Ping’an were the same, both attaining immortality during the final decisive battle!

“I never would have imagined; you never once employed your Dao Fruit’s power, continuously masquerading as a half-immortal. Such forbearance! Meng Junzi, I’ve truly underestimated you!”

Meng Junzi smiled. “Fishing requires patience, after all. See how we have a catch today?”

Guan Shanhai had always acted with utmost caution, avoiding combat whenever possible. Battles could be won or lost, but by not fighting, he would remain undefeated forever. That was why he had lured Jiang Ping’an away. Had he known that Meng Junzi was also an immortal, he would never have appeared in the imperial city.

As if he hadn’t heard Meng Junzi’s provocation, Guan Shanhai sneered. “When I ordered General Yu to intercept the immortal peach, you didn’t even show yourself, merely watching as the Xia Emperor passed away. Truly heartless.”

These were words meant to castigate Meng Junzi’s ulterior motives. Guan Shanhai deliberately brought this up, letting everyone in the imperial city hear it to send a clear message to Great Xia’s citizens: “Your so-called emperor is merely a tool pushed forward by immortals for schemes and machinations.”

This is something that can shake the Emperor’s standing in the people’s hearts!

Meng Junzi was not at all anxious, remaining leisurely as ever. “And how can you be certain that the Xia Emperor truly died?

“Or rather, was the Xia Emperor’s lifespan truly nearing its end?”

~~~

“What do you mean by ‘play-acting?’ The Xia Emperor didn’t die of old age? Is there still time to deliver the immortal peach now?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was still not fully awake and continued to yawn, her eyes bleary. “Immortal peach? Didn’t Lass Yun say she only found one? Who knows where the World Natural Spiritual Root ran off to? It’s really good stuff, Xiao Yangzi; you should eat it. After all, the Xia Emperor’s depleted lifespan was just an act.”

“An act?”

Lu Yang was flabbergasted. He had thought the “play-acting” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mentioned referred to the Xia Emperor’s passing. But from the sound of it, even the problem with the Xia Emperor’s lifespan was all an act?!

Hearing Lu Yang’s raised pitch, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy finally became awake and added, “If he were about to die soon, why would this immortal make him Prime Minister?”

“Immortal Fairy, you knew from the start that the Xia Emperor’s limited lifespan was an act?”

“Not exactly from the start. It was during those three months when this immortal was the acting sect leader, preparing for the Dao-Seeking Sect’s 120,000-year celebration. Didn’t we go to the imperial palace for a meeting and meet the Xia Emperor then? That was when this immortal realized he was putting on an act.”

“But wasn’t that the first meeting?!”

This was something even Yun Zhi hadn’t anticipated. The Xia Emperor’s act could fool Lu Yang, fool the world, and fool Guan Shanhai, but it couldn’t fool the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who possessed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and commanded authority over life and death.

Lu Yang recalled something.

Initially, it was Big Senior Sister who told the Immortal Fairy and me that the Xia Emperor’s time was nearly spent and asked the Immortal Fairy if there were any lifespan-extending immortal items. The Immortal Fairy said she could give the Xia Emperor an Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit and make him the Fourth-in-Command. Only after Big Senior Sister rejected this proposal did the Immortal Fairy mention the immortal peach.

And ever since the Immortal Fairy went to the imperial palace and saw the Xia Emperor, she never again brought up the matter of making him the Fourth-in-Command.

On top of that, after she defeated the four great immortal sect leaders in the imperial palace, she even proposed challenging the Xia Emperor. If the Xia Emperor’s lifespan had really been limited at the time, the Immortal Fairy wouldn’t have done that.

Lu Yang figured it out. From the very beginning, this entire matter had been a trap laid for Guan Shanhai.

No wonder Big Senior Sister hadn’t delivered the immortal peach directly to the imperial palace but had Man Gu pass it to me. She had never intended for the Xia Emperor to consume the immortal peach to extend his life.

If the Xia Emperor had extended his lifespan, the national fortune would have remained within him, and Guan Shanhai wouldn’t have revealed himself.

The purpose of the immortal peach was to make Guan Shanhai intercept it, thereby convincing him that the Xia Emperor was truly at death’s door.

~~~

Guan Shanhai’s expression was so dark that it seemed water could drip from it.

He hadn’t expected everything to be false.

He had been closely monitoring the Xia Emperor’s movements recently, even observing him up close as Dean Qi, yet he hadn’t detected that the Xia Emperor was putting on an act. freewebnovel.com

Guan Shanhai was a suspicious person by nature, but the recent changes in the imperial city did make it seem like the Xia Emperor was dying. First, the Xia Emperor had the First Imperial Prince handle state affairs and test his capabilities. However, the First Imperial Prince was unwilling to inherit the throne, so the Xia Emperor eliminated the Fourth Imperial Prince and the Fifth Imperial Prince in succession, forcing the First Imperial Prince to succeed the throne.

“Well, well, well. I, Guan, have spent my whole life scheming against others, yet I was schemed against by a bunch of juniors!”

Chapter 872: Great Yu’s Imperial Preceptor’s Dao Fruit

“But do you truly believe you have me in your pocket?!”

Although Guan Shanhai had been schemed against, he showed no panic. I’m simply unwilling to fight, not incapable of it! Moreover, Meng Junzi still doesn’t know what my Dao Fruit is.

However, Meng Junzi’s next words made his heart skip a beat.

“If I am not mistaken, Fellow Daoist Guan, the function of your Dao Fruit is ‘assimilation,’ capable of completely transforming one person into another. Otherwise, you could not possibly restore Great Yu.”

Long ago, Meng Junzi and Jiang Ping’an had noticed Guan Shanhai’s existence and his desire to restore the Great Yu Dynasty.

Guan Shanhai’s Dao Fruit wasn’t recorded in any historical texts. Restoring Great Yu wasn’t as simple as eliminating the Jiang Family and replacing them. After a hundred years of evolution, Great Xia was a completely different dynasty from Great Yu.

Both suspected that Guan Shanhai’s Dao Fruit could facilitate the restoration of Great Yu, and they had formed many conjectures about it. Having witnessed Guan Shanhai transform a corpse into the Second Imperial Preceptor earlier, Meng Junzi finally confirmed his hypothesis.

In fact, Meng Junzi’s guess slightly deviated from the truth. Guan Shanhai had named his Dao Fruit the “Imprint Dao Fruit.” For instance, he could use a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator’s corpse as a vessel and imprint his memory of the Second Imperial Preceptor onto it.

This wasn’t merely copying memories—even one’s appearance, bodily memories, Incipient Dao Fruit, instinctive reactions, and special physiques could be fully replicated, almost indistinguishable from resurrection!

However, he was unaware of what had transpired after the Second Imperial Preceptor entered the Dao-Seeking Sect. Hence, the imprinted version of the Second Imperial Preceptor lacked the memories of his final moments.

Using a living person as a vessel yielded better results. Imprinting on a corpse produced only a body with memories, whereas imprinting on a living person could completely alter that person’s soul into another’s!

The power of the national fortune was connected to Great Xia’s populace. This was precisely what Guan Shanhai valued.

In his mind, he held the full panorama of the early Great Yu era, the period Great Xia called the “Wu Yao Golden Age.” Every person, event, and object was etched clearly in his memory. The “Wu Yao Golden Age” lasted three hundred thousand years, and he remembered everything.

Leveraging the national fortune, he could imprint the people of the “Wu Yao Golden Age” onto present-day Great Xia, transforming its citizens into people of that era!

For example, he could employ his Imprint Dao Fruit to turn Lu Yang into a genius from the Wu Yao Golden Age. Only then could he call it the restoration of Great Yu.

In reality, he didn’t need the national fortune to transform Great Xia into the Great Yu he envisioned, but that process would be tremendously slow, and Jiang Ping’an would undoubtedly intervene. It was far less efficient than using the national fortune.

However, he hadn’t even begun the preliminary refinement of the national fortune. Since Meng Junzi appeared, he had been on high alert, not daring to divide his attention to the refinement process.

~~~

A figure was anxiously directing an army into the imperial city.

“Hurry, hurry! Everyone, quickly take the positions I’ve assigned! Deploy the great array! If there’s the slightest mistake, be prepared to face military discipline!”

This was the Imperial City Army Guard, stationed in the vicinity of the imperial city. Now that the imperial city was in peril, though they couldn’t influence the outcome of an immortal battle, they could erect a barrier to prevent the city from being swept up in the clash.

The person commanding them was none other than Meng Jingzhou’s third uncle, Meng Poci, the former frontier grand general who had guarded the Demon Confinement Pass, known as a “scholar-general.”

Meng Poci looked up at the two prominent figures in the sky. He clutched the transfer order he had just received and murmured softly, “I was transferred from the Demon Confinement Pass to the imperial city last year—could it have been for today’s battle?”

The Imperial City Guard’s commander wasn’t originally Meng Poci. However, after the Xia Emperor’s feigned death and Guan Shanhai’s appearance, Meng Poci suddenly received an auditory message from Meng Junzi, ordering him to swiftly go to the imperial city’s barracks and take command of the Imperial City Guard. He was even given a transfer order stamped with the imperial jade seal.

Meng Poci was dumbfounded upon seeing Meng Junzi. He hadn’t expected his old ancestor to appear at this time. Setting aside his shock, he rushed to the military camp outside the imperial city.

Great Xia’s army had many veteran generals whose seniority and cultivation surpassed Meng Poci’s. But when it came to defensive arrays, Meng Poci was unrivalled.

~~~

Guan Shanhai hadn’t noticed the commotion below. He didn’t care about the imperial city’s reaction. All this time, his only formidable foe was Meng Junzi.

“Fellow Daoists of the Heavenly Court, how about leaving this matter to me?” Meng Junzi politely addressed Ao Ling’s trio. He also knew they were on the same side.

Ao Ling’s trio couldn’t intervene in an immortal battle, and Ao Ling’s time in her immortal body was nearly up. Staying here would only become a hindrance to Meng Junzi, so the three tactfully withdrew from the battlefield.

“It seems a battle between us is inevitable,” Guan Shanhai said with a smile that didn’t reach his eyes.

At the same time, the Second Imperial Preceptor erased his own karma, vanished into thin air, and suddenly appeared behind Meng Junzi. He raised a dagger forged from immortal stone and fiercely plunged it toward Meng Junzi’s head.

Meng Junzi reached out his hand to seize the Second Imperial Preceptor’s wrist and crushed it. “The Karma Incipient Dao Fruit is indeed tricky to deal with, but that’s for half-immortals. For an immortal, it’s not even worth a glance!”

The Second Imperial Preceptor’s wrist shattered, and the dagger fell along with it. Meng Junzi extended a hand to pick up the spoils. This thing can be considered an immortal treasure and is quite rare.

Boom!

The dagger exploded without warning, spreading poisonous green smoke around Meng Junzi.

This was a venomous mist condensed from the lingering resentment of hundreds of millions of the dead at the end of the Great Qian era. Those poisoned would be plagued by this resentment, leading to their self-destruction and death.

The Second Imperial Preceptor seized this opportunity to flee far away, also leaving the battlefield. He excelled at ambush and curses, but neither was effective against immortals. The true purpose of his earlier ambush was to make the dagger self-detonate.

Meng Junzi heard countless wails around him, blaming Heaven for its injustice and bringing war to the world, and blaming the dynasty for its tyranny and disregarding the people’s lives.

“Stop wailing. You make it sound like these matters were my fault.” Meng Junzi was completely unaffected by the resentful energy. He directly inhaled all the rancorous mist.

No matter how my opponents judge me, I’ve always acted with integrity and have a clear conscience.

After Meng Junzi absorbed the mist, he discovered five figures standing behind Guan Shanhai—General Yu, the Nightmare Supreme Lord, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, the Wooden Seal Savant, and the Yu Emperor Wu Yao when he was a half-immortal.

Five half-immortals!

Apart from General Yu, the other four were imprinted with Transcendent Tribulation corpses as vessels. General Yu knew what was happening, but the other four were clueless.

Wu Yao’s expression changed drastically. I remember my teacher and I had dealt with the Nightmare Supreme Lord, and we were about to conquer the final province. Also, Teacher should be a half-immortal.

But here, the Nightmare Supreme Lord is still around, Teacher has already become an immortal, and the massive city below doesn’t belong to any place in my memory.

Connecting this to Teacher’s Imprint Dao Fruit, it isn’t hard to guess that I’m an imprinted person.

“Teacher, what time period is it now? Who are you fighting?!”

Guan Shanhai frowned almost imperceptibly. This is the drawback of imprinted people—they are identical to the real person and not under my control.

Chapter 873: Borrow

Although Guan Shanhai was both a teacher and a friend to Wu Yao, and Wu Yao still addressed him as “teacher,” this didn’t mean that Wu Yao placed the same absolute trust in Guan Shanhai as the Second Imperial Preceptor did.

Wu Yao’s curiosity surpassed everything else. His cultivation journey began with his curiosity about a cultivation manual found on a deceased cultivator. Subsequently, his rapid improvement in cultivation came from his curiosity about what higher cultivation realms felt like. Driven by curiosity, he established the Great Yu Dynasty, cultivated until he became an immortal, and even sacrificed the dynasty to discover what lay beyond their world.

The Wu Yao imprinted by Guan Shanhai had a personality identical to the real one. He wanted to know what had happened, why the real him wasn’t here, and why they were fighting now.

Before Guan Shanhai could answer, the Nightmare Supreme Lord staggered several steps back, his expression looking like he had just seen a ghost, his voice quivering. “Guan Shanhai, w-w-w-when did you become an immortal?!”

The Nightmare Supreme Lord’s memories still lingered in the late Great Qian era, where the battle for supremacy was ongoing. At the time, he had defeated countless formidable enemies, including General Yu. To establish a new dynasty, he still needed to defeat the rising star Wu Yao and his teacher, Guan Shanhai.

But even Guan Shanhai has become a damned immortal? How am I supposed to establish a f*cking new dynasty?

The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord and the Wooden Seal Savant also had disbelief painted on their faces upon seeing the three legendary figures—Guan Shanhai, Wu Yao, and the Nightmare Supreme Lord.

Seeing the half-immortals whom he imprinted making a din, each with varied expressions, Guan Shanhai felt a wave of exhaustion. We haven’t even fought yet, and they’ve already become a laughingstock.

Guan Shanhai sighed. In a battle between immortals, every second counted. With a thought, he stripped away the four’s lives and devoured their Incipient Dao Fruits in spite of their terrified expressions.

Although he couldn’t control the thoughts of those he imprinted, he could control the imprinted Incipient Dao Fruits. However, a person and their Incipient Dao Fruit were closely connected, so he couldn’t imprint just the Incipient Dao Fruit.

Hence, he acquired four Incipient Dao Fruits: the Dreamscape Incipient Dao Fruit, the Replacement Incipient Dao Fruit, the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit, and the Wooden Seal Savant’s Rejuvenation Incipient Dao Fruit.

Guan Shanhai instantly accelerated his own time, making himself so fast that Meng Junzi’s spiritual consciousness couldn’t react. To those below, it appeared as if he had vanished into thin air.

“Nine-Cycle Imperishable Golden Body.”

Guan Shanhai activated a mystic Buddhist art. Having endured nine ordeals to forge an imperishable golden body, he transformed into a great golden Buddha. He had used this golden body method to survive his Immortal Ascension Tribulation. Now that he employed it again as an immortal, one could imagine how incredibly tough his immortal body had become, almost as if it were eternally indestructible.

Among everyone in the imperial city, only Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could clearly see what Guan Shanhai was doing.

Watching Guan Shanhai continuously accelerate his time, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy smiled. “Quite resourceful—using the Myriad Spells kid’s Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit to accelerate his own time and then reinforcing his body, making the power in every move rival that of an immortal artifact.”

Like a ghost, Guan Shanhai appeared behind Meng Junzi. His fingers merged into a golden immortal saber, planning to behead Meng Junzi. His hand was also imbued with a curse. Even if Meng Junzi could reattach his head, it would still damage his vitality.

However, to Guan Shanhai’s surprise, Meng Junzi merely tilted his head back slightly, evading the strike!

“How is this possible? You can see me?” Guan Shanhai couldn’t help but be astonished. This initial strike had actually missed.

“Great Compassion Seal!”

“Overturning Heaven!”

“Boundless Primordial Magnetism Immortal Art!”

A Buddha’s hand larger than the imperial city blotted out the sun, tearing through layers of clouds and crashing down. Guan Shanhai carried the might of “Overturning Heaven” as he struck a palm toward Meng Junzi’s chest. The two warping forces, one positive and one negative, trapped Meng Junzi between them, seeking to distort his physical form.

Guan Shanhai unleashed three peerless immortal techniques in succession, each one powerful enough to crush a half-immortal. Only Ao Ling would fare slightly better; her immortal body would be broken, but she could barely survive. Even an immortal who suffered the blow without any defense would vomit blood profusely.

The only two weaknesses of these immortal techniques were their slow activation and inadequate attack speed. But with Guan Shanhai’s own time accelerated, even those two weaknesses disappeared.

“Heaven-Earth Dharma Manifestation, Heaven-Mending Technique, Endless Creation.”

To Guan Shanhai’s surprise, Meng Junzi also unleashed three peerless immortal techniques in an extremely short time.

Meng Junzi transformed into a colossal Heaven-Earth Dharma Manifestation, feet planted on the earth. He pierced through the Buddha hand descending from the sky, letting light return to the imperial city. He used the ancient Heaven-Mending Technique to block Overturning Heaven’s might and performed a creation spell to neutralize the positive and negative warping forces, effortlessly resolving the three-pronged assault.

“How is this possible? Shouldn’t you have the Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit?!”

Toward the end of the Great Yu era, he had paid close attention to Meng Junzi and Jiang Ping’an, using his powerful immortal consciousness to monitor them constantly. He had long learned of their Incipient Dao Fruits.

Meng Junzi had possessed the Borrowing and Lending Incipient Dao Fruit. Its most common usage was to “borrow” an enemy’s magical treasures, spirit stones, and other items. This left the opponent unarmed while he was fully equipped, making them utterly unable to fight him.

But the issue is that the Borrowing-Lending Incipient Dao Fruit’s applications had absolutely nothing to do with time. Otherwise, I wouldn’t have been so confident in engaging him in battle!

“Immortal Fairy, what’s going on? Can the Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit also borrow time?” Lu Yang asked, unable to make sense of a high-level combat like this.

Unlike Guan Shanhai, who was still trying to process what happened, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was knowledgeable and had discerned some clues. “Interesting. Meng Junzi probably didn’t borrow time just now; he simply increased his speed.

“This reminds me of an enemy the Epoch Immortal encountered on his path to immortality. That person wielded the Speed Incipient Dao Fruit, claiming to be the embodiment of the world’s ultimate speed. When speed reaches a certain level, it becomes related to time. Therefore, between that person and the Epoch Immortal, only one could become an immortal.”

Lu Yang theorized, “Could it be that someone in your era also grasped the Speed Incipient Dao Fruit? And Meng Junzi’s Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit can borrow others’ Incipient Dao Fruits?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied, “Do you remember the Meng Family’s ‘Borrowing Spell?’ When cultivators at the Fusion Stage or above borrow money from the Meng Family, they not only leave a promissory note but also lend the Meng Family one of their moves. This ability is something this immortal has never seen before. It must have been developed by the Meng Family; perhaps it evolved from the Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit.”

“That powerful?” Lu Yang was startled. “Wait, if even Incipient Dao Fruits can be borrowed, could lifespan also be borrowed?” Realization suddenly dawned upon Lu Yang.

Since the Xia Emperor could deceive an immortal like the Imperial Preceptor into believing that his lifespan was depleted, it suggests that the Imperial Preceptor hadn’t encountered something like this before, and that this ability should be considered to be at the “immortal” level.

The Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit perfectly matches both conditions.

“That’s likely the case.”

Chapter 874: The Second Dao Fruit That Won’t Be Forgotten

While Guan Shanhai and Meng Junzi’s battle intensified, a half-immortal battle also broke out in a corner of the imperial city, where Ao Ling’s trio clashed with the imprinted Second Imperial Preceptor.

After the Second Imperial Preceptor left the main battlefield, Ao Ling’s trio had directly confronted him.

The Second Imperial Preceptor had ambushed and stabbed Jin Caiwei, and she was determined to have her revenge.

Worried that Jin Caiwei might meet with a mishap, Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi also joined the fight. The Second Imperial Preceptor was an intractable opponent, for he could erase his own karma, becoming elusive and unpredictable.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy noticed the commotion over there. Although she could clearly see the Second Imperial Preceptor’s position, she didn’t inform the three women.

It’s a good chance for them to gain experience battling with the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit. Anyway, with me watching, nothing will go wrong.

General Yu pondered for a bit and decided to lend a hand to the Second Imperial Preceptor.

On one side, it was an immortal battle; on the other, a battle between five half-immortals. Both were legendary clashes not to be missed. Even during the ancient era, when half-immortals were abundant, battles of this caliber were rare.

The imperial city’s cultivators wished they had eight eyes to watch both fights simultaneously. They would never have another opportunity in their lifetimes to witness battles of such magnitude.

However, both battles were rather difficult to observe. In the immortal battle, Guan Shanhai and Meng Junzi moved at absurd speeds, far beyond what these spectating cultivators could follow with their eyes.

As for the five half-immortals, the Second Imperial Preceptor flickered in and out of existence. When he vanished, memories of him also disappeared, making it difficult for the cultivators below to catch a glimpse.

General Yu somewhat regretted helping the Second Imperial Preceptor. When the Second Imperial Preceptor disappeared, he couldn’t withstand all of the attacks from Ao Ling’s trio landing on him.

~~~

Initially, Guan Shanhai thought that using only the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit would resolve the battle. Now it seems that I had underestimated Meng Junzi.

The two immortals fought at extreme speeds. Various large-scale divine abilities clashed, painting the imperial city’s sky in patches of blue and red, as if dye vats had overturned.

Suddenly, Guan Shanhai had a momentary lapse, his reaction slowed by a beat. Meng Junzi executed Black Tiger Heart Strike, hitting Guan Shanhai’s chest. Even the latter’s golden body was ripped open with a large gash.

Meng Junzi practiced another body refinement technique, whose might was no less than Guan Shanhai’s Nine-Cycle Imperishable Golden Body.

Guan Shanhai’s face flushed, and he vomited a large mouthful of blood. The immortal blood splattered onto the barrier deployed over the imperial city, causing it to shake, and the barrier struggled to hold up against the immortal blood’s power.

Meng Poci knew that if this happened a few more times, the array would develop gaps from the residual shockwaves. He hastily dispatched people to request all Transcendent Tribulation cultivators in the imperial city to step forth and reinforce the array.

However, Guan Shanhai quickly recovered. The wound on his chest healed rapidly, as if he had never been injured.

Meng Junzi raised an eyebrow. “The ‘undying’ trait of the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit? No, the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit shouldn’t allow such swift recovery. Let me guess. Among the four people you created, there was only one whom I didn’t recognize. His Incipient Dao Fruit is related to recovery, right?”

Guan Shanhai naturally wouldn’t answer an enemy’s question.

Lu Yang knew Meng Junzi was referring to the Wood Seal Savant, a cultivator from the mid-Great Qian era and also a good friend of the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord. Historical materials recorded him as a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, but according to the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, the Wood Seal Savant was actually a half-immortal.

The Wood Seal Savant had died in his slumber. Lu Yang speculated that he knew something about the Ember Legacy Dynasty and was silenced by Hui Doudou.

“Wait, if the Wood Seal Savant’s Incipient Dao Fruit is related to recovery, doesn’t that conflict with the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit? How did they become friends?” Lu Yang was perplexed.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained smugly, “What’s so hard to understand? The Wood Seal Savant’s Incipient Dao Fruit likely belongs to the ‘eternity’ category, meaning it keeps one’s own state unchanging. Ultimately, the upper Dao Fruit is still this immortal’s Everlasting Dao Fruit.
