“The Everlasting Dao Fruit and the Eternity Dao Fruits are extremely difficult to condense. Even if this immortal weren’t here, he couldn’t become an immortal.

“The same goes for that Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit. Its difficulty is so great that without this immortal and the Epoch Immortal, no one could have become an immortal.

“Since neither could become an immortal, they naturally could become friends.”

Just then, Guan Shanhai hurled countless magical treasures, but not at Meng Junzi, and instead scattered them throughout the skies above the imperial city.

Meng Junzi attacked Guan Shanhai at extreme speed, only to see Guan Shanhai vanish into thin air, replaced by a magical treasure that appeared from nowhere.

That magical treasure shattered upon Meng Junzi’s touch, breaking into countless fragments.

Without any warning, Guan Shanhai appeared behind Meng Junzi, attacking again with the Overturning Heaven momentum. Caught off guard, Meng Junzi was struck and also spat blood.

Meng Junzi whirled around to look at Guan Shanhai, only to find the magical treasures Guan Shanhai had previously tossed behind him. Through some method, Guan Shanhai had moved to a faraway location.

Wiping the blood from the corner of his mouth, Meng Junzi revealed a faint smile of realization. “I got it. You exchanged positions with the magical treasures.” One of the functions of the Replacement Incipient Dao Fruit was to exchange positions with any of one’s possessions.

It was useless even if Meng Junzi shattered the treasures. They were still Guan Shanhai’s possessions, and he could still exchange positions with them.

Meng Junzi continued his assault without batting an eyelid. Guan Shanhai exchanged positions with a magical treasure again, moving far away. However, Meng Junzi also traversed space, catching up to Guan Shanhai.

This time, even without the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s explanation, Lu Yang could tell that Meng Junzi was borrowing the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s Space Incipient Dao Fruit. freewebnovel.com

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, since Senior Meng Junzi has the Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit, doesn’t that mean he doesn’t have the immortal trait of oblivion like you?”

When an immortal employed their Dao Fruit’s abilities, the world would forget. It was the case for the Four Ancient Immortals and Jiang Ping’an’s Dao Fruit. Only the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t possess such a trait.

Lu Yang felt that the Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit also lacked the immortal trait of oblivion. Otherwise, Meng Junzi could simply borrow things and never return them.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t considered this issue. Hearing Lu Yang bring it up, she began to contemplate seriously. “Now that you mention it, it seems that is indeed the case.”

Lu Yang added, “Assuming the Xia Emperor’s lifespan was borrowed by Meng Junzi, that would count as a Dao Fruit ability and should be forgotten by the world. But in reality, it wasn’t. Everyone knew the Xia Emperor had a problem with his lifespan.”

Suddenly, a familiar voice came from behind Lu Yang. “Oh, I didn’t expect Little Junior Brother to have considered even this layer. Senior Immortal Fairy has indeed told you many things that you shouldn’t be privy to at your current cultivation level.”

Yun Zhi stood quietly under an old tree, clad in a plain white dress. Time seemed to freeze. She appeared to have just arrived, yet it also felt like she had been standing there all along.

Sunlight filtered through the sparse leaves, casting dappled, shifting shadows. Her figure seemed particularly cool and detached.

“Big Senior Sister!” Lu Yang called out in delight.

The moment he learned that the Xia Emperor’s death was a ruse, Lu Yang realized that Yun Zhi had long since arrived in the imperial city.

This is an immortal battle; she can’t possibly let me supervise it.

Nevertheless, it is still very heartening to see Big Senior Sister here.

Chapter 875: Meng Junzi Alone Will Suffice

“Lass Yun, don’t speak nonsense! What do you mean this immortal told Xiao Yangzi things he shouldn’t know? It was clearly because Xiao Yangzi was quick-witted and figured these things out himself!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy naturally couldn’t admit that she casually told Lu Yang knowledge meant for immortals whenever she had nothing better to do.

I didn’t tell him; Lu Yang comprehended it all himself.

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, do you think I could comprehend the abilities of Dao Fruits or deduce the traits of immortals all on my own?

Yun Zhi stepped out from under the old tree, her plain white dress dazzling under the sunlight. “Little Junior Brother, it seems you’ve been doing well in the imperial city.”

When Man Gu reached the imperial city, Yun Zhi had also arrived secretly. While waiting for Guan Shanhai to take the bait, she had inquired about Lu Yang’s deeds during his stay in the imperial city.

She hadn’t expected Lu Yang to have such an eventful time in just three months—battling imperial city prodigies, composing poetry at the Shangyuan Festival, reporting the Fourth Imperial Prince’s rebellion, encountering Ao Ling’s trio, persuading the Fifth Imperial Prince’s subordinates to turn themselves in, making the Xia Emperor the Prime Minister, and infiltrating the imperial palace at night to steal the throne... An ordinary prodigy would find any single one of these feats as challenging as climbing to the sky, yet Little Junior Brother has done them all.

Yun Zhi glanced at Ao Ling and the other two women fighting in the corner of the imperial city, quite surprised. She hadn’t expected Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi to be here, nor that the ancient Heavenly Court had gained another half-immortal.

“Big Senior Sister, I’ve been wronged! All those things were done by the Immortal Fairy while using my body!” Lu Yang hurriedly declared his innocence. For the sake of my future, when it is time to sell out the emperor for wealth and glory, one must sell out the emperor; I absolutely mustn’t be softhearted!

“Big Senior Sister, you know me. I’ve always kept a low profile; I don’t do such things. The Immortal Fairy used the acting sect leader’s authority and demanded my body. As a mere mortal, I was powerless to resist. Please judge this fairly, Big Senior Sister!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stiffened her neck. “What’s wrong with this immortal using the acting sect leader’s authority? Lass Yun promised me back then.”

“In that case, Senior Immortal Fairy, do you wish to continue as acting sect leader?” Yun Zhi remembered she had promised to let the Everlasting Immortal Fairy be acting sect leader for a year. There are still many months left.

“I’ve had enough fun. I’m not doing it anymore.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had enjoyed herself the past few days and currently had no desire to continue as acting sect leader.

Lu Yang promptly flattered her. “Since ancient times, those in power have all been greedy for authority, yet the Immortal Fairy remains unmoved by power, willing to step down at her peak to make way for successors. This is truly remarkable; it’s a blessing for the Dao-Seeking Sect and the entire world!”

Hearing her loyal minister’s heartfelt praise, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled incessantly.

“So the Xia Emperor’s lifespan really was borrowed by Senior Meng Junzi?”

“Correct. The Xia Emperor never had a problem with his lifespan from the start. Meng Junzi and Jiang Ping’an noticed long ago that Guan Shanhai coveted the national fortune and sought to restore Great Yu. However, Guan Shanhai acted cautiously and wouldn’t make a move recklessly.

“Having an immortal constantly eying the national fortune was a cumbersome matter. It required constant vigilance, wasting mental and physical effort. Therefore, the two of them jointly planned this incident.

“The national fortune resides in every emperor of Great Xia. When an emperor dies, the national fortune transfers to the next. Even if Guan Shanhai could lure Jiang Ping’an away, he wouldn’t dare attack the Xia Emperor. Since the Xia Emperor possessed the national fortune, he could hold out until Jiang Ping’an rushed back.

“Hence, the two of them first borrowed the Xia Emperor’s lifespan, making him act like his lifespan was about to be depleted. At the same time, they had the First Imperial Prince refuse to inherit the throne. This way, after the Xia Emperor’s ‘death,’ the national fortune would lose its fetters, prompting Guan Shanhai to act—just like what happened today.”

Lu Yang was pensive. “So that is to say that the First Imperial Prince’s previous behavior was all an act? He actually wanted to inherit the throne?”

“No. Only that part wasn’t an act.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“The original plan was for the Xia Emperor to feign death in a few more years. But your and Junior Brother Meng’s journey to the imperial city made me change my mind. I suggested they move the plan forward.”

Faced with Lu Yang’s puzzled gaze, Yun Zhi patiently explained. “I told them that, given your luck, with you in the imperial city, the probability of Guan Shanhai taking action would be higher.”

Lu Yang felt that Yun Zhi had a misunderstanding about him. Eliminating the Fourth Imperial Prince and the Fifth Imperial Prince and making Guan Shanhai believe the Xia Emperor’s condition truly was deteriorating—those were clearly the Immortal Fairy’s doing.

“But you could have told me in advance, Big Senior Sister, so that I could be mentally prepared.” Lu Yang looked at Yun Zhi with a begrudging expression. I’ve always been tight-lipped; even if I had known the truth about the Xia Emperor, I would have kept it a secret.

Yun Zhi sighed. “Little Junior Brother, you naturally wouldn’t leak the information. I was just worried that if you had known the truth, it might attract too many immortals, and the situation would be tricky to resolve.”

Lu Yang didn’t know what to say to that. “Then, Big Senior Sister, are you here to step in as well?”

Yun Zhi looked up at the two immortals battling fiercely in the sky. “Judging by the current situation, Meng Junzi alone will suffice.”

~~~

Not only did Meng Junzi and Guan Shanhai possess Dao Fruits, but they could also simultaneously use several Incipient Dao Fruits. The effects of an Incipient Dao Fruit wielded by a half-immortal compared to an immortal were worlds apart and utterly incomparable.

The two continuously shifted positions, each gaining the upper hand in turn.

With the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit and the Rejuvenation Incipient Dao Fruit, Guan Shanhai could rapidly recover from injuries.

In contrast, Meng Junzi seemed to lack healing methods. He was covered in wounds, with one particularly deep gash on his chest, exposing his bones.

Looking at the wounded Meng Junzi, Guan Shanhai sneered. “Junior, I thought you had some tricks up your sleeves. But it turns out that you’re nothing special. If I weren’t worried you’d steal my immortal artifacts, I would have already used them to kill you!”

Guan Shanhai could use the Dreamscape Incipient Dao Fruit to craft several immortal treasures in his dreams. After materializing them, he could then use the Replacement Incipient Dao Fruit to exchange those treasures for the immortal artifacts he desired.

However, judging by Meng Junzi’s combat style, anyone who fought him during his half-immortal days would have their magical treasures “borrowed” by him. That’s essentially aiding the enemy with supplies—utterly unacceptable.

Meng Junzi didn’t care about his injuries at all. He smiled nonchalantly and activated his Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit. “Fellow Daoist Guan, I see that you’re in good health, but you lack a certain embellishment and don’t look very aesthetically pleasing. How about I lend you all these injuries of mine?”

Guan Shanhai’s expression shifted. Before he could react, he felt as if his entire body was simultaneously attacked. A particularly deep gash appeared on his chest, exposing his bones.

In contrast, Meng Junzi was completely devoid of injuries. freewebnovel.com

Meng Junzi scrutinized the wounded Guan Shanhai with a satisfied smile.

“You look much more aesthetically pleasing now. Fellow Daoist Guan, shall we continue?”

“Meng Junzi!” Guan Shanhai roared, using two Incipient Dao Fruits to heal the injuries.

But these were wounds he had inflicted himself, dealt with immense force. Now that they had simultaneously appeared on him, he couldn’t heal them instantly, unless he possessed the Longevity Dao Fruit or the Rejuvenation Dao Fruit.

“Why are you shouting so loudly? It’ll be terrible if the injuries worsen.” Meng Junzi still smiled nonchalantly, activating his Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit again.

“I shall borrow strength from the past and the future.”

As the words left his mouth, two figures traversed time, arriving from the past and the future, standing shoulder to shoulder with Meng Junzi.

Chapter 876: Disparity in Experience

The two figures that arrived from the past and future were so blurry that their genders were indiscernible.

Witnessing Meng Junzi’s series of actions, the imperial city cultivators were all flabbergasted.

“He can even lend his own injuries to others?!”

“Doesn’t that mean that Meng Junzi can’t be injured at all? He’s inherently undefeatable!”

Some also excitedly pointed at the two blurry figures. “Look at those two figures! His past and future selves have come! Past, present, future—the trinity as one!”

“This is mind-blowing.”

Originally, the imperial city cultivators hoped to gain insights into the Dao by watching the immortal battle, enhancing their cultivation, and breaking through to higher cultivation realms.

But judging by the situation now, we’d better just watch the spectacle. It’d be a miracle if he could gain insights from this.

Lu Yang was also shocked by this scene. Meng Junzi’s Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit is unbeatable.

“Xiao Yangzi, what you’re thinking is too exaggerated. Those two figures aren’t the real Meng Junzi but portions of strength lent by his past and future selves.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had clashed with the Epoch Immortal multiple times. When it came to borrowing strength from the past and future, the Epoch Immortal was the true expert.

She continued, “These two figures combined are probably equal to another complete Meng Junzi. Moreover, since his past and future selves lent out portions of their strength, it would cause those two moments to be in a weakened state.”

“Similar to Tao Yaoye’s Metamorphic Immortal Physique?” Lu Yang felt that it was still exaggerated enough.

“More or less. Otherwise, why do you think such a physique can bear the name ‘immortal physique?’ It’s an immortal skill.

“As for him lending injuries to Guan Shanhai, it’s not that amazing. If this immortal isn’t mistaken, what is borrowed must be returned—and with interest. When returned, Meng Junzi’s injuries would be even worse.

“Lass Yun, did this immortal guess correctly?”

“You have discerning eyes, Senior Immortal Fairy.”

Lu Yang began to worry about Meng Junzi instead. “Doesn’t that mean the longer it drags on, the more disadvantageous it becomes for Senior Meng Junzi?”

Yun Zhi shook her head. “Meng Junzi won’t be injured.”

“Why’s that?”

“Guan Shanhai will heal the injuries. Once healed, there’ll be no issue of returning them.”

Lu Yang, “...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s intuition had always been accurate. Furthermore, she frequently engaged in combat during the ancient era, accumulating rich battle experience. Despite seeing it for the first time, she could identify the flaw in Meng Junzi’s technique at a glance.

But Guan Shanhai was different. Although the late Great Qian era was chaotic, with more than one half-immortal vying for supremacy, the number of half-immortals then couldn’t compare to the flourishing ancient era. His accumulated combat experience was utterly incomparable.

Unable to see through this move, Guan Shanhai had no choice but to help Meng Junzi treat his injuries.

~~~

In the skies above the imperial city, Guan Shanhai’s eyes twitched involuntarily as he watched Meng Junzi and his past and future selves fighting side by side.

I was too careless. This Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit is much more powerful than its incipient form. It’s on a completely different level.

It is a pity that I never found an immortal’s corpse. Otherwise, I could have used my Imprint Dao Fruit to imprint Wu Yao from the early days of Great Yu’s founding. The Wu Yao then wasn’t like he was later, obsessed with going to the external world; he would have chosen to help me.

Having to divide his attention between healing his wounds and dealing with the three Meng Junzis’ pincer attack, Guan Shanhai quickly fell into a disadvantage.

He inwardly cursed. If this continues, forget seizing the national fortune; even I’ll be stuck here.

Guan Shanhai instantly made a decision to cease engaging with Meng Junzi. I’ll flee right now!

“Great Heaven Creation Palm!”

Guan Shanhai unleashed an immortal technique toward Meng Junzi, and the latter countered with another.

Another massive explosion occurred above the imperial city, louder than thunder. Shockwaves radiated from the battle’s center, and Guan Shanhai seized the opportunity to escape.

To his surprise, the closer he got to the imperial city’s edge, the more he felt as if he were carrying an immortal mountain. His body grew heavier and heavier until he could no longer fly.

He tossed a magical treasure outside the imperial city, attempting to exchange positions with it, but that was also futile.

Meng Junzi seemed to have anticipated Guan Shanhai’s escape and followed the latter with a smile, also reaching the edge of the imperial city.

“Fellow Daoist Guan, since you’re already here, you should let me fulfil my duties as host. Stay here as my guest.”

“What move is this?!” Guan Shanhai was stunned, clueless as to when he had been affected.

A sliver of a cold smile tugged at Meng Junzi’s lips. “Do you think I waited until you refined part of the national fortune before acting? I was guarding against you running away mid-battle!

“Although you refined part of the national fortune, it’s merely a part of it. Before you completely refine the national fortune, it will remain a burden to you.

“The national fortune is the collective strength of Great Xia’s populace. To leave the imperial city, your strength must surpass that of all Great Xia’s citizens!

“Fellow Daoist Guan, do you think you possess such strength?”

Guan Shanhai’s expression changed drastically. He hadn’t expected the national fortune to become his shackle.

“Die!” Guan Shanhai’s face hardened with a deathly resolve, no longer showing the confident demeanor from before. Since I can’t escape, I’ll drag you down with me!

“Hundun Primal Chaos into Rainbow!”

A nine-colored rainbow appeared in Guan Shanhai’s palm, spanning the sky, imbued with the destructive intent of hundun primal chaos. It didn’t appear large, but if it struck the imperial city, the entire city would be reduced to nothingness.

I refuse to believe Meng Junzi would ignore the imperial city!

Meng Poci’s expression shifted dramatically. No matter how powerful the Imperial City Guard’s array is, it absolutely can’t withstand this strike of Guan Shanhai that is filled with hatred!

In such a situation, Yun Zhi would need to intervene. But now, Meng Junzi had a better idea.

“Fellow Daoist Jin Caiwei, may I borrow your Incipient Dao Fruit?”

Jin Caiwei was in the middle of combat when she heard Meng Junzi’s call. Although she was unsure what he planned to do, she still lent her Planary Incipient Dao Fruit to him.

Temporarily obtaining the Planary Incipient Dao Fruit, Meng Junzi transformed the descending nine-colored rainbow into a plane.

The planar nine-colored rainbow no longer resembled a rainbow but more like a nine-colored immortal blade. It fell upon the imperial city but didn’t explode.

Instead, it pierced through the array and sliced through the ground as if cutting tofu, drilling deep into the bottomless earth.

“Ridiculous! Let Guan see how many times you can block it!” You only neutralized one move. As long as he knew the imperial city was Meng Junzi’s weakness, Guan Shanhai wasn’t afraid to fight him.

But soon, he couldn’t laugh anymore. From the gash opened by the nine-colored rainbow, immortal light suddenly burst forth, surging straight toward Guan Shanhai’s face!

That immortal light was too fast. Before Guan Shanhai could react, it severed his right hand!

Guan Shanhai instantly realized where the attack had come from. The nine-colored light had penetrated to the very depths of the ground. And what lay at the bottom? It was the peerless immortal array constructed in ancient times to seal the world. Anyone attempting to attack the array would be struck back by it.

Seeing that he couldn’t destroy the imperial city, Guan Shanhai once again clashed with Meng Junzi in a bloody battle. He appeared utterly berserk, eyes bloodshot. No longer healing his wounds, he completely disregarded his injuries, determined to kill Meng Junzi in his final moments.

“Dissolution!” In the end, Guan Shanhai yelled and self-detonated.

The imperial city was also within the blast radius. Meng Junzi dared not use any technique to defuse this attack and had to endure it with gritted teeth, becoming severely injured from the explosion.

~~~

Watching from below all this time, Yun Zhi noticed something amiss. Guan Shanhai’s seemingly frenzied fighting was actually him cutting off his connection to the national fortune. Once the link was severed, he self-detonated to get away.

To have self-detonated to this extent, Guan Shanhai’s condition would only be worse than Meng Junzi’s.

“Little Junior Brother, I’ll be leaving for a while.”

Preventing Guan Shanhai from escaping was the ultimate reason she had come to the imperial city.

Chapter 877: The Battle of the Imperial City Concludes

“Damned Meng Junzi! Had I known this earlier, I should have killed you outright back then!”

Deep in the mountains and old forests, tens of thousands of li away from the imperial city, Guan Shanhai wore a ruthless expression. The battle at the imperial city had ended in utter defeat for him. His subordinates were left behind in the imperial city and Yù Province, and he had abandoned the national fortune he most desired with his own hands.

I have fought countless battles in my lifetime, yet I was outwitted by the schemes of two juniors!

At the thought of this, Guan Shanhai could no longer suppress his fury. He stomped violently, shattering the mountain beneath his feet, sending dust flying.

“Meng Junzi, Jiang Ping’an, just you wait, you two! If I don’t take revenge for this, I swear I’m not a human!”

Although his subordinates were gone, with his Imprint Dao Fruit, subordinates were the least of his worries. He could imprint General Yu, the Second Imperial Preceptor, and the others for his use, allowing him to make a comeback in an instant.

“Now I need to find a place to recuperate.”

The power of his self-detonation was immense. Coupled with the fact that he hadn’t tended to his injuries immediately and had burned immortal blood to flee here, injury piled upon injury. Even simultaneously deploying the Longevity Incipient Dao Fruit and the Rejuvenation Dao Fruit couldn’t facilitate a swift recovery.

“Why don’t you come to my Dao-Seeking Sect to treat your injuries, Senior Guan?”

A cold voice from behind startled Guan Shanhai, causing him to break out into a cold sweat.

“Who is it?!”

I was just momentarily distracted, and someone had approached me without me noticing!

He whirled around to see a cool and detached woman in a white dress standing behind him, watching him with a visage devoid of joy and sorrow.

“Yun Zhi of the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

Guan Shanhai remembered that Yun Zhi had defeated the leaders of four great immortal sects at the Five Great Immortal Sects Tournament. He deduced that she had either reached the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage or was a half-immortal.

Whichever it was, it wouldn't affect his plans in the imperial city, so he hadn't paid it much mind.

“What, you're just a mere immortal. Do you think you can defeat me to gain fame just because I'm severely injured? The juniors from later generations truly are arrogant!”

Yun Zhi didn't respond. She simply took a step forward.

Reflected in Guan Shanhai’s terrified and despairing pupils was a delicate palm. The palm grew closer and closer, utterly unavoidable.

~~~

“Is it finally over?”

Approximately ten minutes after Gain Shanhai escaped, the imperial city cultivators finally dared to ask themselves uncertainly, gulping nervously.

“Was the battle above the East Sea back then also of this level?”

“Immortal battles truly are terrifying.”

“Precisely! That move by the Great Yu Imperial Preceptor just now...what move was that again?”

“How exactly did Meng Junzi and the Great Yu Imperial Preceptor fight again? Who can remember?”

Although Meng Junzi’s Borrowing-Lending Dao Fruit lacked the immortal trait of oblivion, the Imprint Dao Fruit possessed it. This affected the entire immortal battle—no one remembered the specific combat techniques. Even the specially prepared recording orbs’ contents became blank and irrecoverable.

~~~

In a corner of the imperial city, the battle between five half-immortals also concluded.

General Yu went without saying; Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi were familiar with the Yin-Yang Incipient Dao Fruit’s combat style, making it easy for them to find countermeasures. The hardest to deal with was the Second Imperial Preceptor’s Karma Incipient Dao Fruit.

Fortunately, the three women eventually devised a solution. They ceased actively attacking the Second Imperial Preceptor. Jin Caiwei transformed the six surfaces of the surrounding space into planes, sealing off the area. Anyone attempting to breach these six planes would be attacked by the three women.

Afterward, she used the planes as blades to continuously slice the space until the Second Imperial Preceptor had nowhere to hide. With that, the outcome of the battle was determined.

The inspiration for this strategy came from Jiang Lianyi’s recollection of how her husband and the other three immortals sealed the entire cultivation world to find the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s murderer. It proved highly effective.

Hence, this world-shaking battle finally concluded.

~~~

“Old Mu, are you sure about establishing business in the imperial city? This place doesn’t seem very safe.” Creed Leader Chi stood dumbfounded.

The higher one’s cultivation was, the more one could comprehend how terrifying the earlier battle was. It represented combat at the pinnacle of the cultivation path, where every move carried the power to destroy heaven and earth. A single technique could obliterate the imperial city.

Who would have imagined a simple field assessment would lead us to a struggle for the throne, then to a half-immortal battle, and then an immortal battle?

“Look on the bright side. The imperial city has two immortals, Meng Junzi and Jiang Ping’an. Is there any place safer than the imperial city?”

“Now that you put it that way, it does seem so.”

~~~

“So you are Fellow Daoist Yun’s little junior brother?”

Meng Junzi, one of the main characters of the immortal battle, appeared before Lu Yang, scrutinizing him with keen interest.

“Senior Meng.” Lu Yang hadn’t expected Meng Junzi to seek him out right after the battle, and he was overwhelmed by the honor.

“Your cultivation foundation is incredibly solid. Even I was no better when I was at the Nascent Soul Stage. You’re a talented youth indeed.”

“Senior Meng, your injuries...” Lu Yang looked at Meng Junzi with slight concern, his eye twitching. The latter didn’t have a single intact spot on his body. These injuries look severe.

An immortal’s self-detonation unleashed unimaginable power, surpassing any immortal technique Guan Shanhai had used. For Meng Junzi to withstand it head-on and still stand here was quite remarkable.

Meng Junzi laughed heartily. “Hahaha, it’s merely an immortal’s self-detonation. What could it do to me?”

Upon hearing this, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy grew agitated. She jumped up from her throne and rolled up her sleeves, ready to go out and spar with Meng Junzi. “Looking down on an immortal’s self-detonation? Watch this immortal detonate for you!”

“Immortal Fairy, there’s no need to go so far. Senior Meng Junzi was just joking.”

Frightened, Lu Yang hastily stopped the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and ushered her back to the throne.

Unaware that he had narrowly escaped a calamity, Meng Junzi continued his bravado. “These are just minor injuries. They’ll heal after a few days of rest. If you don’t believe me, you can have Guan Shanhai self-detonate again.”

...Senior, please speak less.

After Ao Ling’s trio concluded their battle, they also sought out Lu Yang.

When they saw that Meng Junzi was also present, they were startled but still flew down. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, we have fulfilled our mission and captured these two.” In their hands were General Yu and the Second Imperial Preceptor.

Then they cupped their fists toward Meng Junzi. “Greetings, Senior Meng Junzi.”

Meng Junzi waved his hand. “Although I am an immortal, the three of you are figures from the ancient era. Discussing seniority gets too messy. Why not address each other as fellow Daoists?”

Meng Junzi had previously heard from Yun Zhi that Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi were on the same side as them. For some reason, she didn’t mention Jin Caiwei. Was there some concern?

“Fellow Daoist Jin, thank you for lending me your Incipient Dao Fruit earlier. To conceive such an exquisite Incipient Dao Fruit, you truly possess unparalleled talent.

“An Incipient Dao Fruit cannot be borrowed for free; this goes against my principles. Fellow Daoist Jin, I see that you are from the Qiongqi Tribe. How about I waive all debts between the Meng Family and the Qiongqi Tribe?”

Jin Caiwei’s eyes lit up. She had thought she was lending her Incipient Dao Fruit for free, never expecting such a pleasant surprise.

On this trip to the imperial city, I joined the ancient Heavenly Court, witnessed an immortal battle, captured two half-immortals alive, and finally resolved the debt problem that has plagued the Qiongqi Tribe for so many years—what immense gains!

Chapter 878: The Xia Emperor Revives

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, we shall take our leave then,” said Ao Ling’s trio.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi’s original purpose in coming to the imperial city was to have some fun. Since matters had concluded, there was no need for them to remain here. As for Jin Caiwei, she had accomplished her objective in coming to the imperial city, so she didn't need to stay either.

“As for these two, Great Yu’s Second Imperial Preceptor and General Yu...” Jin Caiwei held the Second Imperial Preceptor and General Yu, who had been compressed into planes, unsure what to do with them.

“Since they are the spoils of you three Fellow Daoists, they naturally belong to you to deal with.” Meng Junzi had no intention of claiming these two half-immortals for himself. I’ve always been a reasonable person.

Moreover, with Yun Zhi going after Guan Shanhai, the greatest prize is already secured. Minor details are no longer important.

“However, it’s best to search the Imperial Preceptor’s soul. Otherwise, if he seizes an opportunity to use his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, he could easily escape,” Meng Junzi kindly reminded them.

“Alright.” Even without Meng Junzi saying so, Ao Ling had planned to do just that.

“By the way, Senior Jin, since your Incipient Dao Fruit is considered a ‘spatial’ type, would you...have a conflict with Founding Ancestor Vast Sea?” Lu Yang asked tactfully. He feared that the two sides might clash during a contention for an immortal position in the future, and he wouldn’t know which side to help.

Jin Caiwei looked at the half-crouching Lu Yang and patted his stiff, tense shoulder, comforting him. “Don’t worry, there won’t be any conflict.”

She grinned, revealing two small tiger teeth. “After all, with this ability of mine, I can’t become an immortal anyway.”

Lu Yang, “...”

The little tiger added, “Furthermore, achieving immortality isn’t that easy. Fellow Daoist Vast Sea may not be qualified to become an immortal either. Your concern is unnecessary.”

“Alright, we should go. We’ll meet again when there’s a chance.”

Watching the three women’s receding figures, Meng Junzi couldn’t help but turn to look at Lu Yang with a sigh. “How on earth did you manage to become so familiar with those three?”

Initially, when Meng Junzi heard that Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi had joined the Heavenly Court, he assumed it was due to Yun Zhi’s persuasion.

But after interacting with those three women, it appears that Lu Yang had played a pivotal role.

It was his first time seeing a minor cultivator mingle so well with half-immortals, especially ancient ones.

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, Naturally, it’s because of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. But the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence was a secret, not to be told to anyone.

Meng Junzi didn’t have the habit of prying. Noticing Lu Yang’s silence, he didn’t dwell on it. “If you can’t say, then don’t. Everyone has secrets.

“Come, I’ll bring you into the imperial palace.”

~~~

“Just who is Lu Yang? Why do you both address him as Senior Brother Lu Yang?” This had perplexed Jin Caiwei all this time. At last, she couldn’t hold back and asked on the way.

Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi flashed a mysterious smile, refusing to tell the little tiger the reason.

Consider this a small revenge.

~~~

“So the Old Ancestor really became an immortal.”

The Meng Family had successfully sorted out the Second Imperial Prince’s faction and returned home to celebrate, drinking and making merry. None had expected the legendary half-immortal Old Ancestor to have become an immortal.

To prevent leaking information about Meng Junzi and arousing Guan Shanhai’s suspicion, only Jiang Ping’an and Yun Zhi were previously aware that he had become an immortal.

Yun Zhi found out only because she had gone to the imperial palace to test her skill level after her breakthrough. Jiang Ping’an didn’t want to lose alone and felt that he should drag Meng Junzi into it as well.

That was how Meng Junzi learned that Meng Junzi had also become an immortal.

As Meng Potian’s sworn brothers, the old horse and Steward Xu also joined the celebration, drinking mirthfully.

Thoroughly drunk, Meng Potian sought out his second and third brothers. He wrapped an arm around the old horse’s neck and poured wine into his mouth. “Old Horse, I think that kid Lu Yang is not bad. He has a sharp mind and exceptional talent. Although his luck is a bit poor, our Meng Family has an immortal presiding over things. Look how big this commotion was, yet the Old Ancestor still suppressed it.”

“I think his luck is just a minor issue.” The old horse glanced at his inebriated brother. What’s an immortal? You don’t know that kid resurrected an ancient immortal on his first mission outside the sect. When he went to the East Sea previously, he even encountered a battle between two immortals.

Though the old horse had no memory of the specifics of the immortal battle at the East Sea, his instincts told him that those two immortals were stronger than the two in the imperial city.

I’ll say it again: Big Brother, if you believe the Old Ancestor can protect Lu Yang, let the Old Ancestor pull the carriage in my stead.

The old horse had been industriously cultivating these past two years, not to reach the Transcendent Tribulation Stage to become Meng Jingzhou’s guardian, but to preserve his own life in future battles.

~~~

Lu Yang entered the imperial palace once again, this time openly and legitimately.

Initially, the Imperial Guard wanted to stop him, but upon seeing Meng Junzi, they could only obediently retreat. Although Meng Junzi’s entry to the imperial palace violated protocol, such matters weren’t something Fusion cultivators like them could manage.

Meng Junzi led Lu Yang to a repose palace. The Xia Emperor was emaciated and not breathing, his corpse lying on a bed crafted from ten-thousand-year ice. This was originally a method to slow lifespan depletion and could serve as a freezer to preserve the Xia Emperor’s body after death, killing two birds with one stone.

“Your Majesty—”

“Your Majesty, why did you leave so soon—”

The consorts knelt on the floor, weeping pitifully until they were gasping for breath. It was unclear how many were genuinely crying and how many were pretending.

Chief Eunuch Li also wept bitterly.

No imperial princes were present. The immortal battle had begun right after the Xia Emperor’s “death.” Who would dare come to the imperial palace at such a sensitive time? Only these consorts from the rear palace could make their way over.

“Alright, that’s enough, everyone out. This guy isn’t dead yet.” Meng Junzi pushed open the doors, employing immortal power to expel the consorts.

The consorts were sobbing when they somehow found themselves outside. Recalling Meng Junzi’s words, they were utterly baffled.

He’s in that state and still not dead?

Meng Junzi activated his Dao Fruit. A string of obscure runes emerged from his body and flowed into the Xia Emperor’s. This was the lifespan he had previously borrowed. When returning the lifespan, Meng Junzi gave the Xia Emperor a few extra years as interest.

Under Lu Yang’s gaze, the Xia Emperor’s shriveled form inflated like a balloon, visibly plumping up. Wrinkles on his face were smoothed away by his lifespan, restoring him to his middle-aged appearance—what he should have looked like.

The Xia Emperor opened his eyes to see Meng Junzi and Lu Yang, exhaling a long, turbid breath. It seems the matter is over; there is no need to act anymore.

After the Xia Emperor revived, the national fortune in Meng Junzi’s hand also flowed into him, signifying that the Xia Emperor had once again become the monarch of the nation.

“Junior of the Jiang Family pays respects to Senior Meng Junzi.”

“Alright, that’s enough. You’ve just recovered your lifespan and need to convalesce. Don’t move.”

“Yes, Senior. May I ask if the battle has concluded?”

Meng Junzi smiled confidently. “A mere Great Yu Imperial Preceptor was naturally no match for me.”

“Then where is the Great Yu Imperial Preceptor?”

Meng Junzi’s smile froze.

Chapter 879: A Blatant Disregard for the Imperial Favor and a Transgression Nothing Short of Rebellious

Meng Junzi found the Xia Emperor an eyesore no matter how he looked at him. This brat didn’t say a word when he was “dead,” so why is he so talkative after coming back to life?

Before Meng Junzi could say anything, they heard a bang as the door was pushed open.

A young man carrying a hoe over his shoulder walked in, his bearing imposing and dignified. Tied to the other end of the hoe was a person, dangling and swaying.

“Haha, the matter in Yù Province is settled. Junzi, how’s it going on your end?”

Meng Junzi glared at the young man carrying a hoe. Did you two grandfather and grandson collude? Taking turns questioning me.

“Get lost. Boasting about defeating a half-immortal, what’s the big deal?”

Seeing Meng Junzi’s mangled flesh after the immortal’s self-detonation, the hoe-carrying young man was amused and hurriedly stepped forward to show his concern. “Aiya, Junzi, what happened to you? I remember you bragging that dealing with a mere Great Yu Imperial Preceptor would be a walk in the park for you.”

Meng Junzi waved his hand dismissively. “Heh, it just looks serious. Actually, they’re all minor injuries, not painful at all. Old Jiang, you’re too easily fooled.”

The young man carrying a hoe poked Meng Junzi’s wound. “Not painful?”

An immortal’s self-detonation could damage even an immortal’s soul. That poke hurt so much that Meng Junzi almost cried out.

But he couldn’t lose face in front of Jiang Ping’an. He swallowed back the “ow,” his face contorted. “Not painful.”

The young man carrying the hoe poked harder. The pain made Meng Junzi grimace, and he kicked Jiang Ping’an.

Jiang Ping’an was sent tumbling by the kick, but he walked back as if nothing had happened.

“You said it wasn’t painful.”

The two immortals glared at each other.

Lu Yang crouched down and examined the person’s face. He hadn’t seen his portrait before and didn’t know which Great Yu half-immortal this was. This half-immortal had no vitality left. Lu Yang guessed that Jiang Ping’an hadn’t held back and searched his soul to obtain information immediately upon reaching Yù Province.

The young man carrying the hoe finally noticed Lu Yang’s presence. “You must be Yun Zhi’s auspicious...little junior brother, Lu Yang.”

“This junior pays respects to Senior Jiang Ping’an.”

The young man carrying the hoe was naturally Jiang Ping’an.

Jiang Ping’an sized up Lu Yang. Should I say that he’s truly the little junior brother personally trained by Yun Zhi? His foundation is absurdly solid. Even with my discerning eyes, I can’t find a single flaw.

“What a handsome and promising young man. Do you have any interest in marrying into our Jiang Family?

“Our Jiang Family has seven young imperial princesses, all stunningly beautiful, especially the seventh. She’s very pretty and about your age and cultivation level. Coincidentally, she has heard stories about you for years and likes you!”

Jiang Ping’an was referring to the Xia Emperor’s seventh daughter, the youngest imperial princess of the Jiang Family.

Meng Junzi extended his arm to block Jiang Ping’an. “Hey, hey, hey, don’t poach. Our Meng Family already has an arrangement with him; he’s going to marry into our Meng Family in the future.

Jiang Ping’an and Meng Junzi’s eyes lit up upon seeing Lu Yang.

This is Lu Yang, whom Yun Zhi assessed as having the makings of an immortal. Yun Zhi’s evaluation isn’t the kind of empty flattery the outside world uses for prodigies. It means Lu Yang has a high likelihood of becoming an immortal in the future.

Isn’t now the time to win him over then?

Lu Yang felt immense pressure from being held in high regard by two immortals, uncertain how to respond.

The door was gently pushed open. It was none other than Yun Zhi, who had left not long ago. She dragged Guan Shanhai, who had also left not long ago.

“I’ve brought him back.

“Two fellow Daoists, what are you doing, sandwiching my Little Junior Brother between you?”

“Hahaha, nothing, nothing. We just thought this kid looks quite sturdy.”

Guan Shanhai’s left cheek was swollen to a bluish hue, and his left eye was bloodshot. Based on Lu Yang’s experience, he guessed it was caused by external impact, leading to a subconjunctival hemorrhage. Guan Shanhai also had his six senses sealed by Yun Zhi and couldn’t perceive his surroundings.

The small room had become a gathering of heroes, each with extraordinary backgrounds—the undefeated Yun Zhi; the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, head of the Five Ancient Immortals; Meng Junzi, who nearly became the founding emperor; Jiang Ping’an, who founded Great Xia; Guan Shanhai, who had sustained Great Yu for a hundred thousand years; the Xia Emperor, who was hailed as an emperor for the ages; and Lu Yang.

“What should we do with Guan Shanhai?” Jiang Ping’an asked. Should we search his soul directly or imprison him and slowly torture him to extract information from him?

“Confine him in our sect’s Incarceration Peak. It’ll be a reunion for the Great Yu bunch.”

Jiang Ping’an and Meng Junzi balked at the idea. We’ve worked hard ourselves to the bone; it’s fine if we can’t get the meat, but not getting a sip of the soup is unacceptable.

Although they were somewhat afraid of Yun Zhi, they still plucked up their courage. “That’s not appropriate, isn’t it? Your Incarceration Peak has no immortal; how can it contain him? If you ask me, I’d say he should be confined in our imperial city. With the two of us keeping watch, it’ll be absolutely foolproof!”

“With me here, our Incarceration Peak can contain him,” Yun Zhi stated insipidly, exuding confidence.

In truth, none of them really wanted to search Guan Shanhai’s soul directly, for it would destroy his immortal soul.

That was an immortal soul. No one had ever used an immortal soul and an immortal body to forge artifacts. What kind of power would an immortal artifact with an artifact spirit crafted from these two materials possess?

An unprecedented peak immortal artifact!

Even the Heaven Mandate Immortal didn’t enjoy such treatment when forging immortal artifacts. At most, he broke off a branch from the Epoch Immortal as a material—that was how the Heaven-Splitting Axe’s handle came about.

Yun Zhi wasn’t trying to hog it all. After all, Jiang Ping’an and Meng Junzi had contributed tremendous effort in capturing Guan Shanhai, whereas she had only done the finishing work. In all fairness, they deserved a share.

But she couldn’t give them all of Guan Shanhai either.

Just as the three were deadlocked, Lu Yang slowly raised his hand and spoke. “Umm, I have an idea. Since there’s only Guan Shanhai, which makes it hard to split, why not directly divide his soul?”

Three ethereal souls and seven corporeal souls—ten portions in total—enough for the three of them. freewebnovel.com

The three thought it over; it was indeed a good solution.

Given Guan Shanhai’s personality, he wouldn’t divulge information easily. Separating his souls would weaken his willpower, making it possible to extract information from him through threats, cajoling, or torture.

“What a great idea.”

Meng Junzi and Jiang Ping’an found Lu Yang more and more agreeable. Not only is his talent top-tier, but his character is also impeccable.

After some discussion, it was decided that Jiang Ping’an and Meng Junzi would take the seven corporeal souls and the immortal body, while Yun Zhi would take the three ethereal souls, the Dao Fruit, and Lu Yang.

“By the way, that kid Meng Jingzhou won’t be returning for now,” Meng Junzi called out. He was resolved to instruct this outstanding junior properly. Among all his descendants, only Meng Jingzhou’s talent came closest to his own. With proper guidance, Meng Jingzhou might even surpass him in the future.

Previously, he couldn’t reveal his identity and cultivation, preventing him from teaching Meng Jingzhou. Now there was nothing to fear.

Lu Yang felt that Meng Jingzhou was really lucky. He has an immortal ancestor teaching him. In contrast, I...seem to have an immortal teaching me too.

Strange, why haven’t I felt it?

Man Gu would remain in the imperial city for the time being. It was his first visit, and in less than two hours after his arrival, he had encountered an immortal battle. Now that it was over, he should stay in the imperial city for a while.

At worst, I can find an excuse in the future to acquire more immortal peaches for Little Junior Brother to eat his fill.

Chapter 880: I Can’t Really Can’t Handle Incarceration Peak Anymore

The immortal peach was plump and juicy, living up to its reputation as a product of the World Natural Spiritual Root. As Lu Yang took a bite, the peach juice exploded in his mouth, sweet yet not cloying. It felt as if every droplet danced on his tongue, awakening all his taste buds. With each chew, the peach’s fragrance filled his mouth and lingered on his lips, its sweetness utterly intoxicating.

This was definitely the most delicious peach Lu Yang had ever eaten.

Apart from extending lifespan, this immortal peach could also expel impurities and purify spirit roots. However, Lu Yang’s body had long been tempered multiple times and cleansed of impurities, and his Sword Spirit Root had no room for improvement. He was simply enjoying his half of the peach.

Compared to Lu Yang, Yun Zhi ate with more elegance. After savoring her half of the immortal peach, she carefully stored the pit, intending to plant it upon return.

Under the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s resentful gaze, Yun Zhi and Lu Yang smoothly returned to the sect.

In recent years, since Lu Yang joined the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Incarceration Peak had become increasingly lively. If one wanted to reflect on the past, reminisce about history, and build a Great Yu history museum, Incarceration Peak was undoubtedly the best choice. At Incarceration Peak, one could meet cultivators from the mid to late Great Yu era. They would personally recount tales of that distant era.

And today, the most pivotal figure of Great Yu arrived at Incarceration Peak, filling in the missing piece of the early Great era.

~~~

Inside Incarceration Peak, under dim oil lamps, the childlike Grand-Shifu Tang Shengyi hovered in the air. Around him lay one depleted spirit stone after another, along with many medicinal dregs.

After the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s attack on the Dao-Seeking Sect the last time, the Grand-Shifu faintly sensed an enormous future crisis and cultivated even more diligently in preparation to face it.

Cultivation began with cultivating the heart. Previously, while guarding Incarceration Peak, he had focused on comprehending the heart. Through conversations with prisoners, exchanging cultivation insights, and listening to their past stories and goals of cultivation, his mental state had become increasingly polished and clear.

And now, he formally began cultivating.

After one’s temperament was refined, cultivation progress could increase dramatically. This was something many high-level cultivators were unaware of.

To become strong as quickly as possible, the Grand-Shifu exchanged contribution points and his pension for vast quantities of spirit stones, precious medicines, and spirit pills. All these had now become part of his power.

“It’s a pity. Although there’s nothing wrong with my cultivation, I still have no clue about forming an Incipient Dao Fruit.”

It wasn’t necessary for one to reach the Apex Transcendent Tribulation Stage to start condensing an Incipient Dao Fruit. One could condense it as long as they reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. After the formation of the Incipient Dao Fruit, one could still cultivate, improving one's cultivation progress at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. The two didn’t conflict. It was just that few managed to condense an Incipient Dao Fruit upon reaching the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and become half-immortals.

The Grand-Shifu had always longed to condense an Incipient Dao Fruit. Unfortunately, he hadn’t made progress in that regard.

What storms have I not weathered? I had safely navigated the chaotic era of the Dao-Seeking Nine. Which of those nine little rascals haven’t been disciplined by me?

Separated from his seven corporeal souls, the prisoner was listless, his head drooping.

“Who is this?” the Grand-Shifu exclaimed softly. He couldn’t help but feel that the figure looked familiar, as if he had seen a full-body portrait of him in some history book.

He walked over and tilted his head upward. Right then, the prisoner abruptly lifted his head, locking eyes with the Grand-Shifu.

Startled, the Grand-Shifu hastily retreated with several loud steps. He gasped for breath, his heart still racing.

He wasn’t frightened by the prisoner’s sudden movement but by the prisoner’s appearance!

The Grand-Shifu’s hand trembled as he pointed at the prisoner’s soul, his voice quivering. “G-Great Yu Imperial Preceptor Guan Shanhai?!”

This is a bona fide immortal!

Detaining half-immortals on Incarceration Peak is one thing—after all, they only have one extra Incipient Dao Fruit compared to me. But immortals are different; they’re at a realm completely beyond the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. How many immortals have there been throughout history?

I’m merely a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator; how could I keep watch over an immortal?

“Imperial Preceptor?!” The Myriad Spells Daoist Lord’s eyes nearly popped out—assuming a soul could have eyeballs. I never imagined that the peerless Imperial Preceptor would also fall into the Dao-Seeking Sect’s hands.

“Guan Shanhai, this day has also come for you!” The Nightmare Supreme Lord gloated upon seeing his former rival become a fellow inmate, almost dancing with joy.

The Black-White Venerable Lord, Azure Lightning Venerable Lord, and other Great Yu cultivators all stared in disbelief.

Wu Youdao looked utterly crestfallen. Originally, he had thought that even if he had been reduced to a prisoner, as long as the Imperial Preceptor remained out there, he would eventually see the light of day.

Now, that hope is shattered. Great Yu is completely wiped out, imprisoned within Incarceration Peak.

Instantly, all order on Incarceration Peak fell apart, and pandemonium erupted. Everyone, regardless of their status, was astonished by the new prisoner’s identity.

“Grand-Shifu, don’t be afraid. Guan Shanhai only has his three ethereal souls left. His power is greatly diminished, and he’s been sealed by me. He absolutely won’t cause trouble and escape.”

The Grand-Shifu shook his head like a rattle-drum, firmly refusing. I really haven’t weathered a storm like this before.

He hurriedly took out a spatial talisman from his robes and tore it. This was a talisman left by the Vast Sea Daoist Lord. He had said that if anything happened, he could use it to contact him, and the Vast Sea Daoist Lord would come in person.

After tearing the talisman, a spatial gate opened. A figure slowly emerged, looking around.

The Grand-Shifu immediately rushed forward to seek help. “Founding Ancestor, I can’t handle Incarceration Peak anymore. Locking up a few Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and even a few half-immortals here was still fine, but now, an immortal has arrived. This is beyond my capabilities!

“Why don’t you take over guarding Incarceration Peak, Founding Ancestor?!”

The Innate Daoist Priest looked down at the Grand-Shifu clutching his leg, then looked up to scan the prisoners around Incarceration Peak.

Wouldn’t that be a bit too much for someone at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage like me?

Chapter 881: Zhu Tian: Why Are There More and More Immortals?

The Grand-Shifu rolled his eyes, not buying the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s nonsense. I had come to Incarceration Peak for an easy life. Who would have imagined that being the Incarceration Peak’s warden would be more exhausting than being the sect leader?

Chapter 882: Going All Out

Since Jin Caiwei had joined the Heavenly Court, holding the title of Northern Great Emperor of Wealth, and had been freed from debts, she felt that with one good thing happening after another, it should be a time of prosperous fortune and limitless possibilities.

With a small wave of her hand, she adopted Chieftain Jin’s proposal. “Alright, we shall buy candles then. It’s about time our Qiongqi Tribe made money!”
