Meanwhile, Lu Yang was still unaware that both the Qiongqi Tribe and the Radiant Sun Creed had coincidentally set their sights on the candle market.

He had been in seclusion in his cave abode for seven days, conserving energy and strength, and adjusting his state. Essence, qi, and spirit unified and were elevated to their peak, while he kept a spirit pill in his mouth to restore his mental power.

Slowly opening his baleful eyes, he was greeted by the sight of a peerlessly beautiful young woman. She blinked with her large, watery eyes, tilting her head as she looked at him.

“Immortal Fairy, please move aside.” In the mental space, Lu Yang helplessly nudged the Everlasting Immortal Fairy away.

“Oh.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy obediently moved aside, revealing the opponent of this battle—the Unbeatable Nascent Soul. freewebnovel.com

Lu Yang had endured countless hardships at the Nascent Soul Stage, all for the sake of defeating his own nascent soul!

Just as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had said, one mustn’t take shortcuts in cultivation. Only by taking one step at a time could one become the strongest.

Throughout his Nascent Soul Stage, aside from various incidents like encountering the Nightmare Supreme Lord and the Void Emptiness Supreme Lord, finding the Innate Daoist Priest, drawing the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord into attacking the sect, the journey to the East Sea, and the trip to the imperial city...Lu Yang had devoted all his time to honing his skills!

After seven days of accumulating his strength, his condition had peaked. Even if a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator appeared before him now, he could slay them with a casual swing of the sword.

“Come fight!” Lu Yang shouted, using his mental power to materialize the Qingfeng Sword, Mingyue Sword, and the Seven Stars Sword Set.

At the same time, nine sharp swords gleamed and hovered around the Unbeatable Nascent Soul. Whatever Lu Yang could do, it could too.

“Xiao Yangzi, jiayou! Show it what you’re made of!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clenched her fists, cheering for Lu Yang on the sidelines.

In contrast, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s side was empty, with no one supporting it.

In terms of morale, Lu Yang had already won.

“Sword Like Dragon!” Wielding the Qingfeng Sword, Lu Yang unleashed a dragon’s roar that resonated throughout the mental space. A black dragon condensed from sword qi surged forth, claws bared, sweeping through everything.

This was the True Dragon Sword Qi that Lu Yang had emulated from Ao Ling.

The True Dragon Sword Qi was further imbued with the Three Flavor True Fire and Golden Bird True Flame.

The sword qi took the form of a true dragon with meticulous details; even among Divine Transfiguration cultivators from Sword Tower, few could achieve this.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul yelled and released its own black dragon from the Qingfeng Sword.

The two True Dragon Sword Qi clashed ferociously. Had a Divine Transfiguration cultivator stood between them, they would have been shredded to pieces.

This was a genuine sword technique that killed. Lu Yang seldom employed it. But since he was facing the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, there was no need to hold back.

He had sparred with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul countless times in the imperial city. He knew that if he didn’t unleash killing moves and waited for the Unbeatable Nascent Soul to do so, he would lose.

Next, a golden phoenix and a bone-winged white tiger flew out in succession.

Sword qi transformed into a dragon, phoenix, and a tiger—three of the Heavenly Court’s Four Regents. This represented the pinnacle of Lu Yang’s Sword Dao comprehension at the Nascent Soul Stage.

“One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords, Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array!”

Nine sharp swords suspended at the top of the mental space transformed into tens of thousands of swords that burst forth with dazzling radiance.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul plunged its nine swords into the ground. The earth seemed to come alive as countless swords broke through the soil, their number matching those above!

Swords descended from the sky like a torrential downpour, while swords sprang from the ground like bamboo shoots after a rain, producing incessant ringing from the clashes between sword qi.

Affected by the Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array, both Lu Yang and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul knelt opposite each other, unable to move.

But that didn’t stop them from attacking!

“Town in Palm!” Lu Yang rapidly formed hand seals. A hand the size of a town emerged from the ground, grasping Lu Yang and smashing him fiercely toward the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

The barrage of swords from the sky and ground fell upon the clenched giant hand, but were all deflected.

Lu Yang could already perform this move at the Golden Core Stage, though back then, the hand wasn’t as large due to his limited cultivation. Now that he was at the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage, the move had correspondingly grown from the size of a village to that of a town, and its power was equally terrifying, no weaker than the sword qi transforming into the Four Regents!

Faced with the descending colossal fist, a sixteen-foot-tall golden Buddha statue suddenly appeared, blocking the fist’s path. This was the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s strongest defensive skill, but before the Town in Palm, it still seemed insufficient.

The golden Buddha shattered, leaving the Unbeatable Nascent Soul exposed beneath the fist.

Earlier, Lu Yang had struck first, reacting even faster than the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, unleashing Town in Palm. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul then used the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body to buy time.

As the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body shattered, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul also completed hand seals, executing Town in Palm.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s Town in Palm required a longer charging time, making it more powerful than Lu Yang’s. If the two moves collided, Lu Yang would definitely lose.

But right then, the fist of Lu Yang’s Town in Palm changed. Its force became extremely regular and carried the Vast Righteous Qi; it was no longer a simple fist smash.

Caught in the midst, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul couldn’t see the whole picture. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy who stood outside the arena saw the principle behind this move and applauded in delight.

“Xiao Yangzi, what a great idea! Combining Town in Palm with Arhat Fist multiplies the power severalfold!”

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul froze, as if it was unsure how to respond.

Logically, after Lu Yang consecutively performed so many moves, his remaining mental power shouldn’t be enough to support executing these two moves simultaneously. It wouldn’t work even if Lu Yang had a pill slowly restoring his mental power because Lu Yang and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul would recover their mental power at the same rate under these conditions.

The two palms collided. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul struggled briefly with its Town in Palm but was ultimately no match for Lu Yang. Its giant hand shattered and vanished.

As Lu Yang’s Town in Palm had successively broken the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s Sixteen-Foot Golden Body and Town in Palm, it became transparent. Only then could the Unbeatable Nascent Soul see what Lu Yang was doing while held within the giant hand.

Lu Yang’s movements were no different from usual, but the Unbeatable Nascent Soul instantly saw through his actions—Lu Yang was performing the Lu Yang Animal Form Fist! This way, he could recover mental power even faster by leveraging his physical body!

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s techniques were indeed exquisite and marvelous, each executed perfectly. The transitions between moves were extremely smooth, leaving no openings.

But when it came to combining and layering techniques, its imagination still fell short of Lu Yang’s. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul simply couldn’t conceive of such a fighting method!

With the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s moves neutralized and Lu Yang possessing more mental power, the stark contrast left the Unbeatable Nascent Soul at a disadvantage.

The giant hand opened. Lu Yang leaped out from the Town in Palm and punched the Unbeatable Nascent Soul squarely in the face. The force was so great that it sent the Unbeatable Nascent Soul flying backward.

“Way to go, Xiao Yangzi!”

Chapter 883: Defeating the Unbeatable Nascent Soul

“Damn it, fighting yourself is really tough. Fortunately, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul isn’t too bright.” After that series of explosive moves, Lu Yang was almost unable to hold on.

To be precise, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul didn’t have a brain; it was Lu Yang’s theoretical peak state.

However, this was limited to techniques. Although it was highly adaptable, it still fell short of Lu Yang’s.

This was a method Lu Yang had devised mid-battle. No matter how adaptable the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was, it couldn’t match Lu Yang’s flexibility and ingenuity. The clearest evidence was the Unbeatable Nascent Soul freezing for a moment at this sight, unable to react.

Moreover, the theoretical peak state didn’t completely translate to reality. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul could only use the power it possessed. But Lu Yang was different; he could borrow power from his physical body!

Less capable in adaptability and borrowing power—these were the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s two major weaknesses.

If he still couldn’t defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul with this strategy, Lu Yang figured he might as well use the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Animal Form Fist to trounce it. After all, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wouldn’t lend her power to the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, so it couldn’t use the Everlasting Immortal Fairy Animal Form Fist.

Fall behind once, and you fall behind at every step. After suffering that punch from Lu Yang, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul lost the initiative again. It also wanted to perform the Lu Yang Animal Form Fist to restore its mental power quickly, but Lu Yang didn’t give it the chance to do so.

Employing Sword Dao and spells in tandem, Lu Yang drove the Unbeatable Nascent Soul back repeatedly, its aura dwindling.

Boom!

Once again, Lu Yang sent the Unbeatable Nascent Soul flying, and it crashed through a pillar in the great hall.

Lu Yang pressed his advantage. Unexpectedly, as if foreseeing its defeat, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul took a step forward and vanished into thin air!

Lu Yang’s pupils constricted. He instantly figured out what technique the Unbeatable Nascent Soul had executed.

“Close Horizon From Cliff?!”

This was the first spatial divine ability Lu Yang had learned, capable of randomly transporting him to some cliff. However, due to its extreme unpredictability and the fact that Lu Yang had other ways to handle danger, he avoided using it where possible. Since learning this move, it had been left to gather dust.

Who would have thought? The Unbeatable Nascent Soul used this spell to flee first before I thought of using it.

Previously, when the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was subdued by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, it hadn’t employed this technique because the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was too powerful, leaving it no time to do so.

But Lu Yang and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul were closely matched, easily giving the Unbeatable Nascent Soul an opportunity to escape during battle.

“Don’t think you can escape like this! Close Horizon From Cliff!”

Although the locations of the cliffs were random, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was ultimately a part of Lu Yang. Wherever the Unbeatable Nascent Soul went, Lu Yang would go too.

Lu Yang’s true form took a step forward and also disappeared from the mental space. Since the Unbeatable Nascent Soul had run from his body, there was no longer a need to fight it in his soul form.

~~~

“Hmm? Where is this?” After taking one step forward, Lu Yang found himself surrounded by utter darkness. Looking up, he saw only a sliver of sky.

He stood on a stone platform jutting out from the side of a sheer cliff. Beside the platform was a cave.

Lu Yang’s intuition told him that the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was hiding deep within this cave.

Using the Three Flavor True Fire to illuminate the cave, he saw that its interior was covered in spider webs, and countless bats hung from the ceiling. Startled by the true fire, all the bats flew out in a rush, like a dark cloud.

A stone stele was erected deep inside the cave.

Lu Yang examined the stele. The general meaning of the inscription was that its author was a mighty cultivation expert who had gone into seclusion here to break through to a higher realm. Unfortunately, he failed, perishing with his Dao extinguished. Before his demise, he left a trial. Whoever passed it would become his successor, inheriting all his legacy.

Lu Yang recited the last line word by word. “My successor, if you have obtained my legacy, it signifies that you possess wisdom, courage, and a Dao Heart. I believe you will surely fulfil your shifu’s lifelong wish in the future—to become a Nascent Soul cultivator...”

The stele’s owner was only at the Golden Core Stage. No arrangement he left behind could escape Lu Yang’s spiritual consciousness. With a brief scan, he saw the legacy hidden beneath the stele: a cultivation manual, a storage ring of unknown contents, and a bag of spirit stones.

“It’s actually an incomplete cultivation manual.” Lu Yang was surprised, quickly browsing the manual with his spiritual consciousness.

This is truly a remarkable fortuitous opportunity! If completed, this cultivation manual can lead to the Divine Transfiguration Stage! Furthermore, even if this is completed, it is only the first half of the cultivation manual. Combining both halves of the cultivation manual could support one up to the Fusion Stage!

Lu Yang soon tossed the matter of the legacy to the back of his mind. When he extended his spiritual consciousness, he successfully found the Unbeatable Nascent Soul hiding behind the stele.

Realizing it had been discovered by Lu Yang, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul transformed into a streak of lightning and dashed out of the cave.

“Don’t run!”

Lu Yang was hot on its heels. Man and infant hugged the cliff, rushing straight toward the slit of sky.

Just as Lu Yang was about to catch up with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, he heard an “Ah—” from above the cliff edge. A herb gatherer with a basket on his back had accidentally fallen.

Lu Yang gave up on chasing the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and went to catch the herb gatherer.

“That was close. You’re lucky to meet me. If you had fallen like that, the branches growing on the cliff might not have caught you.”

After bidding farewell to the bewildered herb gatherer, Lu Yang resumed pursuing the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul continuously executed Close Horizon From Cliff to flee, and Lu Yang employed the same move in pursuit. They fought in different cliff crevices, occasionally encountering hidden blood pools capable of awakening bloodlines, masterless growth-type magical treasures, and elders reduced to souls at the bottom of cliffs...

And just when Lu Yang was about to catch up to the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, he would keep encountering someone falling from the cliffs—a dragon-human, a young cultivator, and a young heir despised by his clan...

Lu Yang could only rescue them first, then continue the chase.

Fortunately, no one fell from the same cliff consecutively. After five cliffs, he finally caught up to the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

“Still trying to run?!”

Without the support of pills, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s energy was long depleted. In contrast, Lu Yang had continuously consumed pills and was in high spirits.

A gigantic hand crashed down as if the sky was collapsing. Unfazed, Lu Yang decisively swung his sword. Sword qi transformed into a dragon and soared through the sky, shattering the formidable yet weak palm and pinning the Unbeatable Nascent Soul onto the cliff face.

“You lost.” With an impassive visage, Lu Yang floated before the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and pointed the Qingfeng Sword at it, its tip gleaming intimidatingly.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul lowered its head in defeat and obediently flew back into the mental space.

“Strange, why do I still feel like I can’t control the Unbeatable Nascent Soul?”

Although he had defeated the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, and it had become docile, Lu Yang couldn’t help but feel that something was amiss, as though the Unbeatable Nascent Soul wasn’t entirely obedient and under his command.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered briefly. This wasn’t something she had encountered before. It shouldn’t be the case though.

“Oh, this immortal gets it! This immortal defeated the Unbeatable Nascent Soul first; you defeated it later. To fully control it, you still need to defeat this immortal!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, you’re doing this on purpose, right?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled as she leaned close to Lu Yang’s livid face, offering an apologetic smile. “Aiya, Xiao Yangzi, don’t be angry. How about you hit this immortal once?”

Lu Yang eyed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suspiciously and gave her a light push.

Staggering back two steps, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy weakly collapsed onto the bed, covering her face as she drawled, “Aiya—this immortal has lost.”

On this day, Lu Yang defeated the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, achieving a feat unprecedented in history.

Chapter 884: Practice

After defeating the Unbeatable Nascent Soul and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang felt a close connection between himself and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, far surpassing what existed before.

“Finally settled.”

Lu Yang crouched at the bottom of some unknown cliff valley, eagerly sensing the changes brought by this victory.

“Come out.”

Lu Yang attempted to control the Unbeatable Nascent Soul. It obediently flew out from the mental space and no longer attacked him.

“Go, move that rock over here.”

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul flew over, effortlessly lifted the thousand-jin boulder, and carried it to Lu Yang.

“Put it back.”

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul obediently returned the boulder to its original place.

Lu Yang couldn’t help but shed emotional tears. Other cultivators could control their nascent souls right upon reaching the Nascent Soul Stage. On the other hand, he was almost about to undergo tribulation to advance to the Divine Transfiguration Stage before he could control his. It’s been so hard.

Defeating the Unbeatable Nascent Soul wasn’t easy, but the rewards afterward were equally remarkable. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul was essentially another version of himself, capable of doubling all his attacks.

However, his moves were too powerful. The space at the bottom of the valley was too constrained to unleash them.

“Let’s go back to the sect to find someone to spar with.”

Leaving the valley, Lu Yang searched for the nearest city, only to discover that through the successive spatial jumps, he had already leaped to a neighboring province.

Eager to test the Unbeatable Nascent Soul’s power, he swiftly rode the Sword-Cleansing Pond back to the Dao-Seeking Sect, planning to seek out Li Haoran at Hundred Refinements Peak.

Old Meng and Man Gu are in the imperial city. If Tao Yaoye uses her Metamorphic Immortal Physique, I can’t win either. Among my peers, the only one left who can be my opponent is Li Haoran.

~~~

“Junior Brother Li, are you free? Let’s spar, uh...you are Junior Brother Li, right?” Lu Yang looked at the armored figure before him, not entirely certain.

“It’s me.” A muffled voice came from within the armor.

Li Haoran was clad in fine metal armor that covered him completely, not even sparing his eyes. He removed his helmet and repeated, “It’s me.”

“Junior Brother Li, what’s with this?”

Li Haoran smiled and patted the armor. “A newly refined magical treasure. I’ve named it Battle Armor. When worn, it offers both offense and defense. Even Divine Transfiguration cultivators would find it hard to penetrate it.”

During the battle with the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, the Dao-Seeking Sect had employed a peerless magical treasure—Founding Ancestor Primordial’s armor, which could elevate a Fusion cultivator to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Inspired by this, Li Haoran spent over a year forging his own suit of armor.

Although it couldn’t allow cross-stage combat like the Primordial Heavenly Sovereign’s armor, it genuinely raised the ceiling of Li Haoran’s combat power.

“Perfect timing. I’ve recently made some gains in cultivation. Why don’t we spar?” Lu Yang smiled. This is truly coincidental.

Li Haoran was also confident in his Battle Armor, not considering himself inferior to Lu Yang. “Sure.”

“There’s not enough space to fight here. Let’s go somewhere else.”

The two left the Dao-Seeking Sect’s core area, passed through the outer grasslands, and landed amidst a range of towering mountains. This was also the Dao-Seeking Sect’s territory, and disciples often came here to test extremely powerful techniques. freewebnovel.com

During the flight, Lu Yang had noticed that Li Haoran’s flying speed increased significantly while wearing the armor.

“Shall we begin?”

“Bring it on!”

The two had made progress in their cultivation and were eager to know their current combat strength, which they needed to verify through battle.

Lu Yang dared not underestimate Li Haoran. This is a half-immortal who possesses the Reincarnation Incipient Dao Fruit. Challenging him while I’m only at the Double Infants Stage is exceedingly difficult.

He drew out the Qingfeng Sword and eight other sharp blades, tossing them into the air to form a sword array. “Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array!”

Li Haoran felt the sword array emanate an intangible force that forced him to kneel. This invisible force was too powerful and tyrannical, and resistance was futile.

“I've long heard that Senior Brother Lu Yang has a sword array that can make people kneel. Now that I've experienced it firsthand today, it’s truly extraordinary. But this move alone isn't enough to deal with your junior brother!”

Just as Li Haoran knelt compliantly, his body suddenly disassembled, splitting into six parts: head, torso, and four limbs.

The Immortal-Exterminating Sword Array was an extremely powerful control skill that could force people to kneel; even Meng Jingzhou couldn't withstand it.

But being unable to withstand it didn't mean that there was no countermeasure.

Li Haoran’s separated legs remained parallel to the ground, indicating that he was still kneeling. But this didn't hinder his combat.

“True Fire Tornado!”

True fire formed a tornado. With wind fueling the true fire, its power multiplied exponentially. The entire forest turned into a sea of flames. Trees in its path were instantly charred to cinders, and the ground became dark, scorched earth.

Though Lu Yang could also control true fire, his mastery couldn't compare to Li Haoran, who had a Fire Spirit Root.

Lu Yang dared not be careless against Li Haoran. The latter felt the same and used one of his trump cards right from the outset.

Although Li Haoran was considered an unbeatable peerless prodigy in the outside world, he knew the one truly sweeping through the Nascent Soul Stage wasn't himself but Lu Yang.

In the outside world, Acting Sect Leader Lu and Young Creed Leader Lu were acknowledged as number one prodigies.

But Li Haoran was aware that these two identities were actually the same person. Senior Brother Lu Yang has only displayed half of his strength to the outside world, yet he is already considered the number one prodigy. How terrifying must his true strength be?!

“Sword Qi into Tiger!”

The sword Qi transformed into a bone-winged qiongqi and roared forth, dispersing the True Fire Dragon Tornado.

“Heavenly Fire Descent!’

In an instant, heaven and earth changed color. The sky turned crimson, and rain fell. The air became so scorchingly dry that even inhaling a single breath could sear one's throat.

In the past, Li Haoran couldn't perform this move. With the Battle Armor’s enhancement now, the built-in arrays reduced the strain and increased his spellcasting speed.

“One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!”

The Qingfeng Sword plunged into the scorched earth. Countless replicas burst forth like bamboo shoots after rain. Ten thousand swords launched together, vowing to pierce the heavens!

This time, Lu Yang and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul executed it simultaneously, doubling the number of swords. Dense Qingfeng Swords flew skyward, forming a barrier. Not a single drop of heavenly fire could reach the ground.

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul could cast spells directly from the dantian.

Had a Divine Transfiguration cultivator observed the battle from the sidelines, they would have trembled in fear. Moving mountains, overturning seas, altering celestial phenomena—how was this combat at the Nascent Soul Stage? Even among Divine Transfiguration cultivators, few could achieve this level.

Suddenly, a black figure appeared behind Lu Yang, launching a fierce attack—it was another Battle Armor!

The Battle Armor had used some unknown material that evaded detection from spiritual consciousness.

A great Buddha ascended. Lu Yang unleashed the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body, dodging the Battle Armor's ambush.

He looked at Li Haoran’s body parts dancing in the air, then at the armor that had ambushed him, and revealed a smile. “Junior Brother Li, this Battle Armor contains your corpse, right?”

Li Haoran could regenerate severed limbs. He could use the detached parts to reassemble a new body, then use the Corpse-Driving Technique to control his own corpse in battle.

“As expected of Senior Brother Lu Yang, you realized so quickly.” Li Haoran’s voice came from the Battle Armor that ambushed Lu Yang; it was Li Haoran's corpse speaking.

Li Haoran felt that only Lu Yang could figure it out this quickly. Anyone else probably wouldn't have thought of this even after the battle has concluded.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, you're too strong. Don't blame me for fighting two against one.”

Lu Yang flashed a broad smile. “How could I blame my junior brother?”

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul flew out from his dantian, unleashing a set of Arhat Fist on Li Haoran’s body.

“Nascent soul?”

Li Haoran couldn't help but feel that Lu Yang’s nascent soul was different from his, seeming to carry an extra spark of sentience. It doesn't seem like Senior Brother Lu Yang is controlling it, but more like the Unbeatable Nascent Soul is attacking independently.

“Fire Infant, appear!”

Li Haoran also summoned his nascent soul, which burned with flames, and was thus called the Fire Infant.

Now, Li Haoran needed to simultaneously control his Fire Infant and corpse to fight the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, while his true self fought Lu Yang. However, this placed extremely high demands on one’s mental power; he couldn’t control both the Fire Infant and the corpse precisely.

On the other hand, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul seemed to require no control; each of its strikes accurately hit vital points, even severing his connection to the corpse several times.

It’s like fighting another Senior Brother Lu Yang!

Just what on earth is going on with Senior Brother Lu Yang’s nascent soul?!

“Junior Brother Li, take this move! Be careful!” Lu Yang hollered.

He and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul simultaneously executed Town in Palm. The sky shattered, and one giant hand descended from above. Mountains collapsed, and another giant hand burst out from the earth.

“Fire Infant, return!” Frightened, Li Haoran hastily recalled his Fire Infant, merging with it to become a Fire Person.

Previously, when he transformed into a Fire Person, he could always avoid all attacks successfully; even Meng Jingzhou couldn’t hit him.

But faced with two palms converging, there was no way he could dodge it. With such a large-scale attack, he couldn’t escape its range even if he ran.

Boom!

The two palms closed, flattening Li Haoran in his Fire Person form.

Town in Palm was a spatial divine ability. It wasn’t merely two giant hands pressing together; it was two miniature spaces colliding. The immense power generated was far beyond what a Nascent Soul cultivator could withstand.

Lu Yang gleefully ceased his attack.

Coordinating with the Unbeatable Nascent Soul in battle yielded surprisingly good results.

Chapter 885: Lose Face

“Senior Brother, the power of your moves is really something.”

Li Haoran, in his Fire Person form, slowly inflated and returned to his original appearance.

He knew that Lu Yang had held back at the last moment. Otherwise, he would have died or been severely injured.

Li Haoran remembered that during the trip to the East Sea, the gap between him and Lu Yang wasn’t this large. How has it widened so much after this real fight?

During the battle, I had executed several moves, thinking that even if I couldn’t defeat Senior Brother Lu Yang, I could at least give him a hard time.

But what happened was the opposite—those moves were all broken by Senior Brother Lu Yang through brute force.

Lu Yang exhaled slowly, as if recalling his experiences, and sighed with emotion. “My nascent soul is finally obedient.”

All those beatings from the Unbeatable Nascent Soul weren’t in vain. At long last, I have reaped the benefits—any technique can be doubled. So satisfying!

Li Haoran, “...”

Senior Brother, so your nascent soul has been uncontrollable all this time?

“Junior Brother Li, you’re also very good. If it were any other Nascent Soul cultivator, they wouldn’t have been able to withstand even two of your moves.” Lu Yang’s words weren’t flattery but the truth.

Li Haoran smiled bitterly and shook his head. “I’m still far inferior to you, Senior Brother.”

After the battle concluded, the two performed the Tree-Planting Mantra, moved mountain stones, diverted rivers, and restored the destroyed mountain forest to its original state before leaving the scene.

~~~

Upon returning to Heaven’s Gate Peak, Lu Yang saw Yun Zhi sitting on the monarch chair, a sheet of paper spread on the table.

Lu Yang walked over curiously and found it was a celestial chart covered with stars. Yun Zhi would circle certain stars every now and then.

“Big Senior Sister, are you studying celestial phenomena?”

“No, I’m marking my golden cores.”

Yun Zhi looked up, sizing up Lu Yang. The corner of her mouth lifted slightly, then quickly smoothed out again. “You’ve finally defeated your nascent soul?”

Lu Yang nodded with relief.

“Not bad. Faster than Senior Immortal Fairy.”

Ah?” Lu Yang was befuddled by Yun Zhi’s words. “Are you saying that the Immortal Fairy hadn’t yet defeated the Unbeatable Nascent Soul when she was at my level?

“Senior Immortal Fairy, care to come out and explain?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted and emerged from Lu Yang’s body in a huff, glaring at Yun Zhi. “Lass Yun, you see it but don’t say it!”

Yun Zhi pretended not to see the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s fury and said leisurely, “The Unbeatable Nascent Soul is the strongest version of oneself. Its techniques are exquisite, its force precise, and even the transitions between moves are flawless.

“Senior Immortal Fairy, even for you, defeating the Unbeatable Nascent Soul wasn’t easy, was it?”

The first time Yun Zhi laid her eyes upon the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, she knew it represented a perfect state of oneself. No one could defeat it immediately upon reaching the Nascent Soul Stage.

Not even Senior Immortal Fairy is an exception.

“In other words, Immortal Fairy, you also suffered beatings from the Unbeatable Nascent Soul?” Lu Yang remarked with schadenfreude.

All along, the Immortal Fairy has acted high and mighty, instructing me and saying things like I can’t even defeat a mere Unbeatable Nascent Soul and that my cultivation isn’t up to par.

Who would have thought? I’m not the only one who was beaten by the Unbeatable Nascent Soul—even its creator couldn’t avoid the beatings.

“Senior Immortal Fairy, with your guidance, Little Junior Brother has progressed and grown faster.

“Back then, you had no one to guide you. Surely you took longer than Little Junior Brother to defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, right? For instance, you only defeated it when you were about to break through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage?”

With her little secret exposed, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stamped her foot furiously. “Lass Yun, you’re doing this on purpose, aren’t you?!”

This was also why the Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt guilty whenever the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was mentioned. To defeat it, she had spent her entire Unbeatable Nascent Soul Stage getting beaten.

This goes against the lofty image I’ve built before Xiao Yangzi.

In order to defeat the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had suppressed her cultivation realm and avoided breaking through. After defeating it, she could no longer maintain the suppression and directly broke through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

Therefore, she didn’t know what could be achieved after defeating it; everything was in theory.

Yun Zhi said seriously, “I’m not exposing your shortcomings, Senior Immortal Fairy. But as you are the creator of the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, sharing your experience with Little Junior Brother will help him better understand its existence. All of this is for Little Junior Brother’s sake.”

“For Xiao Yangzi’s sake?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that Yun Zhi had a point. After a moment of inner conflict, she decided to let the matter of Yun Zhi exposing her flaws slide.

“Little Junior Brother, since you’ve defeated the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, you should cultivate in peace and prepare to break through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.” Yun Zhi pointed out the next step to Lu Yang, exhorting him not to wander around anymore.

“By the way, Big Senior Sister, since you’ve left Incarceration Peak, does that mean Guan Shanhai has confessed?”

Yun Zhi shook her head. “After all, he’s an immortal and has a steadfast Dao Heart. Even with only three ethereal souls, he’s not one to easily yield. I’m just coming out for a temporary break; I’ll return to continue the beating later.”

~~~

What Lu Yang lacked to reach the Apex Nascent Soul Stage was merely the accumulation of spirit energy, a step that required time.

A year and a half passed.

Lu Yang had been meditating on Heaven’s Gate Peak. He would occasionally borrow breakthrough insights written by seniors from the scripture library, with no time to care about affairs in the outside world.

Anyway, there wasn’t much to care about. In this year and a half, the outside world was peaceful; not even Transcendent Tribulation battles occurred.

Finally, Lu Yang felt abundant spirit energy flowing within him—a sign of reaching the Apex Nascent Soul Stage.

If it were some Nascent Soul old fossil, achieving this step would still require struggling to break through a bottleneck.

But Lu Yang was different. He was now only a thought away from the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

Advancing from the Nascent Soul Stage to the Divine Transfiguration Stage was a major hurdle that cultivators must face. Previously, as long as one broke through a bottleneck, the next cultivation realm would come naturally—not too dangerous.

But breaking through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage was different. This was a cultivator’s first direct confrontation with a heavenly tribulation. From then on, every major realm breakthrough would face tribulation trials—extremely dangerous.

And Lu Yang was in even greater danger. He didn’t know if the Heaven Mandate Immortal was still alive and paying attention to this place, or if the heavenly tribulation could sense the ancient secrets he grasped.

“Xiao Yangzi, don’t be afraid. Which heavenly tribulation wouldn’t give this immortal face? Nothing will happen!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy confidently raised a thumb, revealing a brilliant smile.

If someone not in the know saw the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s gesture, their morale would be boosted, and they would break through in one go.

Unfortunately, Lu Yang was in the know.

“Having come this far, not breaking through isn’t an option.”

Lu Yang sighed. He released his self-imposed restraints and drew upon the spiritual opportunities of heaven and earth, preparing to undergo the heavenly tribulation. freewebnovel.com

Crack—

Heaven’s Gate Peak was covered in dark clouds, with lightning flickering and dancing.

“Hey, look, someone on Heaven’s Gate Peak is about to undergo a tribulation.”

“This lightning tribulation doesn’t look that powerful—at the Divine Transfiguration level. It’s Junior Brother Lu Yang, isn’t it?”

“Senior Brother Lu Yang is breaking through the Nascent Soul Stage already? What a fast cultivation speed.”

Hearing that Lu Yang was facing a tribulation, the Dao-Seeking Sect disciples curiously gathered at the foot of Heaven’s Gate Peak to spectate, and the crowd kept growing.

“What kind of lightning tribulation is this?” A junior female disciple who didn’t understand tribulations asked, worried for Lu Yang’s safety.

“White lightning tribulation—it should be the Xuanji Divine Lightning.[1]

“The ninth-ranked lightning tribulation; so impressive.”

Sensing the pressure overhead, Lu Yang secretly exhaled in relief. It’s just the ninth-ranked Xuanji Divine Lightning? I can handle it.

“Strange, isn’t the direction of the lightning tribulation a bit off?” The Void Refinement senior male disciple knitted his brows, sensing something amiss.

Suddenly, a white lightning bolt tore through the sky, not aimed at Lu Yang, but at the spectating disciples at the mountain’s base.

“Run! The Xuanji Divine Lightning is targeting us!”

Someone yelled. Without thinking, everyone turned and ran.

Only after reaching the other peaks did the divine lightning cease its attack.

Witnessing this, Lu Yang’s eye twitched. Why does the Xuanji Divine Lightning look like it’s clearing the area?

Logically, the foot of Heaven’s Gate Peak should already be beyond the attack range of a heavenly tribulation faced by a Nascent Soul cultivator.

Moreover, if the ninth-ranked Xuanji Divine Lightning is merely used to clear the area... At this thought, Lu Yang gulped. Then what heavenly tribulation am I about to face?

1. There are several meanings to Xuanji. First, it could refer to the first four stars of the Big Dipper, though it could also be used to refer broadly to the Big Dipper or the North Star. Alternatively, it could be referring to a rotating part in an instrument for astronomical observations in the past. ☜

Chapter 886: Unbeatable Divine Lightning

“Immortal Fairy, do you know what’s going on?” Lu Yang anxiously inquired of the ancient immortal.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head like a rattle-drum. “No idea. When this immortal became a Divine Transfiguration cultivator, there was no heavenly tribulation.”

Lu Yang remembered. In the ancient era, one didn’t need to undergo a heavenly tribulation when breaking through from the Nascent Soul Stage to the Divine Transfiguration Stage. It was only after the Heaven Mandate Immortal achieved immortality that this rule was added.

Damn Heaven Mandate Immortal, can’t you do something good?

According to the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s theory, having cultivators undergo heavenly tribulations was to test whether their Dao Heart was firm. If they could pass the heavenly tribulation, they would gain great benefits.

Lu Yang looked up at the dark, oppressive sky. There, lightning flickered faintly, as if accumulating power.

He felt that whether he could survive the heavenly tribulation might not have much to do with how steadfast his Dao Heart was.

It mainly depends on whether my fate profile is tough enough.

~~~

“Strange, just what kind of tribulation has Junior Brother Lu Yang attracted?” The Void Refinement senior male disciple frowned in thought. He had never heard of any lightning tribulation that first cleared the area with Xuanji Divine Lightning.

Standing on other peaks far from Heaven’s Gate Peak, and with Xuanji Divine Lightning flickering around it, they couldn’t clearly see the situation at the center of the heavenly tribulation.

“Even when Big Senior faced the top-ranked Three Pure Ones Heavenly Lightning Tribulation back then, something like this didn’t happen.”

“Could Junior Brother Lu Yang have drawn a completely unprecedented heavenly tribulation?”

“A brand-new heavenly tribulation?”

“Not necessarily brand-new. It could also be that someone once faced it but didn’t survive, leaving no historical record.”

Whichever the case, it was sufficient to show that the heavenly tribulation Lu Yang faced would be terrifyingly powerful.

“Look! The real lightning tribulation has appeared!” The junior disciples pointed at the distant Heaven’s Gate Peak and shouted.

“It really is an unprecedented lightning tribulation!” the Void Refinement senior male disciple stated with certainty. Even from such a distance, one could feel the faint crackle of lightning in the air and the quaking of space itself. It was hard to imagine what Lu Yang was experiencing at the epicenter.

“Is it an illusion? Why does it feel stronger than the Three Pure Ones Heavenly Lightning Tribulation?”

Sensing the anomaly at Heaven’s Gate Peak, Yun Zhi left Incarceration Peak and stood atop Pill Cauldron Peak, slightly furrowing her brows as she gazed toward Heaven’s Gate Peak.

~~~

Crack—

Purple-cyan heavenly lightning descended. The divine lightning was resplendent and blindingly bright, like a great sun falling.

This was a divine lightning unprecedented throughout history!

The moment the divine lightning appeared, Lu Yang’s hair stood on end as he sensed extreme danger. This is absolutely something I can’t withstand alone.

“Unbeatable Nascent Soul!”

The Unbeatable Nascent Soul appeared, its little face serious, showing no intention to flee; instead, it faced the divine lightning together with Lu Yang!

Ordinary cultivators absolutely wouldn't dare use their nascent souls to help carry the burden of the lightning tribulation. Nascent souls were fragile, and the slightest mistake could annihilate them in the tribulation. How would they transform the nascent soul into a primordial soul later?

But the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was different. Lu Yang had already witnessed its power. Nothing would happen to it even if it bore half the pressure from the lightning tribulation.

Besides, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul has no intention to flee, which means it can withstand it!

Lu Yang had tested it before. After he defeated the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, it would still want to flee when in danger, but he could control it not to.

The purple-cyan divine lightning forked into two, striking Lu Yang and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul respectively. Gritting his teeth, Lu Yang resisted with pure physical strength, enduring unbearable pain. His clothes shredded, flesh torn open. He felt even his bones and blood tingling, as if they were soaked in lightning.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

Purple-cyan divine lightning struck endlessly. Enveloped by lightning, Heaven’s Gate Peak shook slightly. This was heavenly might, not something a mountain could contend with.

“Strange, why does this tribulation look like the Unbeatable Divine Lightning?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy murmured in the mental space.

No matter how softly she murmured, Lu Yang could still hear it clearly. “What is the Unbeatable Divine Lightning?”

Seizing the moment between waves of divine lightning, Lu Yang hastily consumed pills, rapidly healing himself and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

She replied, “It’s something from when the Heaven Mandate Immortal was creating lightning tribulations. He said he wanted to create one that only cultivators with an Unbeatable Nascent Soul could pass. He asked if this immortal could give some suggestions.”

“What did you say then, Immortal Fairy?”

“This immortal said the more powerful, the better.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, can't you leave me a way out?

No wonder this lightning tribulation has never appeared. So it's because this is a lightning tribulation that only strikes those with an Unbeatable Nascent Soul!

Heaven Mandate Immortal, if you find the Unbeatable Nascent Soul an eyesore, go look for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy! What's the point of bullying me?

“And the name of this lightning tribulation is?”

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal called it the Supreme Heaven-Splitting Golden Palace Divine Lightning. This immortal said this name was too long and hard to remember. I proposed to call it the Unbeatable Divine Lightning; it’s simple, pleasing to the ears, and rolls off the tongue.”

After nine waves of divine lightning, Lu Yang was charred black, spitting dark smoke. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul wasn't any better, heavily injured. Lu Yang quickly had the Unbeatable Nascent Soul return to his dantian to rest. freewebnovel.com

The Unbeatable Divine Lightning’s residual power flowed across Lu Yang’s exterior. His soul and body were slowly strengthening.

~~~

“The divine lightning descended nine times. This should be considered over, right?” Gu Junye remarked earnestly. Among his peers, he was the most knowledgeable about heavenly tribulations.

Nine is the ultimate number. Lightning tribulations only descend nine times; there won't be a tenth.

“That should be the case... Wait, why are there still more lightning tribulations?” The Void Refinement senior male disciple was just about to concur when he saw a new lightning tribulation brewing above Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“How is this possible?!”

“It's the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulations!”[1]

“Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation? Isn't that something Divine Transfiguration cultivators face when advancing to the Void Refinement Stage? And it's also the top-ranked lightning tribulation!”

“Heaven knows what's going on.”

Everyone fell silent, worried for Lu Yang’s safety. A Nascent Soul cultivator surviving the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation—was that possible?

~~~

The moment Lu Yang saw the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation, his heart sank. Is there still time to write my will?

Isn't this lightning tribulation way beyond the syllabus?

“Immortal Fairy, what do I do?”

“Uh, how about this immortal show herself and make the heavenly tribulation leave?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that the heavenly tribulation had poor eyesight and couldn't recognize her. If I were to go out personally, it would probably give me some face and leave.

Lu Yang was somewhat troubled. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence was a secret. He was unsure if the Xuanji Divine Lightning could conceal the traces of an immortal’s moves. It wouldn't be good if the senior brothers and sisters see her.

Sensing the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation already locking onto him, Lu Yang suddenly said, “No need to trouble you yet, Immortal Fairy. I have an idea. This is the perfect time to test it. If it fails, you can still intervene, Immortal Fairy.”

“What idea?”

Lu Yang smiled without answering.

~~~

Gazing at the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation that seemed to carry the might to annihilate the world, a wave of concern washed over Gu Junye and the others.

“Say, do you think Senior Brother Lu Yang can survive it?”

1. “Qian” is one of the Bahia or Eight Trigrams and represents heaven. ☜

Chapter 887: Heart Devil

Sensing the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation locking onto him, Lu Yang immediately executed the karmic divine ability—Defying Heaven Changing Name!

He was no longer “Lu Yang” but “Lu Yin.”

This was a supreme karmic divine ability; even Divine Transfiguration cultivators couldn’t learn it. However, the exceptionally gifted Lu Yang had long mastered it and now found a use for it!

“Defying Heaven Changing Name—defying the heavenly tribulation by changing the name. A great name for this divine ability.”

Above Heaven’s Gate Peak, the Qian-Heaven Divine Lightning dancing within the dark clouds suddenly calmed down. It realized its target was missing.

The cyan Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation circled Heaven’s Gate Peak several times but couldn’t find “Lu Yang.”

Lu Yin saw that this wouldn’t go anywhere. I can’t just stall like this.

“Since Defying Heaven Changing Name works on lightning tribulations...”

He smiled, dispelling the karmic divine ability and reverting to his original name.

Spotting Lu Yang again, the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation became exceedingly excited. While searching for Lu Yang, it had been accumulating power. Now that Lu Yang appeared, it was time to unleash its full power!

Cyan light flickered, illuminating Heaven’s Gate Peak like midsummer noon, blindingly bright.

Just as the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation was about to strike Lu Yang, he performed Defying Heaven Changing Name again, becoming “Lu Yin.”

The Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation lost its target. But it couldn’t retract the lightning bolt it had struck, which bypassed Lu Yin and hit the ground.

“Just as I thought.” Lu Yin heaved a sigh of relief. I’ve found a safe way to survive the tribulation. freewebnovel.com

Generally, no one would avoid lightning tribulations. As the Heaven Mandate Immortal once said, lightning tribulations were both a trial and a fortuitous opportunity. Being struck could strengthen oneself.

But the premise was not being struck to death.

Lu Yin knew his small frame couldn’t withstand the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation. The best method was to evade.

“Lu Yin” changed back to “Lu Yang.” The Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation descended again. Before it could reach Lu Yang, he changed his name once more, causing the strike to miss.

This repeated nine times.

Nine was the ultimate number, and the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation also had only nine strikes. After nine rounds, one could be considered to have passed the tribulation.

~~~

“Heavens, a Nascent Soul cultivator survived the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation?!”

Although no one could tell what Lu Yang had done, they could see that he had passed. The entire Dao-Seeking Sect erupted in cheers.

A Nascent Soul cultivator facing the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation was already impossible, let alone succeeding. This was an unprecedented feat!

Gu Junye stood with his hands clasped behind his back, a faint smile on his lips, his gaze profound as he recalled the past. “As expected of the Xuanyuan Sword Master, reminiscent of his former bearing.”

“What spell did Senior Brother Lu Yang just use? The lightning tribulation didn’t even attack him!” Even Li Haoran, who possessed Creed Leader Qin’s memories, couldn’t figure out what Lu Yang had done.

“It’s finally over this time, right?”

“Why is Senior Brother Lu Yang motionless, just floating in the sky?”

“The Xuanji Divine Lightning around Heaven’s Gate Peak hasn’t dispersed. The heavenly tribulation isn’t over. Junior Brother Lu has fallen into the Heart Devil Tribulation!” A Void Refinement senior male disciple quickly discerned the issue.

Tao Yaoye watched Lu Yang with deep concern, silently praying for his safe return. Senior Brother Lu Yang has a steadfast Dao Heart; he’ll be fine.”

Li Haoran reminded, “Don’t forget, Senior Brother Lu Yang is under our Sect Leader’s tutelage. Has any disciple under the Sect Leader ever been trapped in a Heart Devil Tribulation?”

The reasoning made sense, but Tao Yaoye was still worried about Lu Yang.

~~~

“Where is this?”

Bewilderment flashed past Lu Yang’s eyes. His mind felt muddled, unable to remember what had happened or why he was here.

Lu Yang slowly got up. He wore a magnificent imperial robe woven with gold and silver threads, impervious to weapons, fire, water, and myriad spells. The robe bore an embroidery of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy on the front and Yun Zhi on the back.

Turning his head, Lu Yang saw the monarch chair he had been sitting on. It symbolized supreme status and was a tribute from the Demon Region, said to be personally crafted by Supreme Lord Zhu Tian.

Looking around, he realized he was in a temporary palace. Before him were piled court documents and an imperial jade seal.

He flipped the imperial jade seal, finding it inscribed: “Longevity and Prosperity to the Great Dou Dynasty.”

Lost memories flooded back. Lu Yang finally recalled his identity.

“I remember. I am the Emperor of the Great Dou Dynasty.”

The Dou Emperor’s personal eunuch approached him with a tray holding facedown wooden plaques.

“Your Majesty, whose plaque will you choose tonight?” his personal eunuch Meng Jingzhou inquired.

Lu Yang couldn’t quite remember who was in his imperial harem. He casually flipped one of the wooden plaques.

Huang Doudou.

He flipped another.

Yun Zhi.

Then it was Tao Yaoye, Lan Ting...

“Your Majesty, are you planning to sleep with all of them tonight?” his personal eunuch Meng Jingzhou asked hesitantly.

“Summon them all. I wish to see them.” Lu Yang waved his hand, issuing a command that brooked no refusal.

Soon, the members of Lu Yang’s harem arrived one after another like a flock of orioles and swallows—a feast for the eyes.

“Xiao Yangzi, you’re looking for me tonight?” Huang Doudou wore a light yellow dress, its hem swaying gently. Her clear, lake-like eyes blinked at Lu Yang.

“Little Junior Brother, you’re looking for me?” Yun Zhi resembled an immortal fairy stepping out from a painting. Clad in plain white, she was like plum blossoms covered in first snow, cold and elegant. As she walked, her steps were light, and the bells on her wrist tinkled.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang...”

Tao Yaoye, as delicate and rosy as a peach, and Lan Ting, the daughter of an aristocratic family, entered the temporary palace.

Four peerless beauties surrounded Lu Yang, some reserved, some bold, their eyes holding indescribable emotions.

Watching the four women approach, a growing sense of dissonance finally triggered Lu Yang’s original memories.

“Wasn’t I facing a heavenly tribulation? Why am I here?

“Wait, tribulation? Is this the Heart Devil Tribulation?”

Lu Yang was so startled that he plopped onto the ground, scrambling backward as cold sweat broke out. He kept as far away as he could, especially from Huang Doudou and Yun Zhi.

He hadn’t been this terrified even during the Unbeatable Divine Lightning Tribulation and the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation.

“The books say that during the Heart Devil Tribulation, the heart devil will manifest as your greatest fear or your deepest desire, causing you to lose yourself in the environment it has created. Even when people realize it’s a Heart Devil Tribulation, many willingly continue to succumb.

“To pass a Heart Devil Tribulation, one must not only see through it but also defeat the enemies within.”

Lu Yang looked at Huang Doudou on his left, then Yun Zhi on his right.

Defeating them would be a miracle!

Just as Lu Yang mulled over countermeasures, he heard a crack. Looking up, he saw the space above fracturing, cracks quickly spreading throughout the entire place.

Space shattered. Lu Yang returned to his senses and found himself in the mental space, facing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with rolled-up sleeves.

She leaned close to him in concern. “Xiao Yangzi, are you alright? You fell into a Heart Devil Tribulation earlier. I don’t know what you saw, but you kept grinning foolishly.”

“...Something almost happened.”

“Everlasting, you’re finally alive.” A hearty laugh echoed in the mental space.

Why is there a third person in the mental space? Lu Yang hastily turned to see a figure outside the mental space, carrying the inherent aura of a leader like a monarch.

Lu Yang had seen this face before.

It was the Heaven Mandate Immortal.

Chapter 888: Are You Sure That Was a Heart Devil Tribulation?

“Everlasting, you’re finally alive.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal inherently carried the bearing of a monarch, his speech authoritative yet ethereal, like a deity stepping forth from the pages of a book.

He gazed at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, a myriad of thoughts swirling within him. “History cycles, ages pass; countless dynasties rise and fall, reduced to dust and gravel.

“Old friends depart, beyond recall; past events turn to sand, beyond reshape. How many today have witnessed with their own eyes the ancient splendor when prodigies rose together and dragons and serpents surged across the land? And how many still remember the era when the world was ordered and the Five Immortals governed?

“When I learned of your future through the historical projection back then, I foresaw this day and waited here for your return, Everlasting.

“Fellow Daoist, it’s been a long time. Have you fared well?”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal seemed to stride forth from the end of the river of time, his presence thick with the weight and richness of history. His eyes were profound, as if piercing through all matters of the world; no secret could hide before him, and all changes lay within his foresight.

Even the Qilin Immortal hadn’t given Lu Yang such a feeling.

Clad in white robes and white boots, with his hands clasped behind his back, he took a step forward... then bumped into the barrier of the mental space with a thud, his head snapping back.

“Wait, why is this kid’s mental space so sturdy?”

Standing outside Lu Yang’s mental space, the Heaven Mandate Immortal knocked on the barrier, producing a dull sound.

He had originally intended to pass through and enter.

Who could have guessed this kid’s mental barrier is excessively sturdy? Even I couldn’t penetrate it.

Why do all sorts of mishaps happen whenever I meet Everlasting?

The Heaven Mandate Immortal awkwardly tapped the barrier and called out, “Uh, could you two let me in?”

Lu Yang also didn’t know why his mental space was so robust. I wonder whether the Immortal Fairy or Big Senior Sister reinforced it.

He opened a slit. Seeing this, the Heaven Mandate Immortal hurriedly squeezed through.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal coughed twice. He had initially planned to maintain his dignified air, but after being barred outside, pretending to be formidable now seemed somewhat belated.

“You split off an immortal thought and hid it within the heavenly tribulation?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy discerned that the Heaven Mandate Immortal before her was not his main body but merely a thought left behind countless ages ago.

“Indeed.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy narrowed her eyes, her expression somewhat unfriendly. “In other words, that Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation was your arrangement?”

How could the Heaven Mandate Immortal not realize the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation had displeased her? He hastily explained, “It was my arrangement, but that lightning tribulation couldn’t have killed anyone. It’s true. Everlasting, you must believe me.”

“Really?”

“Really, really.”

Noticing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was still somewhat skeptical, he sighed and had to explain further. “Back then, this young friend’s figure appeared in the historical projection. It should be him who called out your name and resurrected you.

“Yet, none of us were by your side; that shouldn’t be the case. It meant you didn’t find any of us, Everlasting. If you had found any of us, we would have taken you to see the historical projection of the chess game and not let you go alone.

“Therefore, I concluded then that something had happened to all of us, preventing us from contacting you.

“That was why I left this immortal thought within the heavenly tribulation as a contingency.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal hesitated and asked, “Uh, let me ask first. Everlasting, you haven’t seen my main body, have you?”

“No.”

“That’s good then.”

If she had seen my main body, wouldn’t I have wasted forty thousand years camping in the heavenly tribulation for nothing? How embarrassing would that be if word of this gets out?

“At the time, you should have attached yourself to this young friend’s mental space, and you must have taught him to condense the Unbeatable Golden Core, granting him the Unbeatable Nascent Soul during his Nascent Soul Stage.

“Hence, I arranged the Supreme Heaven-Splitting Golden Palace Divine Lightning. When the tribulation detects that the one facing it possesses an Unbeatable Nascent Soul, it will descend.

“However, this single detection method wasn’t sufficient. After all, the person undergoing tribulation might overcome it through other means, or perhaps they had condensed the Unbeatable Nascent Soul themselves.”

Lu Yang carefully recalled. It seems that my Unbeatable Golden Soul indeed had little to do with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. I had condensed it first, and only later did she tell me it was the Unbeatable Nascent Soul.

All she had done was spare me the need to discover its usage, directly telling me how to use it.

“After that, I arranged the Qian-Heaven Heavenly Tribulation, which Nascent Soul cultivators absolutely can’t pass. If you show yourself, the tribulation will automatically disperse on its own.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal looked at Lu Yang, gnashing his teeth. “Who would have thought? This kid survived the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation without relying on you!”

He was merely a thought left by the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s true body. After forty thousand years, his power had nearly depleted, and his control over the heavenly tribulation was limited. Otherwise, he would have unleashed the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation long ago.

His remaining strength was only enough for this single meeting with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, so he had to be cautious with his decision.

“Fortunately, breaking through from the Nascent Soul Stage to the Divine Transfiguration Stage also entails the Heart Devil Tribulation. If this kid knows you, Everlasting, you would surely become his heart devil.

“Just as expected, you appeared in his heart devil. That’s how I confirmed you were within this kid’s body.”

Lu Yang was dumbfounded. “Are you sure that was my heart devil?”

Heart devils either instilled fear or tempted one to willingly lose themselves in it. I don’t think taking Big Senior Sister and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy into my imperial harem fits either category.

“It was naturally your heart devil.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal asked impassively, “When you recall that scene from the Heart Devil Tribulation, do you feel fear?”

The thought that his memories might be noticed by Yun Zhi sent a shiver through Lu Yang. So this Heart Devil Tribulation doesn’t make me recall the scenarios I’m scared of—it creates scenarios to scare me!

Whose Heart Devil Tribulation works like this?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sensed something amiss. “Xiao Yangzi, I appeared in your Heart Devil Tribulation and made you feel afraid. What happened in there?”

Lu Yang dared not say that he had enjoyed the fortune of a harem, embracing both Yun Zhi and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. I’d have to be tired of living to say that.

Tears streamed down his face, and his voice was choked with emotion. “In the Heart Devil Tribulation, Immortal Fairy, your temperament changed drastically. You kept hitting me. It felt so... unfamiliar.”

“But I saw you grinning foolishly?”

“Immortal Fairy, you don’t understand. That was a forced smile, so that you wouldn’t worry about me outside.”

Seeing how her Xiao Yangzi was so pitiful, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy affectionately caressed his head. “Don’t cry, don’t cry. It’s fine. This immortal would never beat you.”

However, Lu Yang kept weeping miserably, utterly inconsolable. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gritted her teeth, resolved to depose the original successor. “How about this? I’ll let Lass Yun be the Third Dou Emperor; you’ll be the Second.”

Startled, Lu Yang immediately stopped sobbing. How did crying get me closer to manifesting the heart devil in reality?

The Heaven Mandate Immortal, “...”

Hold on, Everlasting, this side of you feels so... unfamiliar.

Chapter 889: Hui Doudou’s Origin

“So you are Lu Yang?” the Heaven Mandate Immortal asked calmly.

“Senior Heaven Mandate, do you know me as well?” Lu Yang was overwhelmed by the honor. I haven’t even introduced myself.

“I was watching from above when you changed your name to trick the lightning tribulation.”

Lu Yang was speechless.

“Who could have thought you’d master Defying Heaven Changing Fate at the Nascent Soul Stage? Juniors are redoubtable indeed.”

Lu Yang didn’t know how to respond to that. Should I go along with what the Heaven Mandate Immortal said, or correct him and clarify that I’ve only learned Defying Heaven Changing Name?[1]

Fortunately, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy came to his rescue.

She asked, “So what happened after this immortal perished?”

Since this thought of the Heaven Mandate Immortal had persisted from ancient times to the present day, what he knew likely surpassed even that of Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi.

“After the four of us learned that you would perish in the future, we took precautions through various means. For example, Epoch often used his Epoch Dao Fruit to glimpse future events; my main body split off this thought of mine, hiding me within the lightning tribulation to observe your movements; Nine-Layers and Qilin searched for the ‘Sixth Immortal.’

“One day before your incident, the Epoch Immortal viewed your future, but all he saw was peace.

“On the day of your incident, I saw you enter your cave abode. After about an hour, your aura suddenly fluctuated violently, then abruptly vanished. Your body, soul, and Dao Fruit—everything was gone. All beings also forgot your existence.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned. I don’t remember this. It seems I really wasn’t in the right state back then.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal continued, “My main body, along with Epoch and the other two, sensed something amiss with you. We rushed to the North Star and sealed it.

“Soon, we discovered an unknown immortal in a corner of the North Star.

“No one knew how this immortal struck within your cave above, killing you silently without leaving a trace of battle, nor how they escaped under our very noses.

“A cataclysmic immortal battle commenced not long after. That immortal’s strength exceeded our expectations; they could hold their own against four of us without being at a disadvantage.

“No, I should say that only such combat prowess could have slain you.

“That immortal didn’t fight to the death with us; they kept fleeing throughout the battle and did manage to run away.

“To prevent that immortal’s escape, the four of us refined the stars into continents, laying a Four Immortals Seal at the bottom. Only your resurrection, combined with the power of us four, can break that seal.”

This was to force that immortal to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Clearly, that immortal refused to take the bait, preferring to be trapped in the box-world than revive the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“It was within our expectations that the immortal wouldn’t resurrect you. Thus, we chose our original method, faith power.

“Do you remember the Buddhism we fabricated? That was an experiment in researching faith power. Though you paid little attention to Buddhist matters, Qing He was very invested, especially since Buddhist sects were full of tales about you.

“Qing He researched faith power thoroughly, even surpassing the four of us. According to Qing He, faith power could condense a physical form—that is, your body, Everlasting.

“To gather faith power, my main body, Epoch, and the other two established the Ember Legacy Dynasty.

“Ten thousand years after the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s founding, a prodigy was born from the Shi Huang Clan. With the Insight Dao Fruit as his foundation, he proved the Dao and attained immortality, taking the Dao name ‘Left Historian.’ The world called him the ‘Left Historian Immortal.’

“The Insight Dao Fruit could perceive the past, present, and future—the full macrocosmic loop. My main body had him observe the murder process, yet he saw nothing.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked, “Little Ling told me about this.”

“Everlasting, you’ve met Ao Ling? That saves trouble. She should have told you about the ‘Heavenly Court’ and the ‘Underworld,’ right? That comprised molding your immortal body with the Heavenly Court’s faith and summoning the Everlasting Dao Fruit or condensing the Reincarnation Dao Fruit with the Underworld’s faith system, reversing life and death to revive you.”

“Hold on, are you saying that the Underworld system could condense the Reincarnation Dao Fruit?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy interrupted the Heaven Mandate Immortal. Ao Ling hadn’t mentioned this.

“Ao Ling didn’t tell you? Oh, right, she entered slumber twenty thousand years after the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s founding. The Underworld wasn’t completely constructed then, nor was the concept of the Reincarnation Dao Fruit developed. It’s normal that she didn’t know.

“However, in the end, the Underworld couldn’t condense the Reincarnation Dao Fruit, only its incipient form.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal shook his head and sighed, regretting the decision to establish the Underworld on behalf of his main body. “It’s just that this Reincarnation Incipient Dao Fruit caused a major problem.”

“It couldn’t resurrect the dead?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked curiously.

He continued shaking his head, his expression plagued with remorse. “The Reincarnation Incipient Dao Fruit could resurrect the dead, and it did resurrect you.

“But it didn’t revive you from your immortal days. It was you from your half-immortal days.”

Lu Yang’s pupils slowly contracted. He seemed to have figured out how Hui Doudou came to be.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had two half-immortal periods, one with the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit and the other with the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit.

“You resurrected Hui Doudou?!”

“You slashed yourself with a single cut, stripping away and slaying the you who possessed the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit. Afterward, you returned to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage and recondensed an Incipient Dao Fruit.

“The Underworld resurrected your past self—the you with the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit who you once slew!”

Lu Yang roughly understood how Hui Doudou came to be, yet some points remained unclear. He gingerly raised his hand. “May I interject with a question?”

“Ask.” The Heaven Mandate Immortal was quite amicable toward the young cultivator who revived the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Correct.”

“We encountered her at the East Sea. Her temperament...how should I put it... It was somewhat different from the current Immortal Fairy—ice-cold. Did some mishap occur during the resurrection?”

From the brief contact at the East Sea, that Hui Doudou was decisive, composed, and ruthless, truly unlike the current Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal didn’t quite grasp what Lu Yang was getting at. “Isn’t being ice-cold normal?

“She has always been like that.”

“Ah?”

Chapter 890: Childlike Innocent Heart

Noticing Lu Yang’s dramatic reaction, it was now the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s turn to be stunned.

“Don’t you know? Everlasting’s personality was different in the past. Back then, after Everlasting at the Golden Core Stage defeated Qilin and me at the Foundation Establishment Stage, she maintained a cold expression and said, ‘So-called prodigies are nothing special.’

“I thought she was incredibly cool at that moment and often tried to emulate that demeanor.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal was drawn back to memories over four hundred thousand years ago. In a bamboo grove, he and the Qilin Immortal knelt on the ground, having suffered a tragic defeat. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, clad in cyan robes and a conical bamboo hat, wore a cold and detached expression, her gaze harboring contempt that looked down upon all beings.

He felt that this was how true experts should be!

“Everlasting challenged across levels with an Unbeatable Momentum and condensed the Unbeatable Golden Core. Then, with the Unbeatable Golden Core and the Unbeatable Nascent Soul, she roamed the world unimpeded, sweeping through myriad heroes and forging a resounding reputation. Back then, everyone’s legs would weaken at the sight of her.”

Lu Yang tried to imagine the scene that the Heaven Mandate Immortal described.

At the Foundation Establishment Stage, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy challenged numerous Golden Core cultivators. Icy as frost and exuding a chilling aura, she condensed the Unbeatable Golden Core under everyone’s gaze, defeated her foes, and departed triumphantly.

Pretty cool, actually.

“Later, she slashed herself, slicing away the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit. Heeding Epoch’s advice, she reclaimed her childlike innocent heart.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal looked up, sighing with emotion. “The four of us envied her deeply. Who would have thought? Even after experiencing the tribe’s catastrophe, she could still return to a childlike state of innocence and revert to her original self, achieving the Everlasting Dao through the state closest to nature. That’s how she became who she is today.”

The tribe’s catastrophe?

The phrase stirred Lu Yang’s memories. The Immortal Fairy once mentioned that she was born in a small tribe. A battle between a human and a beast had destroyed it with its residual shockwaves. When the topic came up, she had become visibly downcast. Out of regard for her feelings, I didn’t inquire further.

Judging by the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s words, the Immortal Fairy’s original personality was like her current self. It was only after her tribe’s destruction that she became cold and detached.

But that’s only natural. After all, remaining optimistic and cheerful after such a tragedy would be strange.

Lu Yang now understood. Initially, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was innocent and unpretentious. Since her tribe was destroyed, her temperament changed drastically, becoming as icy as frost. After condensing the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit, with the Epoch Immortal’s guidance, she let go of the past and returned to her original personality, attaining her Dao in Everlasting.

“But Senior Heaven Mandate Immortal, are you certain the Immortal Fairy wore a cold expression when she fought you and the Qilin Immortal back then?”

Immortal Fairy, you were at the Golden Core Stage and had that aloof demeanor, yet you could still do something like challenging across levels?

No matter how Lu Yang thought about it, the scene felt odd.

Hearing the Heaven Mandate Immortal recount her past, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face flushed. She lowered her head, watching her two big toes tap against each other, afraid to see Lu Yang’s current expression.

Only upon hearing Lu Yang’s question did she raise her head to look at him, pouting as she poked his arm. “What does my expression have to do with this? They were the ones who sought me out. With opponents already attacking, how could I possibly avoid battling?

“Besides, at that time, both Heaven Mandate and Qilin were Foundation Establishment cultivators who could challenge Golden Core cultivators. As a Golden Core cultivator fighting the two of them, it was essentially one against two. I was the one at a disadvantage!”

Lu Yang had no idea what to say. Immortal Fairy, so you genuinely consider it an honor to have defeated them both, huh? freewebnovel.com

Lu Yang had another question. “But that’s not right either. Didn’t Hui Doudou destroy the Ember Legacy Dynasty? Even the Immortal Fairy of the past wouldn’t have done such a thing.”

Given the brutality of ancient battles, it was truly rare for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy not to silence the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal after defeating them, especially the Qilin Immortal; he was a qilin born of heaven and earth, his value far surpassing any natural treasure. Yet even then, she hadn’t delivered a fatal blow.

Lu Yang reckoned that if it had been Hui Doudou, she would have eliminated them long ago.
