Chapter 891: Advancing to the Divine Transfiguration Stage

As the three conversed, a gate opened within the mental space. A woman emerged, clad in a white dress, golden threads strung through bells tied at her wrist. Her expression was cool and detached.

“Big Senior Sister, what brings you here?” Lu Yang was overjoyed to see her.

“I was observing from outside and noticed that you were trapped in the Heart Devil Tribulation, so I came to check on the situation. From the looks of it, you’ve encountered something again?”

Her gaze landed on the sole stranger present. “Who are you?”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal braced himself, as if facing a formidable foe. It was his first time meeting an expert whose aura surpassed his own.

His demeanor instantly shifted, becoming profound and inscrutable, imbued with a dense aura of history, as if he had traversed the river of time and the tumultuous mundane realm.

He swung his arms outward, his wide sleeves wrapping around his forearms before settling behind his back, and his gaze directly locked onto Yun Zhi’s eyes. “I am the Heaven Mandate Immortal. I once witnessed Fellow Daoist Yun Zhi within the heavenly tribulation.”

“So it’s a thought left by Senior Heaven Mandate Immortal, one of the Five Ancient Immortals, hidden within the heavenly tribulation. This method has its merits.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal was startled. Just as I thought, she’s an expert. She immediately discerned my origin and hinted that I’m a mere thought, unworthy to stand as her equal, and that I should summon my main body.

“You flatter me, Fellow Daoist. I never imagined an outstanding talent like yourself could appear in later generations. Juniors are redoubtable indeed.”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal smirked inwardly. By deliberately pointing out that Yun Zhi is from a later generation, I’ve seized the advantage in seniority. Let’s see how you deal with this!

“It’s just talent, nothing remarkable,” Yun Zhi said flatly, as if commenting on something utterly trivial.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal, “...”

How am I supposed to respond to that?

But soon, he no longer needed to consider this matter.

Under the gazes of Lu Yang and the other two, the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s form gradually faded, becoming translucent enough to see through.

“Heaven Mandate, is this thought of yours about to be exhausted?”

The Heaven Mandate Immortal thought, Since I’m about to disappear, there’s no need to maintain formality anymore. He pressed two fingers to his temple, then flicked them outward, laughing heartily. “Then I shall take my leave. Though I don’t know where my main body is, I still hope you can find him.”

Then the Heaven Mandate Immortal vanished, as if he had never existed.

Yun Zhi conjured three monarch chairs from nothing, gesturing for Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to sit. Her movements were as practiced as if she were within her own mental space.

“So, what did the two of you do to summon a thought of the Heaven Mandate Immortal?”

Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy truthfully recounted the tribulation process, from encountering the Heaven Mandate Immortal after passing the Heart Devil Tribulation to his mention of the Reincarnation Incipient Dao Fruit before departing.

Hearing about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s past, a trace of pity flickered in Yun Zhi’s eyes, but it was concealed well. “So you’re saying that Junior Brother Li is the Epoch Immortal’s reincarnation?” She nodded her head before continuing. “What about the Gray Immortal Fairy’s transformation? Why does she differ from the original Immortal Fairy’s nature, and why did she destroy the Ember Legacy Dynasty?”

Lu Yang analyzed, “From Senior Heaven Mandate Immortal’s account, the more Hui Doudou killed, the stronger she became, to the point where none of the Four Ancient Immortals could defeat her individually.”

“Little Junior Brother, so you also believe that the gray immortal fairy grows stronger with each kill, which is a trait of the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit?”

Lu Yang shook his head. “I don’t know whether it’s a trait of the Silent Annihilation Dao Fruit, but her power doesn’t increase simply from killing more people. If that were the case, in the three hundred thousand years after the Ember Legacy Dynasty’s fall, she would have long taken action to destroy the world.

“From her attempts to kill Senior Ao Ling and me, I’m more inclined to believe that she only intends to slay those in the know—those aware of her existence. And since those from the Ember Legacy Dynasty all know of her, she became more powerful the more she killed there.”

Yun Zhi was pleased with Lu Yang’s analysis, unswayed by surface information. “Not bad. It aligns with my thoughts.”

Lu Yang added, “However, why is she so thirsty for power, and why does her personality differ from the ice-cold Immortal Fairy? I suspect that this is related to faith power.”

“Why don’t you elaborate?”

“Although my understanding of faith power is limited, certain clues can be gleaned from the matter of the East Sea’s Penglai Island Lord.

“Faith power is a double-edged sword; it can allow one to grow stronger but also control one’s mind.

“Hui Doudou’s immortal body was formed from accumulated faith power, which definitely included the faith of the Four Ancient Immortals. Perhaps even the Four Ancient Immortals themselves were unaware that their thoughts contained not only the desire to revive the Everlasting Immortal Fairy but also the hope that she would join them in slaying the murderer once she was resurrected.”

Even if the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is resurrected, it would still be a life-and-death enmity—a grudge that must be avenged!

“Therefore, Hui Doudou was influenced by these thoughts, and her already ice-cold personality underwent further transformation, driving her to be unscrupulous in pursuing power.”

Yun Zhi replied, “It’s more or less similar to what I thought. However, there’s another possibility you’ve overlooked, Little Junior Brother.”

“What is it?”

“The desire for strength within the faith power might not have originated from the Four Ancient Immortals—it could have also stemmed from that murderer.”

Lu Yang was taken aback. That’s right! How could I have forgotten? In these hundred thousand years, did the murderer simply stand by and watch as the Four Ancient Immortals tried to revive the Everlasting Immortal Fairy? Surely, they must have acted.

“Alright, that’s enough discussion for now. Little Junior Brother, don’t forget you’re still in the midst of a tribulation; there’s one last part to wrap up.” Yun Zhi rose and recalled the three monarch chairs.

Only with Yun Zhi’s reminder did Lu Yang remember that his tribulation was not yet over.

The most crucial aspect of tribulations—the tempering transformation—hasn’t begun yet!

“Has Senior Brother Lu Yang’s Heart Devil Tribulation not yet concluded?” Tao Yaoye watched Lu Yang’s suspended figure from a distance, filled with concern.

Sure enough, Lu Yang opened his eyes as he hovered above Heaven’s Gate Peak. His entire bearing had transformed.

The energy of the Supreme Heaven-Splitting Golden Palace Divine Lightning still lingered within him. Previously, it was suppressed, but now, he would harness it to temper his body.

Releasing the restraint, Lu Yang let the divine lightning’s energy course through him, strengthening every muscle fiber and every meridian.

Unlike the pain from undergoing the tribulation, the tempering process was numbing and tingling, fairly comfortable. Every pore strained to absorb spirit qi from the outside world, converting it to spirit energy within the body.

Spirit energy reserves, mental power, mental space, meridian resilience...his entire being was renewed. It was a complete metamorphosis.

The divine lightning’s tempering effect was unexpectedly sublime. This was a lightning tribulation more powerful than the top-ranked Three Pure Ones Lightning Tribulation. No Divine Transfiguration cultivator had ever undergone tempering by divine lightning at such a level.

Lu Yang gazed inward at his dantian, observing his nascent soul crack and gradually disintegrate, releasing purer and more potent energy. A new energy form began to coalesce, ultimately turning into a primordial soul the same size as Lu Yang.

Tempered by divine lightning, the nascent soul had transformed into a primordial soul.

Lu Yang had successfully advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage!

Chapter 892: Changes at the Divine Transfiguration Stage

“Finally, I’ve advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage.” Lu Yang let out a long breath.

The leap from the Nascent Soul stage to the Divine Transfiguration Stage brought a world of change. One’s status and strength became vastly different from before.

Many Nascent Soul cultivators halted their journey before the lightning tribulation, unable to advance further.

In the eyes of the higher-ups, Golden Core and Nascent Soul cultivators were talents who had yet to mature. Only by surviving myriad sufferings to reach the Divine Transfiguration Stage could one be considered a full-fledged genius.

Upon reaching this stage, major factions would begin instructing disciples in managing the sect, navigating between other factions, and establishing diplomatic relations...

Wait, why does it feel like I’ve already begun managing the sect back at the Foundation Establishment Stage?

Although my status remains unchanged, my strength has grown tangibly.

At the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage, my combat prowess rivals that of Basic Fusion cultivators, leapfrogging the Void Refinement Stage!

Challenging across levels and skipping two major realms—what a terrifying concept!

For example, Senior Brother Dai Bufan is at the Basic Fusion Stage...oh, he has broken through; I can’t beat him.

For example, Senior Brother Ji Hongwen is at the Basic Fusion Stage... I can’t seem to beat him either.

At the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage, my combat prowess rivals that of Basic Fusion cultivators outside the sect, provided they don’t employ the power of rules!

In a first-class sect, I’d even qualify as an elder.

“Congratulations, Junior Brother Lu Yang.”

As the tribulation clouds around Heaven’s Gate Peak dispersed, the other disciples rushed over to offer their congratulations.

Lu Yang had undergone two lightning tribulations in succession, a unique feat in the cultivation world’s three hundred thousand years of history, an achievement worthy of being recorded in historical annals. His reputation certainly surpassed even the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord, who was once famous in the early Great Yu era.

“Junior Brother Lu Yang, the first lightning tribulation you faced was unprecedented. Have you thought of a name for it?”

When a cultivator encountered an unknown lightning tribulation, they had absolute priority in naming it.

Just like the first person who called their physique the “Single’s Spirit Root,” though the naming sense was questionable, it became the official designation, with names like “Pure Yang Spirit Root” being mere aliases or common names.

Without a second thought, Lu Yang blurted out the name that the Heaven Mandate Immortal had given to the divine lightning long ago. “Of course, it shall be called the Supreme...”

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy tugged at Lu Yang’s sleeve and tilted her head upward, her limpid eyes fixed upon him. “Xiao Yangzi, can we call it the Unbeatable Divine Lightning? Pretty please?”

When had the Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at him in this manner? His heart softened instantly, and he gave in to her wish.

“Of course, it shall be called the Unbeatable Divine Lightning.”

The crowd of disciples exchanged odd glances. Junior Brother Lu’s naming sense is truly...something.

“Junior Brother Lu’s naming sense is truly unique.”

“No wonder he could achieve what he has today; his thinking truly differs from that of normal people.”

“Yay! It's called the Unbeatable Divine Lightning!” Mission accomplished, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy let go of Lu Yang's sleeve and punched her small fists in the air, hopping about to celebrate.

Lu Yang finally realized the folly he had just committed, clutching his head in agony. Why did I lose my mind and listen to the Immortal Fairy's nonsense just now?

“Xuanyuan Sword Master, you're not bad. I shall soon catch up to you.” Gu Junye’s gaze burned intensely, not looking at Lu Yang but at his past life—the Sword Dao paragon who lived for the sword and achieved the pinnacle in swords.

“Congratulations, Senior Brother Lu Yang.” Tao Yaoye, Man Gu, and Li Haoran offered their congratulations.

Their cultivation progress lagged only slightly behind Lu Yang's and would soon face their tribulations. Seeing Lu Yang successfully undergo the tribulation and his heroic demeanor, they felt emboldened, eager to face their tribulations and match his stride.

Now, the way Lu Yang looked at Li Haoran had completely changed.

Damn, the reincarnation of the Epoch Immortal! I defeated Li Haoran at the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage. This is roughly equivalent to defeating the Epoch Immortal. What a monumental feat!

At this thought, Lu Yang's grin stretched from ear to ear.

After seeing off the other disciples wishing him well, Lu Yang finally looked inward to assess the gains from this breakthrough.

The most obvious change was his mental space; it had expanded tenfold.

Previously, the mental space could let the Everlasting Immortal Fairy build one Grand Brilliance Hall, but now, it could accommodate ten. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy could begin constructing the Great Dou Dynasty’s imperial palace here, adding places such as the Imperial Study, the Mental Cultivation Hall, and the Purple Heaven Palace.

However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy currently had no such plans; vast expanses of the mental space remained empty, devoid of structures.

Next was the primordial soul that had evolved from the nascent soul. If the primordial soul left the body, it would be as tall as Lu Yang, capable of prolonged, distant separation for reconnaissance, surveillance, or missions—essentially a clone.

Other Divine Transfiguration cultivators’ primordial souls couldn't achieve such cloning effects. Only Lu Yang, whose Unbeatable Nascent Soul had repeatedly hit him, was able to do so after it evolved into a primordial soul.

Like the nascent soul, the primordial soul obeyed Lu Yang's commands. He didn't have to keep enduring beatings and could choose to defeat it only at the Advanced Divine Transfiguration Stage.

Lu Yang scrutinized his primordial soul carefully, then his heart skipped a beat.

“Wait, I remember the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was ninety percent similar to me. Why does it resemble me less now?!”

Logically, the primordial soul should look identical to the cultivator. The Unbeatable Nascent Soul had been ninety percent similar to him, but now, it was only around eighty percent similar.

Reclining in the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy yawned, finding Lu Yang's question silly. “Isn't that perfectly normal? Back when I borrowed your body in the imperial city, I helped you cultivate.”

Lu Yang pressed a hand to his forehead. That's right, why had I forgotten that?

“Immortal Fairy, how about you don't help me cultivate anymore?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was very considerate of Lu Yang. “That won't do. I'm occupying your body for my own use, so how could I let you fall behind in your cultivation?”

Immortal Fairy, can you direct your goodwill somewhere more appropriate?

Lu Yang continued examining himself. He realized his will seemed capable of influencing external spirit qi.

“Is this what texts describe as ‘Divine Transfiguration cultivators can preliminarily commune with heaven and earth and manipulate spirit qi?’”

Fusion cultivators’ ability to employ rules evolved from the Divine Transfiguration Stage’s foundation of communing with heaven and earth.

When two Divine Transfiguration cultivators battled, they competed not only in combat power but also in their degree of communion with heaven and earth.

Additionally, his dantian had transformed into a spirit energy pool to store vast amounts of spirit energy. He no longer needed to consume pills or absorb ambient spirit qi mid-battle like he did during the Nascent Soul Stage.

“What a fragrant scent.” Lu Yang's nostrils flared, catching a familiar aroma.

“Come, Little Junior Brother, try some freshly ripened Immortal peaches.” Yun Zhi carried a basket of immortal peaches and placed it before Lu Yang.

Immortal peaches also had the function of stabilizing one's cultivation realm, perfect for consumption right after a breakthrough.

“Big Senior Sister, you've found that World Natural Spiritual Root?” Lu Yang was surprised. He thought he wouldn't get to eat a second immortal peach in this lifetime.

Yun Zhi shook her head. “No, I didn't find it. I planted the pit of the immortal peach from last time, and it just ripened.” freewebnovel.com

This time, it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s turn to be puzzled. “Ah? That works? Why do I remember that the pits from the World Natural Spiritual Root yield normal peaches?”

“I naturally have my methods,” Yun Zhi said calmly.

“Really?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remained skeptical.

“Senior Immortal Fairy.”

“What is it?”

“Say more, and there'll be no peaches for you.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy immediately took over Lu Yang’s body. “Xiao Yangzi, leave some for me.”

Chapter 893: Good Things Must Be Shared

The immortal peach was a rare immortal item that both Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy found delectable. One could imagine just how exquisite its flavor must have been.

Despite Lu Yang suffering from having his body taken over by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Yun Zhi remained unmoved, even revealing a sliver of a smile—a terrifying scene indeed.

“Immortal Fairy, don’t eat them all! I still want to let Junior Sister Tao and the others have a taste.” With a whole basket of immortal peaches before him, it didn’t sit right with Lu Yang to hog them all himself.

“I have no intention of eating them all. I’m just tasting one to recall the flavor.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wiped her mouth clean and returned control of Lu Yang’s body to him.

“Big Senior Sister, can I share these immortal peaches with others?”

Yun Zhi readily agreed. “These immortal peaches are all yours. It’s your choice to eat them yourself or share them.”

It’s good that Little Junior Brother is willing to share. These immortal peaches were harvested from my secret domain. If he wants to eat more, I can simply pluck more.

She reminded him, “After stabilizing your cultivation realm, don’t forget to continue writing the cultivation manual.”

Lu Yang’s face turned bitter immediately. The joy of breaking through and eating peaches vanished instantly.

The thought of writing the continuation of his cultivation technique gave him a headache. It’s so difficult. Who knows how many days I’d have to stay in the scripture library this time?

“Third Senior Sister, I have something good for you.” Lu Yang first looked for Gan Tian, who also resided on Heaven’s Gate Peak.

As always, Gan Tian had her eyes covered with a black cloth. She sat by the stream and played the qin as if she had melded with nature. She was comprehending the state of unity between heaven and humans.

“What a fragrant peach scent.” Even from a distance, Gan Tian caught the aroma of an immortal peach. She had eaten many exotic fruits in the Demon Region, but none compared to this.

“It’s said to be a product of the World Natural Spiritual Root; this is a true immortal fruit.”

Gan Tian was somewhat embarrassed. “Little Junior Brother, you’ve just broken through, and I haven’t even prepared a congratulatory gift as your senior sister. Instead, you’re the one bringing me a present.

“How about this? Let me play the piece Spring Snow[1] for you to aid your communion with heaven and earth.”

“Then thank you in advance, Senior Sister.”

Gan Tian’s delicate fingers lightly brushed across the strings. A faint, subtle fragrance seemed to permeate the air, and even the surrounding birdsong fell silent. As she played, the melody of Spring Snow flowed forth slowly. The qin’s notes were crisp and mellifluous, like a clear mountain spring babbling, yet also like a spring breeze caressing the face, warm and gentle.

Lu Yang closed his eyes. His perception spread outward, sensing the rustling in the mountain forest and the changes in nature. After his breakthrough to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, his communion with heaven and earth had felt hazy and indistinct. Now, with the help of the qin music, he tangibly experienced this feeling of controlling his surroundings, elevating his soul as a whole.

“Oh, right, qin cultivation has this effect. I’ll have Zhu Tian play a piece for you sometime.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy recalled Zhu Tian, who was proficient in all forms of music.

“Where did this immortal peach come from?” Gan Tian asked, holding the fruit.

“Big Senior Sister said she planted it.”

Gan Tian pondered. Big Senior Sister planted it?

I remember Big Senior Sister mentioning that the secret domain she inhabited was filled with peach blossoms and peaches. Is there some connection?

Lu Yang walked to the deepest part of the Great Mission Hall with familiarity, without anyone stopping him. Dai Bufan had said that Lu Yang could find him anytime.

“Senior Brother Dai, are you busy?” Lu Yang knocked and entered.

Dai Bufan involuntarily shuddered at the sight of Lu Yang.

He had witnessed the entire process of Lu Yang’s breakthrough and had just returned from Heaven’s Gate Peak, but seeing Lu Yang in his own room always gave him an ominous feeling, as if the next moment, Lu Yang could recount some “good deeds” he had done in the outside world.

From Transcendent Tribulation cultivators to immortals—there have been precedents for this. Although he hasn’t gone out this time, it doesn’t mean that everything is fine.

Dai Bufan eyed Lu Yang warily. “You’re not here to tell me you encountered an immortal during your heavenly tribulation, are you?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Senior Brother Dai, did you gain the power of clairvoyance after breaking through to the Intermediate Fusion Stage?

Lu Yang chuckled nervously and produced an immortal peach from behind. “Senior Brother Dai, you jest. How could I cause trouble every time? I just felt that it hasn’t been easy for you to manage the Great Mission Hall, and I happen to have something good, so I brought it for you to have a taste.”

“So this is that legendary immortal peach that is said to extend lifespan?” This information had been mentioned in the intelligence gathered from the imperial city.

“Yes.”

Although Dai Bufan felt awkward about accepting his junior brother’s gift, he still took the immortal peach after some consideration. “If you need any intelligence in the future, feel free to ask me.”

After Lu Yang left, Dai Bufan examined the peach for a moment, then left the Great Mission Hall for an ancient tomb hidden in the cliffs deep within the Dao-Seeking Sect.

He walked to the main chamber, where a jet-black coffin rested, and before the coffin was an empty plate.

Dai Bufan placed the peach on it, lit three incense sticks, bowed three times to the coffin, and inserted them into a small incense burner.

“Shifu, remember to eat this when you’re awake.”

This was the First Elder’s seclusion spot. Lu Yang had come here when he first learned Close Horizon From Cliff.

~~~

After giving Man Gu an immortal peach, Lu Yang went to Spotless Peak to see Tao Yaoye.

Tao Yaoye held the immortal peach, unable to put it down. My surname is Tao[2], and Senior Brother Lu Yang has given me this precious immortal peach. Is this some kind of hint?

“Junior Sister Tao, the immortal peach has the effect of stabilizing one’s cultivation realm. If possible, I suggest you wait until you break through to the Divine Transfiguration Stage before eating it.”

Tao Yaoye nodded repeatedly.

Lu Yang sighed inwardly. Among all the female cultivators I know, only Junior Sister Tao is this obedient. Look at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Big Senior Sister—does it look like I have any say with them?

~~~

For the last immortal peach, Lu Yang decided to give it to Li Haoran.

“Old Meng is training under an immortal; he must be living like a deity and have no shortage of natural treasures to feast on. He won’t miss this small bite.”

“For me?” Li Haoran was deeply moved. I didn’t expect Senior Brother Lu Yang to remember me when encountering such good things. I thought he only seeks me out when he needs a sparring partner.

Lu Yang plastered on a solemn expression. “Junior Brother Li, I am now a Divine Transfiguration cultivator. How could I forget you when I have something good?”

Li Haoran was silent.

You purely wanted to show off that you’ve reached the Divine Transfiguration Stage, don’t you?

“When you smell the immortal peach, do you feel a sense of familiarity?” Lu Yang attempted to awaken Li Haoran’s incarnation from his first lifetime.

The Five Ancient Immortals often ate immortal peaches, especially the Epoch Immortal and the other three. After tasting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s cooking, the immortal peaches would surely seem like the finest delicacy, leaving a deep impression.

If I can awaken his first life, it will be a great boon to understanding the late Ember Legacy era and Li Haoran himself.

“A sense of familiarity?” Li Haoran was baffled by Lu Yang’s question. “Senior Brother Lu, are you saying that Qin Haoran had eaten an immortal peach? How is that possible? If he could obtain one, he wouldn’t have resorted to borrowing money.”

Something that can extend lifespan without restriction. Even at an auction for Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, this would have been a highly coveted highlight item.

Lu Yang felt a bit discouraged. True, even now, Junior Brother Li hasn’t fully absorbed Qin Haoran’s memories, let alone those from his first life. Even if the Everlasting Immortal Fairy herself is standing right in front of him, he probably still wouldn’t be able to remember the memories from his first life.

Chapter 894: The Primordial Soul’s Usage

After attempting to awaken Li Haoran’s memories from his first life to no avail and repeatedly flaunting the good news of his advancement to the Divine Transfiguration Stage, Lu Yang headed to the scripture library in satisfaction.

On the other hand, Li Haoran hefted his hammer and pounded away at myriad metals with fierce clangs, determined to catch up to Lu Yang’s cultivation progress as quickly as possible, lest he come boasting about his achievements again.

~~~

Not long ago, Lu Yang had visited the scripture library to study various knowledge related to lightning tribulations as preparation. Unfortunately, though he had learned a great deal, none of it proved useful during the actual tribulation.

As usual, Lu Yang leafed through cultivation manuals, hoping to glean inspiration from other cultivation techniques to incorporate into his own.

Most Divine Transfiguration cultivators had two main points of focus. The first was to maximize the primordial spirit’s capabilities, such as out-of-body projection and combat.

This was of little use to Lu Yang. His primordial soul was virtually indistinguishable from his real self and highly adaptable; there was no need for deliberate cultivation in this area.

The other major focus was on effectively communing with heaven and earth. This was an area Lu Yang hadn’t previously explored, yet essential for every Divine Transfiguration cultivator.

The smoother one’s communion with heaven and earth, the easier future advancements to the Void Refinement and the Fusion stages would be, and establishing rules later on would also be simpler.

Common methods included increasing contact with nature, whether it was by immersing oneself in mountains far from clamor or wandering amidst the bustling, mundane realm. Mere seclusion would not work.

Lu Yang clutched a stack of cultivation manuals. These were carefully selected Divine Transfiguration-level cultivation techniques that could aid him in writing the continuation of his own.

“No matter what, I mustn’t let Big Senior Sister revise it again this time!”

As a full-fledged Divine Transfiguration cultivator, I can’t rely on Big Senior Sister for everything.

Isn’t it just a Divine Transfiguration cultivation technique? Easy peasy!

Divine Transfiguration cultivation techniques were far more abstruse than Nascent Soul ones. Many cultivators who had just advanced to the Divine Transfiguration Stage would spend days deciphering a single volume.

However, Lu Yang was different. From the very beginning of his cultivation, he had studied all kinds of cultivation techniques, forming a personal system for comprehending them. Applying this system to any cultivation technique allowed him to grasp about seventy to eighty percent.

Soon, Lu Yang slumped directly onto the desk, exhausted.

“This won’t do. There are too many cultivation techniques.” Although understanding cultivation techniques wasn’t difficult, the sheer volume of information was immense. After flipping through five manuals, his head spun, and drowsiness set in.

“Why not have your primordial soul help read them?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suggested.

“The primordial soul can do that?” Lu Yang hadn’t seen any text mention such a use for the primordial soul.

“This is the almighty Unbeatable Primordial Soul! How could it be on the same level as common mortals’ primordial souls?” freewebnovel.com

Lu Yang figured it was worth a try. He summoned his primordial soul, which bore roughly eighty percent resemblance to him. “Little Primordial, go find two Divine Transfiguration cultivation manuals for reference.”

Not all cultivation techniques could serve as references. For instance, cultivation techniques of the Single’s Spirit Root lineage were utterly devoid of reference value. He had assigned this task to test the primordial soul’s discernment.

Not long after, the primordial soul returned with an armful of cultivation manuals. Lu Yang inspected them and found that they were all indeed useful to him.

He picked one at random. “Here. Read this through.”

The primordial soul obediently sat down, eyes fixed on the text, concentrating intently, analyzing the content and principles.

By the time the primordial soul returned to Lu Yang’s body, he was astonished to find that he had absorbed all it had learned. The only drawback was that the fatigue had transferred to him as well.

“Well? Impressive, right?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was smug. She had spent over a month researching the applications of the primordial soul, and the more she learned, the more useful she found it.

“Use it while you can,” she kindly reminded him. “When you reach the Fusion Stage, your primordial soul will fuse with you, and it’ll no longer be usable then.”

Back when I was at the Nascent Soul Stage, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul had beaten me up badly. Once I reached the Divine Transfiguration Stage, I got my revenge.

“The primordial soul can assist you in cultivation, studies; there are plenty of uses.”

“It’s indeed impressive.” Lu Yang nodded sincerely. All those beatings at the Nascent Soul Stage weren’t in vain. Finally, I’m reaping the sweet rewards after the bitter hardships.

“Then go help me write the Divine Transfiguration Chapter of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra.” Lu Yang entrusted his primordial soul with a task crucial to his future fate.

Meanwhile, Lu Yang arranged three chairs against the wall. He lay down with his arms behind his head, crossed his legs, half-closed his eyes, and propped his legs up, basking in the scripture library’s peaceful atmosphere, utterly at ease.

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, how did you manage to sever your own Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit back then?” Lu Yang was curious. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy truly was amazing, worthy of being the head of the Five Ancient Immortals.

Previously, the Heaven Mandate Immortal praised this action of hers, even admitting that the four of them couldn’t match her, a testament to how powerful she was. She wasn’t bragging. She was the first of the Five Ancient Immortals and the Ten Ancient Beauties.

“Hmph! Naturally, I split myself into a Transcendent Tribulation body and the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit body, then used the Transcendent Tribulation form to sever the past!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s chin lifted slightly; she, too, found this feat of hers remarkable.

“Tell me, tell me! How did the battle go?” Lu Yang grew excited. As expected of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. She can defeat her Incipient Dao Fruit form even without one herself.

“Basically, I first performed the Play-Dead Technique and then separated the Transcendent Tribulation body. While the Silent Annihilation Incipient Dao Fruit form was feigning death, with a clean and quick kerchak, I got rid of her!”

Lu Yang was speechless. Why is this battle process not quite what I had imagined?

Suddenly, Lu Yang shivered, as if disaster loomed. He snapped his eyes open to find Yun Zhi bent over and looking at him, holding his primordial soul by the scruff.

“Little Junior Brother.”

“Here!” Lu Yang shot up, sitting rigidly, hands on his knees.

“Your primordial soul just came to me, asking me to help write the continuation of your cultivation technique. Care to explain this?” Yun Zhi’s tone was flat, but Lu Yang was familiar with her and could already sense the displeasure beneath.

I’m doomed!

Lu Yang glared at his primordial soul. I told you to write the cultivation technique! Why did you ask others for help?!

“Uh, Big Senior Sister, if I said this was all the primordial soul’s doing and had nothing to do with me, would you believe it?”

Yun Zhi continued staring at him quietly.

Lu Yang had no choice but to honestly confess that he had instructed his primordial soul to study and write the cultivation technique.

“An interesting primordial soul; it can even study cultivation techniques. But remember, Little Junior Brother—the primordial soul assists you in studying cultivation techniques. You are the one in charge.”

“Understood!”

“Also, Senior Fairy Immortal.”

“Here! Lass Yun, are you going to say that I should supervise Xiao Yangzi? Don’t worry, I won't let him misuse his primordial soul,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke with righteous fervor, as if she was ready to punish her kin for the sake of justice.

“No, I was going to say that you should stop helping Little Junior Brother cultivate. If you continue, I’m afraid his primordial soul might change gender.”

Chapter 895: Method to Commune With Heaven and Earth

Truth be told, the moment Yun Zhi laid eyes on the primordial soul, she was startled. The primordial soul bore an eighty percent resemblance to her little junior brother and twenty percent to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Her initial thought was that Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had some sort of liaison, such as a spiritual union or the like.

Then she realized that it was a consequence of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy assisting Lu Yang in his cultivation.

Even so, the sight of the primordial soul gave her a strange feeling. She felt that if the Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued to help Lu Yang cultivate, causing the primordial soul’s features to change further, that peculiar feeling would only intensify.

During the Nascent Soul Stage, it wasn’t a big deal. After all, the Unbeatable Nascent Soul was still small. Aside from Lu Yang himself, no one could discern whom it resembled.

But it wouldn’t do for the primordial soul at the Divine Transfiguration Stage.

Out of this consideration, Yun Zhi spoke up to prevent the Everlasting Immortal Fairy from aiding Lu Yang in cultivation.

Of course, continuing to help him cultivate did also carry the risk of gender transformation.

Compelled by Yun Zhi’s earnest admonition, Lu Yang had no choice but to abandon his vengeful exploitation of his primordial soul and treat it better instead, letting it assist him in studying cultivation techniques.

With Lu Yang and his primordial soul studying simultaneously, the efficiency doubled.

And the exhaustion also doubled.

But with Spirit-Restoration Pills on hand, a mere increase in fatigue was trivial. These were specially formulated Spirit-Restoration Pills, complete with pill patterns and pill clouds—the cream of the crop.

Lu Yang’s contributions to the Dao-Seeking Sect were so immense that his contribution points were practically inexhaustible. He purchased top-grade pills by the jin—extremely extravagant.

Considering the pills’ monotonous flavor could lead to aversion with prolonged use, Lu Yang placed numerous small plates before him, holding bean paste, fermented tofu, chili sauce, chive flower paste... He could have whatever flavor he desired. If his identity jade tablet didn’t contain a particular dip he craved, he would send his primordial soul to the commercial street to buy some—extremely convenient.

When his primordial soul returned, it was stopped at the entrance and refused entry on the grounds of carrying food. Lu Yang went downstairs to find his primordial soul also carrying a handful of barbeque skewers.

This was definitely not part of the instructions.

Needless to say, the Everlasting Creed members must have foisted them upon my primordial soul to curry favor with me.

Lu Yang remained in the scripture library throughout, with only three breaks during the entire period.

Top-grade Spirit-Restoration Pills weren’t omnipotent; prolonged use diminished their efficacy. Lu Yang had to slow his studying pace and sleep on the chairs.

His primordial soul was fortunate enough to rest alongside its master.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, uncharacteristically, didn’t stir up a racket in the mental space, granting Lu Yang a peaceful environment to rest.

A month and a half slipped by. The brilliant principles of Divine Transfiguration cultivation techniques, from ancient times to the present day, had gathered in Lu Yang’s mind, forming what was practically a mobile repository of cultivation techniques.

Lu Yang spent another half a month deconstructing these principles, attempting to align them with the Nascent Soul Chapter of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra.

“Time to write the cultivation technique!”

During these two months, Lu Yang felt as if he was conversing with Divine Transfiguration cultivators across three hundred thousand years, discussing the meaning of cultivation techniques and exploring the purpose of cultivation, allowing him to reap tremendous gains. His entire being was renewed inside and out; even his speech and demeanor had transformed.

Lu Yang flashed a confident smile. Truly, the wisdom of past sages is not to be underestimated; it has provided me with much edification.

His primordial soul laid out brush, ink, paper, and inkstone. It ground the ink and presented the brush to him. With a wolf-hair brush in hand, Lu Yang proceeded to write. His writing seemed to be imbued with the blessings of the divine, as he wrote rapidly.

The insights over two months coalesced and were integrated into the cultivation technique.

“Mission accomplished!” freewebnovel.com

~~~

“Your cultivation technique needs to be completely rewritten,” Yun Zhi said callously.

“Ah?”

Seeing Lu Yang’s shocked expression, Yun Zhi sighed and explained, “Little Junior Brother, studying others’ cultivation techniques and drawing on their strengths is commendable. But you’ve forgotten the unique nature of your Divine Transfiguration Stage.”

“Unique nature? My primordial soul?”

“Correct. The most crucial aspect of a Divine Transfiguration cultivation technique is how it enables you to commune with heaven and earth. Your cultivation technique includes worldly experience, comprehending life’s myriad forms, playing the qin by streams, and so on. These methods are effective, but you can have better ones.”

“Such as?”

“Do you know that on the brink of death, a cultivator’s perception expands infinitely? Even mortals in their final moments can perceive ghosts, spirits, and things they never could while they were alive, let alone cultivators.”

Lu Yang shuddered. “Are you suggesting that I maintain a near-death state?”

Yun Zhi shook her head. “That’s too dangerous. From my observation, when your primordial soul returns to your body, its senses synchronize with yours.”

Lu Yang’s eyes lit up as he grasped what she was getting at. “Big Senior Sister, do you mean having my primordial soul die in my stead?”

“Not die—keep it on the verge of death,” Yun Zhi corrected. There is a distinction between the two.

Lu Yang nodded repeatedly. Pretty much the same.

“Then shall we try?” Lu Yang proposed excitedly. He summoned his primordial soul and ordered it not to flee, no matter what danger it could encounter.

Yun Zhi nodded slightly, signaling Lu Yang to step back, then struck the primordial soul that remained in place with a palm. If it weren’t for Lu Yang’s command, the primordial soul would have long fled.

Before the palm even came close to the primordial soul, it dimmed instantly, as if under massive pressure, becoming utterly feeble.

Noticing this, Yun Zhi ceased her attack and signaled Lu Yang to withdraw his spirit.

With just a fraction more force, Little Junior Brother’s primordial soul would have crumbled.

The moment his primordial soul returned, Lu Yang dropped to his knees and gasped for breath as he received the primordial soul’s sensations.

That palm strike was terrifying. Though he had reached the Divine Transfiguration Stage, when faced with that palm, he was but an ant before a mountain—a gulf too vast for any measure.

Lu Yang’s consciousness grew hazy, and he felt the world spin. His eyes rolled back, and he collapsed, his gaze vacant.

In that moment, his perception expanded infinitely. He could hear spirit energy coursing through his body, sense spirit qi traversing through leaves, feel the solemn majesty of Heaven’s Gate Peak... Even listening to Gan Tian’s qin hadn’t felt this clear.

Lu Yang slowly regained consciousness, realizing this was communing with heaven and earth. With a few more times, his perception of changes in heaven and earth would surely sharpen.

Yun Zhi produced a drop of water from her identity jade tablet and held it in a leaf, feeding it to Lu Yang.

He didn’t know the water’s origin, but his mind cleared considerably after consuming it.

“How do you feel?”

“It works!” Lu Yang grinned.

A near-death state without real danger... how many Divine Transfiguration cultivators would be envious of this?

The only drawback was that it couldn’t be done in succession. His primordial soul was severely wounded and required lengthy recuperation. However, the strong stopped at nothing to grow stronger. Lu Yang felt no sympathy for his primordial soul.

“As long as it works.” Yun Zhi nodded. “You need to include this in your cultivation technique. That way...”

“My cultivation will count as a pass?”

“That way, only sixty percent of your cultivation technique will need revision.”

Lu Yang was speechless.

Isn’t that still considered a fail?

Chapter 896: Learning the Play-Dead Technique

The remaining sixty percent of the cultivation technique would be difficult to revise, not something Lu Yang could grasp with just a few pointers, and explaining it to him in depth would be like pulling a seedling to help it grow faster, hindering his growth. Thus, Yun Zhi felt that it would be simpler to modify it herself.

“Leave the matter of the cultivation technique to me.”

Hearing he wouldn’t have to revise the cultivation technique, Lu Yang secretly heaved a sigh of relief. Having Big Senior Sister around is wonderful; I don’t even have to worry about the cultivation technique.

Wait, didn’t I previously vow to complete the cultivation technique independently without Big Senior Sister’s help?

After a moment of inner conflict, Lu Yang decided that he shouldn’t decline Yun Zhi’s goodwill. I'd better not mention it, lest it strain our relationship as senior sister and junior brother or give outsiders the impression that I plan to strike out on my own.

“Xiao Yangzi, didn’t you say you’d complete the cultivation technique yourself? Why did you hand it to Lass Yun?”

Lu Yang was silent.

“Hmm? Xiao Yangzi, why aren’t you speaking?”

Immortal Fairy, if you keep questioning, you’ll lose a minister and a pillar of the Great Dou Dynasty.

To divert the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s attention, Lu Yang quickly changed the subject. “By the way, Immortal Fairy, can one commune with heaven and earth through the Play-Dead Technique?”

“Of course not. The Play-Dead Technique puts you in a death state. Communing with heaven and earth requires you to be in a near-death state. They’re two completely different things.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes sparkled as she leaned toward Lu Yang. “Xiao Yangzi, are you interested in the Play-Dead Technique? Wanna learn it?

“The Play-Dead Technique is my pride and joy. I guarantee there’s no downside to learning it. Only my trusted confidants are qualified to learn it.

“Look at Little Ling and Lianyi. Though they’re outer disciples, I deeply love them. I made an exception and imparted the technique to them.

“Now look at Bu Yaolian. Though he’s an inner menial disciple, he lacks immortal affinity. I won’t impart it to him!”

Lu Yang had never heard of inner menial disciples before. Does our Everlasting Lineage need menial labor?

He initially wanted to refuse. The Play-Dead Technique doesn’t suit my heroic and dashing sword cultivator image. But faced with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s limpid eyes, he couldn’t bring himself to say no.

“Alright, I’ll learn it.”

“Come, call me ‘teacher,’” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said gleefully. This is Xiao Yangzi’s first time learning a technique from me; I can be considered his teacher now.

If Xiao Yangzi is the Second Dou Emperor, I’ll be considered the Imperial Tutor.

To look the part, she specially changed into a loose, dark Confucian robe and held two books, appearing quite erudite.

Lu Yang’s eye twitched at the sight, but on second thought, he should indeed call her ‘teacher’ since he was learning from her.

Resigned, he cupped his fists in proper student etiquette and respectfully addressed her, “Teacher.”

“You won’t lose out by being my disciple. Back then, I was the Barbarian Tribe's teacher, and everyone respectfully called me ‘Barbarian Teacher.’ As my disciple, you have the same seniority as the Ancient Barbarians. That’s very senior.”

So... I am now not only Man Gu’s senior brother but also his ancestor?

“Teacher, could we learn the Play-Dead Technique after Big Senior Sister finishes revising the cultivation technique?”

Lu Yang felt it was safer with Yun Zhi present.

“Sure.”

Having just become the Imperial Tutor, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was in high spirits and agreed to whatever Lu Yang said.

After about four hours, the Divine Transfiguration Chapter of the Clear Heart True Nature Mantra was handed to Lu Yang.

He carefully pored over it, feeling ashamed. Big Senior Sister’s wording is precise, her sentences concise—far beyond what I’m capable of.

Lu Yang could vaguely discern that Yun Zhi hadn’t written it from scratch but had revised his subpar draft, following his line of thought. She has really gone through much trouble.

Circulating through one macrocosmic loop with the cultivation technique was exceedingly smooth, without the slightest blockage, which meant the cultivation technique suited him perfectly.

“Don’t rush with matters of cultivation techniques, Little Junior Brother. One day, you can write one even without my help.”

“I will work hard!” Lu Yang’s fighting spirit soared. He vowed that he absolutely wouldn’t trouble Yun Zhi with writing the cultivation technique the next time!

“By the way, Big Senior Sister, the Immortal Fairy will be teaching me the Play-Dead Technique in a bit.”

“Play-Dead Technique?” Yun Zhi was also interested in this technique. It had played an integral role in Ao Ling and Jiang Lianyi’s survival. Previously, when Jiang Lianyi challenged her, she had even relied on it to fight to a draw with Yun Zhi. Truly a divine skill.

Soon, Teacher Everlasting began her lesson. Lu Yang sat upright and solemn as the student, while Yun Zhi crossed her legs, sipping tea and listening from the side.

“The Play-Dead Technique is a top-tier art I created, concerning life and death, time and karma. It is quite challenging. Back then, Little Ling and Lianyi struggled significantly to barely grasp it.

“However, with your talent and my guidance, I believe learning it shouldn’t be difficult, Xiao Yangzi.

“The Play-Dead Technique is a heaven-deceiving art. To deceive the heavens, one must first deceive oneself.

“One must harbor a heart to seek death, with the heart like dead ashes. Only by maintaining this state can one fool everyone and sever karma.

“One must also preserve a sliver of vitality. This is the key to coming back from the dead.”

Speaking about familiar topics, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy grew animated, gesturing excitedly. Both Lu Yang and Yun Zhi listened attentively, greatly satisfying her desire to be a teacher and role model.

The only flaw was her flighty mind; sometimes, she would digress to another topic while lecturing.

Fortunately, Lu Yang had known her long enough and gotten used to her way of speaking, easily following her train of thought.

“Well, Xiao Yangzi, have you learned it?”

“I can try.” Lu Yang felt he had grasped about seventy to eighty percent and could give it a shot.

“Jiayou, Xiao Yangzi!”

Lu Yang took two deep breaths, calmed himself, and tuned out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s shouts, focusing solely on immersing himself in the mental state of seeking death. Following her instructions, he circulated the mystic art and silently recited the incantation, concealing a sliver of vitality within his death-seeking heart.

His consciousness grew heavier; he lacked even the strength to open his eyes. Finally, darkness enveloped him, and he lost all sensation.

“Is this considered a success?” Yun Zhi turned to ask the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The creator of the Play-Dead Technique scrutinized Lu Yang’s deathly appearance. “On the surface, it looks genuine. Best to give it a series of tests.”

“For example?”

“For example, when Lianyi executed the Play-Dead Technique, Little Ling woke her by burning her. You could try that.”

Yun Zhi raised her hand, a golden flame appearing in her palm, radiating terrifying heat and a destructive aura. She hesitated whether to scorch her little junior brother.

What if it backfires?

As Yun Zhi deliberated, a figure rushed over to her.

“Big Senior Sister, it’s terrible! Junior Brother Lu is dead!” Dai Bufan held an extinguished soul lamp. An extinguished lamp signified the person’s death. Noticing Lu Yang’s lamp extinguished, he rushed over in panic to consult Yun Zhi.

Then, he saw Lu Yang lying lifelessly on the ground, with Yun Zhi wielding a destructive golden flame, about to incinerate him.

“Big Senior Sister, you...” Dai Bufan gulped.

Have I stumbled upon a murder scene?

He quietly backed away, ready to flee.

Yun Zhi hesitated for a bit, then explained, “If I say that Little Junior Brother committed suicide, would you believe me?”

Dai Bufan had no idea what to say. Why don't you guess whether I'll believe that?

Chapter 897: Coming Back From the Dead

How could Big Senior Sister’s words be false?

“Of course, I believe that Junior Brother Lu committed suicide,” Dai Bufan said with a forced smile, his legs trembling. He had never felt this close to death.

No matter how I see it, this looks like Big Senior Sister had accidentally beaten Junior Brother Lu to death and is about to destroy the corpse and dispose of the evidence. Yet I blindly came right over to check on him.

Have I lived long enough? I can’t even protect myself now!

This immortal peach really isn’t so easy to accept. First, I owe Junior Brother Lu a favor, and now I have to repay him with my life. Is this what they call karmic inevitability?

“In that case, please continue with your business, Big Senior Sister. Call me if you need anything.”

Dai Bufan quietly retreated. Seizing a moment when Yun Zhi wasn’t paying attention, he turned on his heels and flew outward desperately, not daring to look back.

“Wait, come back.”

How could Yun Zhi let Dai Bufan flee? If I don’t clarify it now, it would be impossible afterward.

With a mere thought, Yun Zhi pulled him back, even retracing his exact path.

“Big Senior Sister, please spare my life! I really didn’t see anything!” Sensing the situation turn dire, Dai Bufan immediately knelt and begged for mercy.

Yun Zhi pressed her forehead helplessly. “Little Junior Brother isn’t really dead. He’s in a play-dead state. He just feigned his death so well that it fooled the soul lamp.”

Dai Bufan had never heard of such a technique, but like a fish with a knife at its throat, he believed whatever Yun Zhi said.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had detected Dai Bufan’s arrival early on. Understanding that outsiders mustn’t know of her, she had immediately hidden herself.

Originally, Yun Zhi would have detected him too, but she had been preoccupied with deliberating over whether to scorch her little junior brother.

Had I known that Junior Brother Dai would come over, I would have hidden Little Junior Brother Lu’s body properly... though why does something still feel amiss?

Yun Zhi was perplexed. No matter how I handle this, it still seems wrong.

As Yun Zhi approached Lu Yang with the golden flame, before the fire touched him, Lu Yang sprang up with a shot, his corpse coming back to life on the spot.

The soul lamp in Dai Bufan’s hand reignited.

“You were really playing dead?!” Dai Bufan was flabbergasted. He hadn’t imagined such a miraculous technique existed, deceiving even a soul lamp. Is it a lost ancient art or an art created by Big Senior Sister?

He secretly exhaled a sigh of relief. It seems I won’t die after all.

“Junior Brother Lu, are you alright?”

Lu Yang winced in pain. He had been sleeping like he was dead when his soul suddenly felt scorched, jolting him awake.

After waking up, that burning sensation vanished.

“I’m...I’m fine. Senior Brother Dai, what are you doing here?”

Dai Bufan replied inwardly, I came to be buried with you. “Are you sure? Why don’t you check your current condition?” He scrutinized Lu Yang, an odd expression on his visage.

“What condition?” Lu Yang was baffled. He looked down and saw his own body lying peacefully on the ground, while he was a soul in an out-of-body state!

If Dai Bufan weren’t around, Lu Yang would have asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy what was going on.

“Minor issue. I’m truly fine.” Lu Yang waved dismissively, indicating everything was under control.

Since Lu Yang appeared alright, Dai Bufan departed, though still suspicious.

After Dai Bufan left, Lu Yang leaned backward, trying to merge with his body.

Unfortunately, he failed. Standing up, his soul remained in an out-of-body state.

“Immortal Fairy, how about you come out and explain what’s happening?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emerged from behind a large tree, praising Lu Yang’s talent. “Xiao Yangzi, you’ve grasped the fundamentals!”

Lu Yang pointed at his soul, then at the corpse on the ground. “Are you sure this counts as grasping the fundamentals?”

“Of course! What is the Play-Dead Technique? It’s a heaven-deceiving art. To deceive heaven and earth, one must first deceive oneself.

“Your physical body is now in that deceived state. It’s become a corpse! If you don’t believe me, have Lass Yun use a Corpse-Driving Technique on it. I guarantee she can manipulate your corpse.”

Lu Yang dared not say he didn’t believe her.

“In your current state, you could even fool insurance companies and make a fortune. Therefore, this isn’t called an ‘out-of-body state;' it’s more accurate to call you a ‘lone wandering ghost,’" the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said, correcting his terminology.

“Your learning pace is much faster than Little Ling and Lianyi’s. When they first learned it, it shouldn’t have been called the ‘Play-Dead Technique’ but the ‘Play-Sleep Technique.’ They forcibly pretended to be dead even without knowing how. As if I couldn’t tell they were just pretending to be asleep.”

Observing from the side, Yun Zhi nodded slightly. “So that’s how it is. Playing dead fooled the soul lamp, Dai Bufan, and even your own body. It seems you can deceive Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, Little Junior Brother.”

Yun Zhi could discern a faint spark of vitality in Lu Yang’s soul when he performed the Play-Dead Technique. This level of vitality was one even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators couldn’t notice.

“Immortal Fairy, save the praise. First, tell me how to return to normal,” Lu Yang said calmly, unswayed by her compliments.

“Simple. Just take over the body.”

“Take over the body?”

Lu Yang was about to ask whose body he should take over when he looked down and saw his body peacefully lying on the ground.

“Take over your body, of course.” Circling Lu Yang’s corpse, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy spoke enthusiastically, like a salesperson pitching unsold goods. “Look how perfectly your soul matches your body—it’s totally a match made in heaven. Taking over your body will not result in any rejection!”

Lu Yang. "..."

Immortal Fairy, I admit you have a point, but could you please stop talking?

Although Lu Yang had never systematically studied how to take over a body, as a frequent victim of having his body taken over by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he picked it up easily.

Circulating the mystic art, he merged with his body, successfully taking over his own body.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy planted her hands on her hips proudly. “Hmph, now you know why I'm so skilled at taking over your body, right? I perfected it while developing the Play-Dead Technique back then!”

Lu Yang wasn’t exactly sure what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was proud of.

“Is this how the Play-Dead Technique is executed?” Yun Zhi murmured. Attempting to circulate the mystic art, she sat on the monarch chair, utterly devoid of vitality.

Just then, a spatial gate opened. The Vast Sea Daoist Lord rushed in with a soul lamp in his hand, urgently checking on the situation.

“Did something happen to Yun Zhi?”

The moment he arrived, he saw Yun Zhi seated on the throne lifelessly, with not a trace of vitality in her.

Seeing this, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord heaved a sigh of relief. “So she’s playing dead.”

Beside him, Lu Yang was bewildered. “Founding Ancestor, you know the Play-Dead Technique too?”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord was befuddled. “What Play-Dead Technique?”

“Then why did you say she was playing dead?”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord rolled his eyes. “There isn’t a single wound on her, no signs of battle, and it doesn’t look like something went awry during her cultivation. If she’s not playing dead, am I supposed to believe you killed her, kid?”

Chapter 898: Invitation From Sword Tower

To be frank, when the Vast Sea Daoist Lord discovered that Yun Zhi’s soul lamp had been extinguished, his entire body trembled in fear.

If even Yun Zhi had perished, just what level could this enemy be at?

Fortunately, upon rushing over, he realized that Yun Zhi was only playing dead.

“Thank goodness she’s just playing dead.”

Lu Yang also felt that the Vast Sea Daoist Lord’s reasoning made sense. An enemy capable of silently eliminating Big Senior Sister would be an existence beyond imagination.

Wait, silently eliminating Big Senior Sister... why does this sound so familiar?

He hurriedly asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hiding in his mental space. “Immortal Fairy, could you have used the Play-Dead Technique back then and then been ambushed?”

“Impossible. I had already mastered the Play-Dead Technique with major success by then. Why would I use it for no reason?

“Besides, I can’t remember what happened during that period; my mind was foggy. Something else must have occurred. It had nothing to do with the Play-Dead Technique.”

Lu Yang ruminated. True. The Play-Dead Technique has no amnesia side effects.

“Do you know how to let her break free from this play-dead state?” Although he knew Yun Zhi was only feigning death, the Vast Sea Daoist Lord still felt anxious at the sight of her corpse.

“Based on my play-dead experience, we just have to attack her. Once she senses a threat, she’ll wake up.”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord fell silent for a moment, finding it extremely difficult.

He glanced around—only Lu Yang was present.

Comparatively speaking, taking action myself seems more feasible.

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord gritted his teeth. “I’ll try!”

On his chest, a vaguely visible fruit appeared, shaped like an apple but indistinguishable in color. He furiously activated his Space Incipient Dao Fruit.

Boundless spatial power gathered in his arm, seeming capable of tearing heaven and earth apart. The entire space grew unstable. Standing nearby, just a glance made Lu Yang feel as if he were about to be riven apart.

Seated serenely on the monarch chair, Yun Zhi slowly opened her eyes and turned to look at the Vast Sea Daoist Lord.

“Truly awake?” The Vast Sea Daoist Lord excitedly dispersed the spatial force in his hand.

My strongest attack had actually threatened Yun Zhi? Have I unknowingly become this powerful?!

“Big Senior Sister, how do you feel?” Lu Yang rushed forward to ask.

Yun Zhi hesitated for a moment. “I felt my clothing was about to be damaged, so I woke up. Little Junior Brother, do you know what happened?”

The Vast Sea Daoist Lord had no idea what to say. He coughed dryly twice, warning Lu Yang with his eyes not to speak of what had just transpired, then opened a spatial gate and fled.

Another half a month passed.

Lu Yang continued cultivating assiduously without slacking off the slightest.

“Little Junior Brother, there’s a letter for you.” Lu Yang looked up to see that Gan Tian was looking for him.

“A letter?”

“Mmm. When I descended the mountain, I bumped into a junior brother. He was heading to Heaven’s Gate Peak to find you, saying that the Sword Tower had sent a letter. Since it was on my way, I brought it.”

“A letter from the Sword Tower?” Lu Yang was curious. I seem to have no connection with the Sword Tower, though Shifu’s generation had many interactions with them.

The front of the envelope was drawn with a sword piercing the sky—the Sword Tower’s insignia. Every Sword Tower disciple had this pattern embroidered on their chest. Apparently, it was personally designed by the Sword Tower Supreme Lord.

“Let me see. The letter says that the Sword Tower is hosting the centennial Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony, inviting all sword cultivators in the world to attend.”

“So it’s the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony. It’s indeed held around this time.”

The Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony showcased the Sword Tower’s status in the Sword Dao. At that time, sword cultivators from Great Xia, the East Sea, the Demon Region, and the Buddhist Kingdom would all attend, making it a lively and grand occasion. In the hearts of every sword cultivator, attending this ceremony at least once in a lifetime was a must; it was the glory of being a sword cultivator.

“Perfect timing. My Mingyue Sword is barely keeping up with my cultivation. A trip to the Sword Tower would be good; they should sell swords there, too.”

The Mingyue Sword was forged using the Qilin Immortal’s sword array, supposedly at the immortal level. But unless the Qilin Immortal’s mind had been addled by the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s beating, they wouldn’t have used immortal gold. The sword array’s material was ordinary. Now that Lu Yang’s cultivation was exceptional, brandishing the Mingyue Sword with full force would likely snap it.

Although he could ask Yun Zhi to help find him a sword, Lu Yang was a man of character; he couldn’t rely on her for everything.

Lu Yang could also gather materials and ask Li Haoran to forge a sharp sword. However, considering that he constantly flaunted his cultivation before Li Haoran, asking for a favor now would be somewhat awkward.

“Then I shall go and witness sword cultivators from across the world,” Lu Yang said cheerfully.

Cultivating in the sect all this time has been so boring. At last, I have an excuse to go out.

With a month remaining until the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony, there was still plenty of time. The Sword Tower was located in Shu Province, more than halfway across Great Xia from the Dao-Seeking Sect. Flying there would take half a month; setting out now would be a bit too early.

However, Lu Yang was worried that something unexpected could happen along the way, so he decided that departing early was better.

~~~

Before setting out, Lu Yang sorted out his inventory with practice: Spring Breeze Restoration Pill, Great Rejuvenation Pill, Qingfeng Sword, Seven Stars Sword Set, spirit stones, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy...

“All set, let’s go!”

The Sword Tower was too far from the Dao-Seeking Sect; even a Divine Transfiguration cultivator couldn’t fly there in one go. Lu Yang chose a flying vessel—slower but less trouble and more comfortable.

On the flying vessel, an eldest young miss from some family loudly declared that she fancied Lu Yang’s seat and intended to toss him some spirit stones to purchase it.

Just then, a righteous but inexperienced youth stepped forward in the name of justice, accusing the young lady of being willful and bullying others with her status.

Unable to win the argument, she signaled her bodyguards to teach him a lesson. Unexpectedly, even though the youth’s cultivation was low, his combat prowess was formidable, allowing him to easily defeat the two bodyguards whose cultivation was higher than his.

He even gave the eldest young miss a spanking. Her cheeks flamed red, and she let out embarrassed cries. The way she looked at him changed—no one had ever dared beat her like this in all her life.

Not long after, the flying vessel docked at a major city. The authorities arrested the eldest young miss and her two bodyguards for disorderly conduct and the youth for indecent assault.

Lu Yang also noted the eldest young miss had a marriage engagement. Her trip was to meet her fiancé, who she had never met, and whose family had come down in the world.

The youth also had a marriage engagement. His trip was to meet his fiancée, who he had never met, and whose family had suddenly come into wealth.

An old and a young Daoist priest in tattered robes were also aboard. The old Daoist priest carried a gourd at his waist, swaying as he walked, and reeked of alcohol. It was unclear how long it had been since he last bathed, and his stench mingled with his liquor breath.

The young Daoist priest resembled a child. He repeatedly cried out “Shifu” and hurried to keep pace. Fellow passengers held their noses in disgust, but the old Daoist Priest paid them no mind, completely at ease.

Finally, a passenger couldn’t bear the old Daoist priest’s stench any longer and wanted to upbraid him. No one expected this unassuming Daoist priest to be a mighty Fusion cultivator having fun in the mortal world.

Even more unexpectedly, the passenger was also a mighty Fusion cultivator doing the same. Soon, the two were locked in combat.

Lu Yang sidled up to the young Daoist priest, suggesting that if he considered changing shifu, he could come to the Dao-Seeking Sect, as their members were very hygienic.

After the battle, suspecting that this cabin’s feng shui was poor, Lu Yang decided to pay extra for the luxury cabin.

Not long after, grim news arrived from the luxury cabin—a passenger was murdered in the dead of the night. The other twelve passengers in that cabin could vouch for each other and had alibis. No one knew who the culprit was.

Lu Yang figured that he ought to have avoided changing cabins after all.

Chapter 899: Which Family’s Young Miss Are You?

Upon hearing this, the child seated beside Lu Yang lit up with an intrigued smile. “A murder case? I’ve cracked several difficult cases back in my hometown. I wonder if I can solve this one too.”

Considering that the problem could not just be with this cabin’s feng shui but the entire flying vessel’s, Lu Yang decided to disembark and fly to the Sword Tower instead, treating the remaining fare as money down the drain.

However, during the flight, several unexpected incidents occurred, such as stumbling upon a secret domain that only opened once in a millennium, encountering an aristocratic family’s young miss who was dissatisfied with an arranged marriage and dragged Lu Yang in as a shield, and other miscellaneous matters. The journey that should have been half a month took a full month instead.

Lu Yang arrived at the Sword Tower just in time.

Sensing the dense humidity of Shu Province, Lu Yang couldn’t help but remark, “Good thing I set out early. Otherwise, I might have missed the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony.”

"Is it possible that if you’d set out a day later, you wouldn’t have encountered any of these matters?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t help but ask.

“That makes sense. When the Sword Tower holds the next Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony in a hundred years, I’ll set out a day later.” Lu Yang was meticulous, understanding that experiments required controlled variables—only one condition should be changed at a time.

The Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony was an event of the highest order in the cultivation world, attracting many cultivators from beyond Great Xia. The Shu Province authorities placed great importance on it. If they could leverage this opportunity to persuade some sword cultivators to remain in Shu Province, that would be ideal, for it would be considered a genuine political achievement.

Since flying carriages became popular, many sword cultivators had switched from flying with swords to carriages. After entering Shu Province, Lu Yang saw many flying carriages accompanying him in the air.

Many sword cultivators frequently glanced sideways, even turning back for another look at Lu Yang after passing.

After all, they had never seen anyone fly with a Sword-Cleansing Pond; it was quite the novel sight.

Lu Yang paid no heed to these rude behaviors. The flying carriage patent was in his name. These cultivators have essentially paid me spirit stones, making them customers.

I’ve always maintained a good attitude toward customers, evident since my barbeque shop days.

“Time for hotpot.”

Since I’ve already arrived, there’s no need to rush. I should savor the local cuisine calmly; otherwise, my trip to Shu Province would be wasted.

This was a habit Lu Yang had picked up from Yun Zhi.

Hotpot eateries were ubiquitous in Shu Province, each touting itself as authentic and boasting exquisite flavor, claiming to be a local establishment with a time-honored reputation.

Amidst a hotpot street, the Once More Time Barbeque Shop stood firm, a testament to how delicious the Barbarian Tribe’s recipe combined with the Three Flavor True Fire and the Pure Yang True Fire was, carving out its own path here.

Tripe, yellow beef, filefish, duck blood, fuzhu beancurd sticks...ingredients on small dishes piled high on the table. Lu Yang placed them into the nine-grid (jiugongge) hotpot[1], and a spicy aroma assailed his nostrils.

“Hello, I see you've ordered a lot. Would you be able to finish them all? Could I have some?” A rather casually dressed woman stood before Lu Yang's table, her tone hesitant. She gazed eagerly at the bubbling hotpot.

Looking up, Lu Yang saw an exceptionally beautiful woman speaking to him. Her looks rivaled Tao Yaoye’s, and she had an excellent figure. The only issue was that he didn't know her.

Lu Yang initially wanted to say that he was a cultivator, but his heart softened upon seeing her pitiful expression, and his original words died on his lips.

“Well, sit down and eat then.”

Lu Yang waved to the waiter. “Shopkeer, give us another pair of chopsticks and prepare another bowl of dipping sauce!”

Lu Yang sighed in relief. Good thing Old Meng didn't come; my luck has changed.

“Thank you, thank you.” The peerless woman repeatedly expressed her gratitude.

“Which family’s young miss are you? Did you run away from home and forget to bring money?” Lu Yang asked with a smile.

Although the woman appeared penniless, her clothing was expensive, signifying that she was from a wealthy background, probably a young miss from some noble family who slipped out and forgot her money.

It wasn't Lu Yang's first time encountering someone like this. On previous flying vessels, he had seen young ladies disguised as beggars and smudged with grime. After sneaking aboard, they would get discovered by people from merchant guilds, and some kind-hearted youths would help the young ladies pay their fares.

Realizing that Lu Yang had misunderstood, the woman hurriedly explained, “Forgot to bring money? No, no, I simply forgot that money is needed outside. Where I'm from, we don't use money.”

“Looks like your family has protected you well; you never had to spend money,” Lu Yang teased offhandedly.

“Ready to eat.”

Hearing the food was ready, the woman mimicked Lu Yang's movements. She skilfully picked up a slice of chili-covered yellow beef, dipped it in the sauce, and placed it in her mouth, revealing an expression of bliss.

Lu Yang chuckled. “Come on, you've never eaten this before?”

He admitted that the hotpot in Shu Province was delicious, but not enough to warrant such an exaggerated expression.

The woman blushed at his teasing and smiled sheepishly. “Indeed, I've never eaten anything like this before. I came out just to eat this. Truly delicious.”

The woman genuinely loved the hotpot. Her expression made Lu Yang momentarily wonder whether they were eating the same thing. The passers-by saw a beauty enjoying herself, and they found it a pleasant sight to behold. They involuntarily entered the shop, making the already-packed restaurant even more crowded.

The two wolfed everything down and finished with two bowls of bingfen ice jelly,[2] completely satisfied.

“Waiter, the bill please, and also two pieces of hotpot base.”[3]

“What is a hotpot base? Can you eat it?” the woman asked in puzzlement.

Lu Yang shook his head and smiled. “You can't eat it directly. I'm buying two pieces back for my Big Senior Sister to have a taste.”

Yun Zhi made it a habit to sample local specialities whenever she visited an unfamiliar place, and if circumstances allowed, she would bring some back.

“I’m heading to the Sword Tower in a bit. What are your plans, miss?”

Lu Yang was somewhat worried about the woman. How did her family protect her? And how did she manage to slip out? She looks naive and lacks common sense, yet she's so beautiful. If I leave her here alone, and something happens... The woman pondered. I indeed know little about the outside world, and he seems like a good person, too.

Since I have no urgent matters, I might as well follow him and learn about the outside world.

“Can I follow you?” she asked hesitantly.

“Yes, but once the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony ends, I'll have to send you home.” Lu Yang couldn't possibly let her keep following him.

I already have a silly ornament in my mental space; I can't have another one.

“Then thank you, Fellow Daoist,” the woman said earnestly.

“By the way, we've been chatting for so long, yet I still don't know how I should address you. I'm Lu Yang.” Lu Yang introduced himself. His name now rang far and wide; there wasn't a cultivator who didn't recognize it.

The woman showed none of the surprise or shock he expected, as if she hadn't heard of his name. She smiled sweetly. “So it's Fellow Daoist Lu Yang. I'm Yun Mengmeng.”

“So it's Miss Yun... Wait, what did you say your name was?”
