Chapter 900: You Have the Same Name as a Prominent Figure

“I'm Yun Mengmeng,” she repeated, though she sensed that Lu Yang's reaction to it was rather peculiar, as if he had heard of it somewhere before.

So she really is called Yun Mengmeng?!

Isn't this the alias that Big Senior Sister used when impersonating the Heavenly Court Creed Leader?!

Lu Yang sized up Yun Mengmeng. Quite an interesting name you have here, miss. It coincides with Big Senior Sister's alias.

“Do you know me?” Yun Mengmeng asked hesitantly, feeling that Lu Yang's scrutinizing gaze didn't seem like that of a good person.

“I don't know you, but I've heard this name before; it's the same as a prominent figure’s. If you use this name while traveling, it could likely lead to misunderstandings.”

“Which prominent figure?” Yun Mengmeng wondered, Is my name so common that it coincides with a big shot?

Lu Yang naturally couldn't say that her name matches their creed leader’s alias. My current identity is a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect, not the Young Creed Leader of the Heavenly Court.

“At this hour, there should be storytellers around.” Lu Yang heightened his senses, sifting through the surrounding noise to locate a nearby teahouse with a storyteller.

This was a hotpot street, and adjacent to it were a snack street and an antiques street. Areas like this were full of teahouses.

“Come, I'll take you to listen to some pingshu storytelling. Then you'll understand.”

After several twists and turns, the two arrived at a teahouse. Lu Yang ordered a pot of the finest tea and a table full of pastries, treating Yun Mengmeng to the pingshu performance.

“However, in that battle at Hanshui City, two mighty ancient supreme lords used dreams as their Dao, pulling millions of citizens into a dreamscape and waging a war that could be described as contending with heaven and earth.

“Yet, no one imagined that someone could break into the dream world constructed by the two mighty supreme lords. That person strolled through it leisurely as if in a courtyard, completely ignoring the two supreme lords!

“The moment those two supreme lords saw that figure, they braced themselves as if facing a formidable foe, cold sweat covering their foreheads. In a hoarse voice, they demanded, ‘Who are you?!’

“That person merely glanced at the two supreme lords, and they felt as though they were plunged into an icy abyss, like an outsider from beyond beholding the vast heavens.

“In a tone as unchanging as the ages, that person introduced themselves. ‘Yun Mengmeng, Creed Leader of the Heavenly Court Creed.’”

Gasps rose and fell in the teahouse. Though patrons had heard this tale before, those few words depicting the Heavenly Court Creed Leader Yun Mengmeng’s entrance still conveyed a sense of dominion that spanned eternity.

“Let's now speak of the battle at the East Sea. An immortal emerged from the gray mist, with every gesture displaying the might of heaven and earth, seeking to slay one of the Heavenly Court’s Four Regents—the Dragon Ancient Ancestor.

“Right then, the Heavenly Court Creed Leader appeared, commencing the first immortal battle since ancient times. The two immortals clashed, the commotion alerting the whole cultivation world...

“It was unclear how many exchanges occurred before the immortal from the gray mist was routed. Creed Leader Yun pressed the advantage and gave chase until the two disappeared from heaven and earth...”

Lu Yang offered Yun Mengmeng the last piece of pastry on the plate. “That’s the gist. You share a name with the Heavenly Court Creed Leader.”

Yun Mengmeng listened with rapt attention. We're both called Yun Mengmeng, so why is she so impressive while I'm so useless?

Lu Yang sighed. “I suppose your family never expected that the name they gave you would be the same as that of an ancient, mighty expert.

Yun Mengmeng replied, “Alright, alright, these are trivial matters. I'll follow you to that Sword Tower. Once things are over, I'll take you to seek refuge with my good sister.”

“Good sister?”

Lu Yang thought, I knew this young miss couldn't have just foolishly run away from home without a place to stay.

He noted that Yun Mengmeng’s strength was at the Golden Core Stage, and it wasn't just for show; her cultivation talent was commendable.

Now that he had advanced to the Basic Divine Transfiguration Stage, few cultivators could conceal their cultivation from him, unless they were at the Fusion Stage. But which Fusion cultivator would travel without money and freeload their way through meals?

“Mmm, my good sister is amazing; she's incredibly formidable at fighting, though she's very low-key, so few are aware of her prowess. If she gave you a few pointers, I guarantee you'd benefit immensely.” As she spoke of her good friend, Yun Mengmeng’s expression radiated pride.

“Incredibly formidable at fighting?”

“Absolutely. Where we're from, she's the strongest. No one can beat her.” freewebnovel.com

Lu Yang didn't take her words to heart. No matter how incredible your good sister is, can she compare to Big Senior Sister?

Forget Big Senior Sister, it'd be impressive if she could even surpass me.

~~~

Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng meandered along, eating and drinking, eventually arriving at the Sword Tower.

“Did your family never feed you before?” Lu Yang gave Yun Mengmeng an odd look as she held a shaofen[1] skewer, bought from One More Time Barbeque Shop.

“Of course, they fed me. The food was quite good too, like peaches and whatnot. But after a while, it gets a bit tiring, and the flavors are very mild, not as good as here.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, If you want strong flavors, Shu Province is the right place. If you find even the flavors here mild, I can only ask an immortal to possess me and cook for you.

He vaguely glimpsed a colossal immortal sword piercing the clouds and thrust into the ground, its handle veiled by the clouds, flickering in and out of sight.

On closer inspection, he realized it wasn't a colossal immortal sword but a wooden tower in the shape of a sword.

It was none other than the Sword Tower.

Numerous sword cultivators streamed toward it, and figures rarely seen now gathered in throngs. Here, Lu Yang saw supreme sword cultivators in snow-white robes carrying spirit swords, Buddhist disciples with prayer beads and wisdom swords at their waists, and various fully or partially transformed great demons. Swords weren’t exclusive to humans; many demons also favored them as weapons.

Aside from the Demon Region, the East Sea, and the Buddhist Kingdom, Lu Yang also saw cultivators from the Extreme North.

The Extreme North was frigid and sparsely populated, lacking major factions like Penglai Island. Cultivators there were generally rogue cultivators or relied on simple master-disciple traditions.

Many sword cultivators liked to journey to the frigid land to hone their Sword Dao, hoping to elevate it further. Thus, sword cultivators from the Extreme North were naturally among the strongest.

After circling half the tower, Lu Yang quickly located his destination—the sword shop.

Inside, myriad swords adorned the walls—long, short, broad, narrow—a dazzling assortment. Those displayed here were all excellent swords; even the Sword Tower's disciples had to purchase from this shop.

Yet they still failed to meet Lu Yang’s standards.

“The quality’s lacking.”

The sword he sought must at least withstand force at the Fusion Stage. How could swords displayed outside possess such quality?

“Who said the quality of our shop’s swords is lacking?” A displeased voice came from within. A young man pushed through a curtain, grasping a large iron hammer.

Spotting Lu Yang, the young man froze. “Senior Brother Lu Yang!”

Lu Yang also recognized him. “Junior Brother Mingtai.”

He was Mingtai, a true lineage disciple of the Sword Tower and the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s sword spirit.

Chapter 901: Qingfeng Sword’s Sword Spirit

Compared to three years ago, aside from Mingtai’s more mature appearance, the biggest change was his eyes. They were as bright as two sharp sword tips.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, I heard you overcame the unprecedented Unbeatable Divine Lightning and the top-ranked Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation, which only appears when Divine Transfiguration cultivators break through, and that you have reached the Divine Transfiguration Stage.”

Mingtai set down his hammer and cupped his fists in salute. He was genuinely happy to see Lu Yang.

Although everyone at the Sword Tower praised his talent in Sword Dao to the heavens, in his eyes, only Lu Yang possessed supreme talent, while he himself fell somewhat short.

If I were to encounter the Unbeatable Divine Lightning and the Qian-Heaven Lightning Tribulation during my tribulation, I certainly wouldn’t survive.

“This is...” Mingtai noticed Yun Mengmeng, who had been standing quietly nearby.

“Her surname is Yun. I befriended her on the road; she’s traveling with me for now.”

“So it’s Miss Yun.” Mingtai greeted her politely, showing no contempt despite her lower cultivation level.

Yun Mengmeng thought, The people in the outside world are pretty nice, not at all like Granny described—full of treachery and scheming. She even warned me to keep a low profile while traveling; I must suppress my cultivation and not reveal my true level until meeting Little Zhi.

“You’re forging swords here?” Lu Yang noticed the large hammer Mingtai just set down.

“It’s a tradition left by the first Tower Leader. He believed sword cultivators could enhance their understanding of the Sword Dao through forging blades. Since then, every Sword Tower disciple must learn forging techniques.”

The first tower leader was the Sword Tower Supreme Lord, a prodigy of his generation. He advanced rapidly but halted at the Half-Immortal Stage, perishing under the Immortal Ascension Tribulation.

Typically, Mingtai addressed the Sword Tower Supreme Lord as “Master.” However, it was a secret that he was the Sword Tower Supreme Lord’s sword spirit. Only a few higher-ups in the Sword Tower were privy to this. Hence, Mingtai couldn’t let anything slip in front of Lu Yang.

That said, Lu Yang knew Mingtai’s origin, for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had told him.

“So that’s how it is,” Lu Yang replied.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, are you here to purchase a sword? These personal swords are all forged by our Sword Tower disciples. They probably wouldn’t meet your standards.”

“Not necessarily...” Lu Yang felt embarrassed to say directly that their swords were too low-grade to be worthy of him.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, why don’t you try your luck at the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony? If a sword resonates with you, it will naturally follow you.”

“There’s such a thing at the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony?”

Although Lu Yang was a sword cultivator and the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony was the most important event for all sword cultivators, he hadn’t paid much attention to it. He only knew it was a tradition left by the Sword Tower Supreme Lord, held once every century.

“Our Sword Tower forges swords frequently. Across the generations of tower leaders and elders, several enjoyed forging spirit swords. Occasionally, they would forge one possessing a spiritual nature.

“After the lifespans of the tower leaders and elders were depleted, these swords became masterless. If they are forced upon sword cultivators without affinity, it would incur the swords’ displeasure.

“However, if they are kept sealed and gather dust, their spiritual nature would eventually fade.

“Sword Tower is unwilling to let the spirit swords gather dust, so we opened our sword vault. Whoever can resonate with a particular spirit sword may take it, letting it shine in the hands of a suitable sword cultivator. However, it’s for personal use only—no selling or gifting is permitted. Upon the cultivator’s death, the spirit sword must be returned to our Sword Tower.”

“Your esteemed sect is truly magnanimous!” Lu Yang exclaimed sincerely. The value of swords with a spiritual nature needs no elaboration. Sword Tower’s magnanimity in allowing outsiders wield them is admirable. As expected of the sword cultivators’ sacred ground.

“We’re just unwilling to let the spirit swords gather dust,” Mingtai stressed. As a sword spirit himself, he felt this most profoundly.

“How about asking the Sword Tower to consider cooperating with our Dao-Seeking Sect?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suggested from the mental space.

“Cooperate?”

“You see, the Sword Tower is unwilling to let the swords’ spiritual nature disappear, and our Dao-Seeking Sect has just the capability.”

“Is Fifth Elder that capable?”

“Not that kid. To preserve a sword’s spiritual nature, you must either find a master for it or elevate the spiritual nature to a sword spirit. Look at our sect’s River Spirit—that belongs to the latter method.”

Hearing this, Lu Yang roughly grasped the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s idea, his eye twitching. “In other words, Immortal Fairy, you’re suggesting to refine all the prisoners at Incarceration Peak into sword spirits and merge them with the Sword Tower’s swords?”

“Correct. A good idea, isn’t it?”

“No,” Lu Yang flatly rejected the proposal. This isn’t how a righteous sect should act.

Mass soul refinement, eerie winds, ghostly wails—if outsiders were to see this, they’d think the Dao-Seeking Sect is a diabolic creed.

“Besides, when the time comes, how would we settle the ownership of the spirit swords? Are we supposed to steal all these swords for the Dao-Seeking Sect? Our sect is the leader of the righteous path; we can’t behave like this.”

“You seem to have a point.

“What a pity. I was thinking of organizing a large-scale sword spirit refinement event and refining Guan Shanhai into your Qingfeng Sword. An immortal sword with a sword spirit would be the ultimate immortal artifact; even the Heaven Mandate Immortal couldn’t forge one.

“Wait, it seems that giving your immortal sword a sword spirit doesn’t require refining Guan Shanhai.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy thought of a brilliant idea to elevate the Qingfeng Sword’s quality.

“What do you mean?”

She smiled mysteriously. “Xiao Yangzi, take out your Qingfeng Sword.”

Lu Yang complied, retrieving the Qingfeng Sword from his identity jade tablet, though he still couldn’t figure out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s intentions.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flew out of the mental space, slid down Lu Yang’s arm, and darted into the Qingfeng Sword.

“Now, your Qingfeng Sword is a top-tier immortal artifact with a sword spirit!”

I’ve been in the mental space for so long; a change of environment is nice.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy warned sternly, “You can’t put the Qingfeng Sword back into your identity jade tablet.”

“Fine...”

Lu Yang casually swung the Qingfeng Sword a couple of times. According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s theory, it should now be the world’s most powerful weapon, but he felt no difference; it seemed the same as before.

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, why did you suddenly take out your sword?” Mingtai was baffled. Senior Brother Lu Yang seemed to be possessed by some inauspicious thing just now, abruptly brandishing his sword as if he wanted to randomly slash someone.

“Nothing. Just letting it get some fresh air.”

“Oh.” Mingtai could understand. Sword cultivators regard their swords as their beloved; it’s understandable that they’re a little unhinged.

“By the way, Immortal Fairy, is there something off about the lady called Yun Mengmeng?” Lu Yang couldn’t help but feel that something was amiss with Yun Mengmeng, though he couldn’t pinpoint what it was.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy snorted discontentedly. “You treated her to hotpot, storytelling, and pastries; what problem could there be?”

Even I haven’t enjoyed such treatment before.

Chapter 902: Nameless Sword Cultivators

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, several of my senior brothers and sisters have long wanted to meet you. Would it be convenient for you?”

“Sure, let’s go meet them then.” Lu Yang smiled, sheathing the Qingfeng Sword and casually hanging it at his waist.

Previously, Lu Yang had tried not to reveal the Qingfeng Sword. As it was an immortal blade refined by Wu Yao, he was worried it would be recognized by Great Yu cultivators, thereby inviting trouble.

For instance, the Myriad Spells Daoist Lord attacked the Dao-Seeking Sect after recognizing the Qingfeng Sword and deducing that the sect possessed the immortal treasure left behind by Wu Yao.

Now, Lu Yang had no such concerns. Everyone who knew the Qingfeng Sword’s origin was imprisoned at Incarceration Peak; no one in the outside world could recognize it.

Yun Mengmeng gazed at the Qingfeng Sword, a thoughtful expression on her visage.

“Miss Yun, what are you thinking?” Lu Yang noticed her reaction.

“Do you remember that sister I mentioned earlier?”

“The one incredibly formidable at fighting?”

“Yes. She actually likes swords quite a bit. She secretly practiced for a while and studied plenty of theory. However, she never achieved much, not even grasping the fundamentals. Eventually, she gave up.”

Lu Yang chuckled. “That’s just how the Sword Dao is. Effort alone doesn’t guarantee success; talent and comprehension are both integral. It suggests that your sister’s sword talent is pretty average.

“That said, since she’s interested in Sword Dao, I could offer some guidance. I’m not trying to boast, but I have some talent in Sword Dao. Among the younger generation of the cultivation world, few surpass me.”

Hearing this, Mingtai smiled too. “Senior Brother Lu Yang is being modest. Among the younger generation, I doubt anyone’s talent in Sword Dao exceeds yours.

“Perhaps that Young Creed Leader Lu comes close, but he’s from the ancient era; strictly speaking, he’s not from our generation.”

“That’s wonderful then.” Yun Mengmeng was happy for her good friend. According to her, she also belongs to the younger generation, so her talent definitely falls short of Lu Yang’s. This is a perfect chance for Lu Yang to teach her.

Little Zhi always brings gifts home; this time, I’m reciprocating by finding her a shifu.

~~~

The Sword Tower had eighteen floors altogether. The first eight were open to visitors; sword cultivators attending the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony could choose rooms here to stay for a few days, with cultivation resources provided by the Sword Tower.

Floors nine to twelve were for inner and true lineage disciples. As the Sword Tower’s core area, they were not easily accessible to outsiders.

Mingtai brought Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng to the twelfth floor.

“Who are those two? Why can they go up?”

Sword cultivators exchanging insights on the eighth floor were astonished. From Mingtai’s clothing, he was clearly an inner disciple, but Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng were obviously outsiders.

“Why does one of them look like Lu Yang?”

“He’s Lu Yang? Right, I’ve seen his portrait—that is Lu Yang!”

“I heard that when he was at the East Sea, he had already comprehended Sword Dao to the point where all things could become a sword. He even used people as swords to execute One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords!”

“He was only at the Nascent Soul Stage then, wasn’t he? To perform One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords at that level is truly terrifying.”

Those eligible to attend the Sword-Seeking Grand Ceremony were all prodigies of their respective regions and unmatched in Sword Dao, inevitably carrying some pride. Yet compared to Lu Yang, they were like novices showing off before a master, unable to muster even the will to compete with him.

A nameless sword cultivator sitting in a corner curled his lips into an enigmatic smile. “Lu Yang, eh? I wonder if he’s worthy to test my sword.”

In another corner, another nameless cultivator’s eyes were fixed on Lu Yang until the latter vanished up the stairs. “Looks like he’s nothing special.”

The former nameless cultivator took offense. “Hey, watch your words. Lu Yang is the opponent I’ve chosen. Are you saying my test subject is mediocre?”

The latter nameless sword cultivator sneered coldly. “And what if I am?!”

The two nameless sword cultivators glared fiercely at each other, their right hands silently gripping their sword hilts, poised to draw their swords at any moment.

Just then, an outer Sword Tower disciple led an elder to the eighth floor, pointing at the two nameless cultivators in the corner. “Elder, it’s these two. When registering at the entrance, they refused to give their names and sneaked into our Sword Tower!”

The elder looked down at them imperiously. “So you two entered without registering. Shall I escort you out, or will you leave on your own?”

One nameless cultivator smirked disdainfully at the elder. “Chase me out? Is this the Sword Tower’s hospitality? Do you know who I am...”

Without another word, the elder opened a window and tossed them both out.

“Lunatics. You wouldn’t give your names during registration, and now you want to? Too late.”

~~~

“Senior Sister Little Mi, Senior Brother Yu...look who I’ve brought.”

Mingtai led Lu Yang and Yun Mengmeng to a stone chamber on the twelfth floor, where six people gathered. Apart from Mingtai, they were the most talented disciples of the Sword Tower.

“Greetings, fellow Daoists. I am Lu Yang.” Lu Yang inverted the Qingfeng Sword and cupped his hands in salute.

“Fellow Daoist Lu Yang, your reputation precedes you.” The six Sword Tower prodigies rose and returned the salute, genuinely elated to meet him.

“This is Miss Yun. She’s traveling with me for now.”

“Greetings, Miss Yun.”

“Hello.” Yun Mengmeng stood quietly to the side. I know little of the outside world; speaking too much may make me a laughingstock.

“Come, come, come, let me introduce them to you, Senior Brother Lu Yang. This is Senior Sister Mi Li[1]—everyone likes to call her Senior Sister Little Mi.”

Lu Yang noticed that Mi Li’s aura fluctuated, rising and falling unstably, indicating she was at the Void Refinement Stage.

“This is Senior Brother Yue Chuan, the Tower Leader’s closed-left-door disciple.”

Yue Chuan resembled a libertine, openly embracing a woman in public without any sense of impropriety.

“This is Senior Brother Li Tang, the Tower Leader’s closed-right-door disciple.”

Li Tang was reticent, cradling a sword, his hair tied in a high ponytail. He merely nodded to Lu Yang without speaking, exuding the aura of a sword cultivator.

Yun Mengmeng couldn’t help but ask, “What are a ‘closed-left-door disciple’ and a ‘closed-right-door disciple?’”

“When the Tower Leader decided to take only one person as his closed-door disciple, both senior brothers were excellent, and it was hard to choose, so he accepted both.

“The Tower Leader said that since closing a gate requires closing two doors, taking in two disciples was perfectly normal.

“Senior Brother Li Tang is shy and unwilling to speak. Please don’t mind, Senior Brother Lu Yang.”

After a round of introductions, Mingtai still hadn’t introduced the woman in Yue Chuan’s arms, which Lu Yang found odd.

“And this is?”

“Oh, I forgot to introduce. This is a sword spirit nurtured by Senior Brother Yue Chuan—truly remarkable. Senior Brother Yue Chuan is strengthening his communion with the sword spirit. He’s the only disciple of our generation with a sword spirit.”

1. “Mili” literally means rice grain. ☜
